Disease: dama (Asthma) Description: suukasham shavaas naliyom mem koe rog utapanan ho jaane ke kaaraण jab kisee vayakati ko sms lene mem pareshaanee hone lagatee hai tab yah sathiti dama rog kahalaatee hai, es rog mem vayakati ko khmsee kee samasaya bhee hotee hai। Symptoms: - jab dama rog se peeda़it rogee ko daura pada़ta hai to use suukhee ya ithanadaar khmsee hotee hai। - jab rog bahot adhik badha़ jaata hai to daura ane kee sathiti utapanam ho jaatee hai jisase rogee ko sms lene mem bahot adhik dikakat atee hai tatha vayakati chhatapataane lagata hai। - dama rog se peeda़it rogee ko kaph sakhata, badabuudaar tatha doreedaar nikalata hai। - peeda़it rogee ko sms lenem mem bahot adhik kathinaae hotee hai। - yah rog sataree-porosh donom ko ho sakata hai। - raat ke samay mem lagabhag 2 baje ke baad daure adhik pada़te haim। - rogee ko rog ke shoroatee samay mem khmsee, sarasaraahat aur sms ukhada़ne ke daure pada़ne lagate haim। - sms lete samay adhik jor lagaane par rogee ka chehara laal ho jaata hai। - sms lete samay halakee-halakee seetee bajane kee avaaj bhee sonaae pada़tee hai। - sms lene tatha sms ko baahar chhoda़ne mem kaaphee jor lagaana pada़ta hai। Reasons: - aushadhiyom ka adhik parayog karane ke kaaraण kaफ़ suukh jaane se dama ho jaata hai। - khaana-paan ke galat tareeke se yah rog ho sakata hai। - maanasik tanaava, karodh tatha adhik bhay ke kaaraण bhee dama home ka ek kaaraण hai। - khuun mem kisee parakaar se dosh utapanam ho jaane ke kaaraण bhee dama ho sakata hai। - nasheele padaarathom ka adhik sevan karana bhee es rog ka kaaraण hai। - khmsee, jokaam tatha najala rog adhik samay tak rahane se dama ho sakata hai। - bhuukh se adhik bhojan khaane se dama ho sakata hai। - miracha-masaale, tale-bhone khaaday padaarathom tatha garishath bhojan karane se yah rog ho sakata hai। - phephada़om mem kamajoree, haृday mem kamajoree, goradom mem kamajoree, mtom mem kamajoree, sanaayomaणdal mem kamajoree tatha naakada़a rog ho jaame ke kaaraण dama ho jaata hai। - manoshay kee shavaas nalika mem dhuul tatha thmd lag jaane ke kaaraण bhee dama ho sakata hai। - dhuul ke kaण, khopada़ee ke khoraणda, kochh paudhom ke poshaparaja, aणde tatha ise hee anay padaarathom ka bhojan mem adhik sevam karame ke kaaraण yah rog ho sakata hai। - manoshay ke shareer kee paachan naliyom mem jalan utapanan karane vaale padaarathom ka sevan karane se bhee dama ho sakata hai। - mala-muutar ke veg ko baara-baar rokane se yah rog ho sakata hai। - garada, dhom, gmdagee, badabuu, gmde bisatara, poraanee kitaabem aur kapaड़om kee jhaaड़, khetom kee jhaaड़, sakhat saradee, barasaata, jokaama, phaluu, adi suukasham kaणom ka sms davaara phephaड़om mem jaane se dama ho sakata hai। - vaataavaraण mem paraduushaण se hone vaalee elarajee - esake alaava kae logom mem kochh nishachit davaaom (esapireen aur betaa- balaॉkarasa) ke sevan se bhee dama ke risak phaikataras badha़ sakate haim। - atayadhik bhaavanaatamak abhivayakatiym (jaise cheekhane-chilalaane ya phir joradaar tareeke se hmsana bhee) bhee kochh logom mem dama kee samasaya ko badha़aakar daure kee sathiti utapanan kar sakatee haim। - asathama ya elarajee ka paarivaarik etihaas (anivmshik damaa) - janam ke samay kam vajan aur samay se pahale bachachom ka janama, janam ke pahale aur / ya janam ke baad tmbaakuu ke dhoem ke smparak - bheeda़, vaayoparaduushaण, dhuul (ghar ya baahar kee) ya pepar kee dasata, rasoe ka dhom, namee, seelana, mausam parivaratana, saradee-jokaama, dhuumarapaana, phaasataphuudasa, tanaav v chimtaa, paalatuu jaanavar ke smparak mem rahana aur peड़-paudhom aur phuulom ke paraagakaणom (paudhe ke phuulom mem paaye jaane vaale suukasham kaणom ko paraagakaण kahate haim) adi ko shaamil kiya jaata hai। Treatments: - rogee ko garam bisatar par sona chaahie। - dhuumarapaan naheem karana chaahie। - bhojan mem miracha-masaaledaar cheejom ka sevan naheem karana chaahie। - dhuul tatha dhome bhare vaataavaraण se bachana chaahie। - maanasik pareshaanee, tanaava, karodh tatha lada़aae-jhagadom se bachana chaahie। - sharaaba, tamabaakuu tatha anay nasheele padaarathom ka sevan naheem karana chaahie। Home Remedies: - lahason dama ke elaaj mem kaaphee kaaragar saabit hota hai। 30 milee duudh mem lahason kee pmch kaliym ubaalem aur es misharaण ka har roj sevam karane se dame mem shoroatee avasatha mem kaaphee phaayada milata hai। - adarak kee garam chaay mem lahason kee do pisee kaliym milaakar peene se bhee asathama niymtarit rahata hai। sabere aur shaam es chaay ka sevan karane se mareej ko phaayada hota hai। - adarak ka ek chamamach taaja rasa, ek kap maithee ke kaaढ़e aur savaadaanosaar shahad es misharaण mem milaaem। dame ke mareejom ke lie yah misharaण laajavaab saabit hota hai। - dama rogee paanee mem ajavaaen milaakar ese ubaalem aur paanee se uthatee bhaap lem, yah ghareluu upaay kaaphee phaayademmd hota hai। - 4-5 laumg lem aur 125 milee paanee mem 5 minat tak ubaalem। es misharaण ko chhaanakar esamem ek chamamach shodadh shahad milaaen aur garama-garam pee lem। har roj do se teen baar yah kaaढ़a bamaakar peeme se mareej ko nishachit ruup se laabh hota hai। - 180 mimee paanee mem motatheebhar sahajan kee patatiym milaakar kareeb 5 minat tak ubaalem। misharaण ko thmda hone dem, usamem chotakeebhar namaka, kaaleemirach aur neebuu ras bhee milaaya ja sakata hai। es suup ka niyamit ruup se esatemaal dama upachaar mem kaaragar maana gaya hai। - maithee ka kaaढ़a taiyaar karane ke lie ek chamamach maitheedaana aur ek kap paanee ubaalem। har roj sabere-shaam es misharaण ka sevan karane se nishachit laabh milata hai। - ek paka kela chhilaka lekar chaakuu se lamabaae mem cheera lagaakar usamem ek chhota chamamach do garaam kapaड़a chhaan kee hoe kaalee mirach bhar dem। phir use bagair chheele hee, kele ke vaृkash ke patate mem achachhee tarah lapet kar dore se bmdh kar 2-3 ghmte rakh dem। baad mem kele ke patate sahit use ag mem es parakaar bhuune kee upar ka patata jale। thmda hone par kele ka chhilaka nikaalakar kela kha lem। Disease: madhomeh (Diabetes) Description: madhomeh ya daayabiteej haal ke saalom mem hone vaala sabase khataranaak jeevamashailee rog maana jaata hai। har saal kae hajaar log esase parabhaavit hote haim। aeyem jaanem madhomeh ke baarem mem jise log am bolachaal kee bhaasha me shogar (Sugar ki Bimari) bhee kahate haim। Symptoms: - atayadhik payaas lagana aur baar baar peshaab ana (Excessive Thirst): yah madhomeh hone ke pokhata lakashaण haim - jakhamom ka jaladee nahee bharana aur baar baar smkaramaण se parabhaavit hona (Slow Healing Sores amd Recurrent Imfections) - thakaan mahasuus hona (Feeling Lazy): koshikaaom mem galuukoज़ nahee pahomchane ke kaaraण shareer ko oraja apuurati puuree tarah se nahee ho paatee hai aur madhomeh ka rogee hamesha thakaan mahasuus karata hai - dhomdhala dikhana (Blurred Vision): rakat mem atirikat shogar kee upasathiti ke kaaraण nkhom kee koshikaaom mem rakat apuurati par asar paड़ta hai aur dheere dheere nkhe parabhaavit hone lagatee haim - pairo aur haathom mem jhanajhanaahat hona (Timgling in Hands & Feet): rakat mem atirikat shogar ka kaaraण hamaare tmtarika paraणaalee ko nokasaan pahomcha sakata hai - masuuड़om mem suujan (Swollen Gums): madhomeh ke kaaraण masuuड़om mem smkaramaण ka khatara baढ़ jaata hai - rakat mem atirikat shogar kee upasathiti ke kaaraण gorade rakat ko saaफ़ karane ke lie adhik kaam karane lagate haim aur muutar ke davaara atirikat shogar ko shareer se baahar nikalate haim। es kaaraण baar baar peshaab ata hai aur atayadhik payaas lagatee hai - vajan kam hona (Weight Loss): hamaare shareer mem jab koshikaaom ko galuukoज़ nahee milata to shareera, shareer mem upasathit vasa tatha mmsapeshio se usakee apuurati karata hai jisake kaaraण shareer mem jama vasa aur mmsapeshio mem kamee atee hai aur vajan bahot jaladee kam hone lagata hai Treatments: madhomeh ya daayabiteej se bachaav ka sabase baढ़iya upaay hai esakee jaanakaaree rakhana aur savasath jeevanashailee apanaanaa। daayabiteej se bachane ke kochh khaan upaay niman haim: - paratidin ek ghmta vayaayaam jaruur karem। - apane ghar mem paratidin madhomeh ka tesat karem। rakat mem shogar kee maatara ka dhayaan rakhem। - enasolim rakhanaa। - rakatachaap (Blood Pressure) kam hone par matavapuuraण jaanakaaree ka dhayaan rakhana Disease: vaayaral bokhaar (Viral Fever) Description: vaayaras ke smkaramaण se hone vaale bokhaar ko vaayaral pheevar (Viral Fever) kahate haim। vaayaral bokhaar ke vaayaras gale mem sopataavasatha mem nishakariy rahate haim। thmde vaataavaraण ke smparak mem ane, pharij ka thmda paanee, sheetal pey peene adi se ye vaayaras sakariy hokar hamaare paratirakasha tmtar ko parabhaavit kar dete haim। Symptoms: - nkhem laal hona - es bokhaar mem shareer ka taap 101 digaree se 103 digaree ya aur jayaada kamajoree mahasuus karana - siradarad hona Reasons: vaayaral bokhaar shareer ke kamaज़or paratirakasha tmtar (Immune System) kee vajah se hota hai। agar shareer kee paratirakashaण kashamata ya emayuun sisatam majabuut ho to yah beemaaree jaladee naheem hotee। Treatments: vaayaral bokhaar ka upaay (Treatment of Viral Fever) - bokhaar agar 102 digaree tak hai aur koe aur khataranaak lakashaण naheem haim to mareej kee dekhabhaal ghar par hee kar sakate haim। - mareej ke shareer par saamaanay paanee kee patatiym rakhem। patatiym tab tak rakhem, jab tak shareer ka taapamaan kam n ho jaae। patatee rakhane ke baad vah garam ho jaatee hai esalie use siraph 1 minat tak hee rakhem। - agar maathe ke saath - saath shareer bhee garam hai to naॉramal paamee mem kapada़a bhigokar nichoda़em aur usase puure shareer ko pomchhem। - mareej ko har chhah ghmte mem pairaasitaamaॉl (Paracetamol) kee ek golee de sakate haim। duusaree koe golee daॉkatar se puuchhe bina n dem। - bachachom ko har chaar ghmte vaayaral hai, to usase thoda़ee duuree banaae rakhem aur rogee ke davaara esatemaal kee gae cheejem esatemaal n karem। - mareej ko puura araam karane dem, khaasakar tej bokhaar mem। araam bhee bokhaar mem elaaj ka kaam karata hai। - mareej chheemkane se pahale naak aur momh par romaal rakhem। esase vaayaral hone par duusarom mem phailega naheem। - vaayaral pheevar mem emteebaॉyatik davaaom kee koe chaahie। Disease: khasara (Measles) Description: khasara (Measles), ek ataymt smkaraamak beemaaree hai। khasara meejalas vaayaras (Measles Virus) se phailata hai। esase garasit rogee ka pahale gala bachaav ka sabase behatareen tareeka hai esake rogee ke smparak mem ma amaa। lekin agar khasara (Khasra) ho bhee jaae to niman upaay davaara esase bachaav momakin hai: - parabhaavit bachache/rogee ko umahem roj badalem। - bokhaar kee tejee mem sir par deshee ghee kee maalish v paanee mem suutee mota kapaड़a bhigokar rakhem। - mokh v dmt saaph rakhane ke liye gonagone paanee mem thoड़ee see laal dava ka teekaakaraण hai। Disease: badahaज़mee (Gastric Problem) Description: paachanakariya ke dauraam pet mem gais ka banama ek saamaanay parakariya hai। shareer kee anay parakariyaaom kee tarah pet mem gathiya (Gout) Description: gathiya (Gout) ya vaatarakat ek saamaanay rog hai jisamem rogee ke ek ya kae joda़om mem darada, akada़m ya suujan  jaatee hai। es rog mem joda़om mem gmthem ban jaatee par paड़ne vaala adhik dabaav es darad ko aur adhik baढ़a deta hai। Treatments: ​​ghotanom ke darad se nijaat paane ka sabase behatar upaay esase bachana maana jaata hai। daॉkatarom ke anosaar savasath jeevanashailee aur vajam ko niymtaraण mem rakhakar es beemaaree se asaanee se bacha ja sakata hai। ghotanom ke darad se bachaav ke kochh anay upaay niman haim: - apana vajan miymtarit rakhem। - soem। - din mem kam se kam 2 baar baraph lagaaem। - daॉkatar se samaya-samay par jmch karaate rahem। Home Remedies: ghotanom ke darad kee sabase baड़ee vajah hai ovaravet honaa। agar apake shareer ka vajan jayaada hai to jaahir hai apaka bhaar sahane mem apake ghotanom ko takaleeph hogee। esake alaava phijikal ekativitee kam hone, kailashiyam kee kamee hone ya aratharaaetis (arthritis) hone se bhee ghotanom mem darad rahata hai। mmsapeshiyom mem tanaav rahane ya kisee chot kee vajah se bhee ghotanom ka darad apako pareshaan kar sakata hai। aee jaanem kochh ghareluu upaaya, jinahem apanaakar ap ghotamom ke darad se raahat pa sakate haim। 1. thmda sek (Cold fomentation) ghotanom ke darad se raahat ke lie thmda sek diya ja sakata hai। yah sabase asaan aur parabhaavee tareekom mem se ek hai। ghotanom ko thmda sek deme se yah rakat vaahikaaom ko kasata hai jisase rakat paravaah kam hota hai aur suujan bhee ghatatee hai। kaise karem- ek patalee tauliya mem baraph ke tokaड़e lapet lem। 10 se 20 minat ke lie darad parabhaavit ghotane ke hisase ko sekem। apaka darad dheere dheere duur ho jaaegaa। es upaay ko rojaana do ya teem baar kar sakate haim। 2. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar) seb ka siraka bhee ghotane ke darad ko kam karane mem sahaayak hai। ye ghotame ke joड़ ke bheetar khanij ekathatha karata hai aur haanikaarak vishaakat padaarathom ko mashat karata hai। kaise karem- do kap फ़ilatarad paamee mem do chamamach seb ka siraka milaaem। dinabhar mem yah ghol peeem। puuree tarah theek hone tak rojaana es taॉnik ka sevam karem। baalatee mem garam paanee daalakar usamem do kap seb ka siraka milaakar 30 mimat ke lie paanee mem parabhaavit ghotane bhigaakar baith jaaem। esase ghotamom ke darad mem kaaphee raahat milegee। ek chamamach seb ka siraka aur jaituun ke tel ko baraabar bhaagom mem milaakar ghotanom kee maalish karem, phaayada hogaa। 3. laal mirach (Red Chilli) laal mirach ke esatemaal se ghotanom ke darad mem bhee raahat milatee hai, esamem maujuud kepasaaesin darad nivaarak kee tarah kaam karata hai। kaise karem- ek se deढ़ kap tel mem do baड़e chamamach laal mirach paaudar daalakar ek pesat taiyaar karem। kam se kam ek sapataah tak har din do baar yah pesat ghotanom par lagaaem। ghotanom ke darad se raahat milegee। ek kap seb ke sirake mem ek chauthaae ya adha chamamach laal mirach paaudar daalakar mitaraण taiyaar karem। es mitaraण ko ghotanom par lagaane se darad aur suujan kam ho jaatee hai। jab tak ghotanom darad se raahat m ho tab tak har din es pesat ko 20 minat ke lie ghotanom par laga sakate haim। 4. adarak (Ginger) ghotane ka darad mmsapeshiyom mem tamaav kee vajah se ho ya gathiya ke kaaraण, adarak donom hee sathiti mem behad laabhaparad hai। esamem emtee़phalemebal goण hote haim jo ghotane kee suujan aur darad ko kam kar dete haim। kaise karem- ek kap paanee mem thoड़a sa adarak ka tokaड़a lekar 10 minat ubaal lem। esake baad esako thmda karake esamem thoड़a sa neembuu ka ras aur shahad milaaem। es ghol ko roj peeem। ap chaahem to adarak ke tel se ghotanom kee maalish bhee kar sakate haim। 5. haladee (Haldi) haladee ghotane ke darad ko duur karame ke lie ek parabhaavee aur paraakaृtik upachaar hai। haladee mem maujuud korakayuumin emteeऑkaseedemt kee tarah kaam karata hai aur darad kam karane mem madad karata hai। kaise karem- ek kap paanee mem adarak aur haladee ko thoड़a thoड़a milaakar 10 minat ke lie ese ubaal lem। esake baad esako gonagona hone ke baad shahad milaaem। din mem do baar ese peeem। ek gilaas duudh mem haladee daalakar ubaalem aur usamem shahad milaakar peeem। esase bhee ghotanom ka darad theek hota hai। nota: * haladee rakat ko patala karatee hai, ise mem khuun patala (Blood Thinning) karane kee dava lene vaalom ke lie yah theek maheem। * shahad ko bahot garam paanee ya duudh mem naheem milaana chaahie। 6. neembuu (Lemon) neembuu bhee gathiya kee vajah se ghotane ke darad ke lie ek ghareluu laabhakaaree upaay hai। neembuu mem paaya jaane vaala saaetarik esid (citric acid) gathiya mem yuurik esid karisatal ko gholaata hai। kaise karem- ek neembuu chhote-chhote tokaड़om mem kaatem। en tokaड़om ko suutee kapaड़e mem daalakar garam til ke tel mem dobaaem। esake baad pmch se 10 minat ke lie parabhaavit ghotane par kapaड़a rakhem। ek din mem do baar isa karane se darad puuree tarah chala jaata hai। ek gilaas paanee mem neembuu nichaaड़kar peene se bhee laabh hota hai। ko khatam karate haim। Disease: aganaashayashoth (Pancreatitis) Description: aganayaashayashoth (Pamcreatitis) aganayaashay (Pancreas) mem suujan hona hai। aganayaashay pet ke peechhe udar goha mem namak daalakar potalee bmdh lem। kamar par esake davaara sek karem। Disease: seene mem darad (Chest Pain) Description: seene mem darad ( Chest Pain) kee baat ate hee ham dil ke daure (Heart Attack) seedha asar mmsapeshiyom par bhee paड़ta hai। Disease: parosatet kaimsar (Prostate Camcer) Descriptiom: parosatet kaimsar poroshom ko hota hai। ye kaimsar shoruuatee daur mem pata chal jaae, to asaamee parosatet kaimsar 40 kee umar ke baad sabase jayaada hota hai। umar baढ़ne ke saath hee parosatet galaimd baढ़ne lagata hai, jo kaimsar hone kee smbhaavana ko baढ़aata hai। 50 saal kee umar paar kar rahe logom mem yah bahot tejee se phailata hai। parosatet kaimsar (Prostate Cancer) ke har 3 mem se 2 mareejom kee umar 65 ya usase jayaada hotee hai। - amovmshik beemaaree: parosatet kaimsar anovmshik bhee hota hai। ghar mem agar kisee bhee vayakati ya rishatedaar ko parosatet kaimsar hota hai to bachachom mem esakee hone kee smbhaavana jayaada hotee hai। - khaanapaana: adhonik jeevanashailee mem Disease: haipetaaetis (Hepatitis) Description: livar shareer ka ek mahatatavapuuraण mg hai। vah bhojan pachaane mem mahatatavapuuraण bhuumika nibhaata hai। shareer mem hone vaalee chayaapachay har teen maheene mem barash badal lem। Home Remedies: saphed aur chamakate dmt kisee kee bhee parasamelitee mem nikhaar la sakate haim। bahot se log peele dmtom ke kaaraण logom ke saamane hmsane se bachate haim ya momh par haath rakhakar hmsate haim। dmt jayaadaatar umar ke kaaraण, dmtom kee theek se saphaae n hone ke kaaraण, bahot jayaada chaay ya kaॉphee peene ke kaaraण athava tmbaakuu aur sigaret peene ke kaaraण peele ho jaate haim। kabhee kabhee kisee beemaaree ke kaaraण bhee dmt peele ho jaate haim। haalmki peele dmtom ko saphed banaana koe moshakil kaam naheem hai। thoड़ee see mehanat se ap peele dmtom ko saphed bana sakate haim। aee apako kochh ghareluu nosakhe bataate haim jo apake dmto kee saphedee aur chamak ko banaae rakhemge। 1. bekimg sodaa- (Baking Soda) bekimg soda dmtom ko saphed banaane ka sabase asaan tareeka hai। yah dmtom se palaak ko khatam karake dmtom kee saphedee aur chamak banaae rakhata hai। kaise upayog karem - roj barash karate samay apane pesat mem thoड़a sa bekimg paaudar daalem aur barash karem। dmtom kee saphedee laut aegee। - ek kap paanee mem bekimg soda aur haaedarojan par ऑkasaaed (hydrogen peroxide) milaakar maauth vaॉsh (mouthwash) kee tarah bhee esatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। 2. smtare ka chhilakaa- (Peel of Orange) smtare ke chhilake se roj dmtom kee saphaae karane se kochh hee dinom mem peele dmt chamakane lagemge। kaise upayog karem - roj raat ko sote samay smtare ke chhilake ko dmtom par ragaड़em। smtare ke chhilake mem vitaamin see (vitamin c) aur kailashiyam ke saath maaekaroऑragenijam (micro organism) hota hai jo dmtom kee majabuutee aur chamak banaae rakhata hai। 3. sataraॉberee- (Strawberry) sataraॉberee mem bhee vitaamin see parachor maatara mem hota hai jo ki dmtom ko saphed banaane mem sahaayak hai। kaise upayog karem - sataraॉberee ke kochh tokaड़om ko peesakara, es lep ko dmtom par lagaakar masaaj karem। ese din mem do baar karane se kochh hee dinom mem peele dmt saphed hone lagate haim। - bekimg soda aur sataraॉberee ke palap ko milaakar bhee dmtom par ragaड़ne se dmtom ka peelaapan khatam hota hai। 4. neembuu- (Lemon) neembuu ke paraakaृtik baleechimg (natural bleach) ke goण dmtom par bhee asar dikhaate haim। peele dmtom ke lie neembuu ke chhilake ko dmtom par ragaड़a ja sakata hai, ya neembuu ke paanee se garaare bhee kie ja sakate haim। kaise upayog karem - neembuu ke saath namak milaakar dmtom kee masaaj karem। - do haphatom tak rojaana do baar karane se dmt chamakane lagemge। 5. namaka- (Salt) namak ko poraane samay se hee dmto kee saphaae ke lie esatemaal kiya jaata raha hai। yah dmtom ke khoe minaralas lautaata hai jisase dmtom ka saphed rmg bana rahata hai। kaise upayog karem - rojaana sobah tuuthapesat kee tarah namak ko dmtom kee saphaae ke lie esatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। namak ko chaarakol mem milaakar bhee dmtom kee saphaae kee ja sakatee hai jisase dmt saphed hote haim। - namak aur bekimg paaudar milaakar bhee mmjam taiyaar kiya ja sakata hai। 6. tolasee- (Basil) tolasee mem bhee dmtom ko saphed banaane ka goण hota hai। esake saath hee tolasee paayariya adi se bhee dmtom kee rakasha karatee hai। kaise upayog karem - tolasee ke patatom ko sokhaakar paaudar bana lem। es paaudar ko rojaama esatemaal karane vaale tuuthapesat mem milaakar dmtom kee saphaae karem। - tolasee ke patatom ka pesat banaakar usamem sarasom ka tel (mustard oil) milaaem। es pesat se dmtom kee saphaae karane par bhee bahot phaayada hota hai। 7. seba- (Apple) seb ko daaet mem shaamil karane se bhee dmtom kee saphedee lautaae ja sakatee hai। seb kee karmcheemes dmtom ko paraakaृtik taur par sakarab karatee hai। rojaana ek ya do seb jaruur khaaem aur khuub chaba chaba kar khaaem। esee tarah gaajar aur kheera bhee kachacha khaane se dmt saphed tatha majabuut banate haim। Disease: tee. bee. (Tuberculosis) Description: tayuubarakayolosis (Tuberculosis) maayakobekatiriyam tayuubarakayolosis naamak jeevaaणo ke kaaraण hota hai। tee.bee. rog ko anay kae maam se jaana jaata hai, jaise tapedika, kashay rog tatha yakashamaa। Symptoms: - agar apaka vajana, bagair koshish kiye hoye, pichhale 2 maheenom mem, 5 kilogaraam se adhik ghat gaya hai - agar apako khmsee mem khuun ata hai - agar apako khmsee mem balagam ata hai - agar apako teen haphate se adhik se khmsee hai - agar apako bhuukh kam lagatee hai - agar apako raat mem adhik paseena ata hai - agar apane apane balagam ka kabhee tee bee ka jmch karavaaya hai, jise poज़itiv kaha gaya ho Reasons: teebee kae kaaraणom se phailata hai lekin esake paramokh kaaraणom mem aparayaapat v apaushatik bhojana, kam jagah mem adhik logom ka rahanaa, gmdagee, gaay ka kachacha duudh peema adi haim। esake anay kaaraण niman haim: teebee ke kaaraण (Causes of Tuberculosis) - tee bee ke mareej ke jahm-jahm thuukame se esake vishaaणo savasath vayakati ke shareer mem paravesh karake use rogee bana dete haim। - kapaड़a mil mem kaam karane vaale sharamik ya reshe-roe ke smparak mem rahane vaale loga, - bonakara, dhuul ke smparak mem rahane vaale log tatha mdheree kothariyom ya chaalom mem rahane vaale log bhee es rog ka shikaar ho jaate haim। - madiraapaana, dhuumarapaan tatha rogagarasat pasho ka mms khaane vaale log bhee teebee ka shikaar ho sakate haim। - asaavadhaaneevash rogee ka khuun anay kisee rog ke shareer mem chaढ़aane se vah vayakati rogagarasat ho jaata hai। Treatments: teebee ka upachaar (Treatment of Tuberculosis in Hindi) - yadi teen athava adhik sapataah se khnsee ho rahee ho to kaफ़ kee do baar jnch karaaem। ye jnch sarakaaree kaफ़ suukashamadarashee kenadarom par ni:sholak kee jaatee hai। - sabhee davaaom ko niyamit ruup se, bataae gae puuree avadhi tak lem। - khnsate ya chheemkate samay ruumaal ka parayog karem। Home Remedies: teebee yaani tayuubarakolosis (Tuberculosis), ek parakaar ka emphekashan hota hai jo ki maayakoekateeriyam tayuubarakolosis (mycobacterium tuberculosis) baikateeriya ke kaaraण phailata hai। teebee adhikatar phephephaड़om mem hotee hai lekin yah shareer ke kisee bhee hisase mem ho sakatee hai। teebee ke mareej ke kaph mem khuun ana teebee ka am lakashaण hai esake alaava smsom ka tej chalanaa, vajan ka kam honaa, bokhaar honaa, kidanee aur seene mem darad hona adi bhee tayuubarakolosis ke lakashaण haim। vaise to teebee se puuree tarah nijaat ke lie chikitasak se paraamarash avashayak hai lekin kochh ghareluu upachaarom ke davaara bhee teebee ko theek karane kee parakariya tej kee ja sakatee hai। aee apako bataate haim teebee ke upachaar ke lie kochh ghareluu nosakhe- 1. lahason (Garlic)- lahason mem salaphayuurik esid (sulphuric acid) parachor maatara mem hota hai jo ki teebee ke keetaaणoom ko maarane mem sakasham hai। esake saath hee lahason mem eleesin (allicin) aur ejoenee (agoeni) bhee hote haim jo ki teebee ke panapame vaale keetaaणoom ka khatam karane ka kaam karate haim। etana hee naheem lahason ke emteebaikateeriyal goण emayuunitee ko bhee baढ़aate haim। kaise karem upayog adhee chamamach lahasona, ek kap duudh aur chaar kap paanee ko ek saath milaakar ubaalem। ese tab tak ubaalem jab tak yah misharaण ek chauthaae rah jaae। es misharaण ko din mem teen baar peeem। garam duudh mem lahason ka ras milaakar bhee peeya ja sakata hai। esake baad paanee n peeem। garam duudh mem lahason ko ubaalem। esake baad lahason ko chabaakar bache hoe duudh ko pee lem। 2. kela (Banana)- kela poshak tatavom aur kailashiyam ka bahot achachha satarot hai। yah teebee ke mareej ka emayuun sisatam badhaa़ne mem sahaayak hai। esake saath hee bokhaar aur kaph se bhee raahat deta hai। kaise karem upayog ek pake hoe kele ko ek kap naariyal ke paanee mem masalakar milaaem। esake baad esamem dahee aur shahad milaaem। ese din mem do baar khaaem। kachache kele ka juus banaakar rojaana peeem। kele ke tane ka juus banaakar bhee peeya ja sakata hai। 3. mvala (Amla)- mvala mem emteephalemetaree (anti inflammatory) aur emteebaikateeriyal (antibacterial) goण hote haim। jo shareer ka emayuun sisatam majabuut karake shareer ko oraja paradaan karate haim। kaise karem upayog mvala ke beej nikaalakara, juus banaaem aur esamem ek chamamach shahad milaakar sobah sobah peeem। 4. smtara (Orange)- smtare mem bhee jaruuree minaralas (minerals) aur kmpaaumd (compound) hote haim। smtare mem maujuud salaaen (salain) shareer ko emphekashan se bachaata hai saath hee emayuun sisatam ko majabuut karata hai। kaise karem upayog taaja smtare ke ras mem thoड़a sa namak aur shahad milaakar rojaana sobah shaam peeem। smtare ko chheelakar usakee salaaes par bhee namak chhiड़k kar khaaya ja sakata hai। 5. shareepha (Custard apple)- teebee ke upachaar ke lie shareepha bhee behad phaayademmd hai। shareephe ka palap nikaalakar ese khaana chaahie। kaise karem upayog do shareephom ka palap mikaalakar use paanee mem ubaal lem, esake saath pachachees kishamish (kishmish) ko bhee ubaal lem। jab paamee ek tihaae rah jaae tab ese chhaamakar esamem paaudar shogar milaaem। es pey mem elaayachee aur daalacheenee milaakar din mem do baar peeem। 6. kaalee mirach (Black pepper)- kaalee mirach phephaड़om (lungs) kee saphaae ka kaam karatee hai। jisase teebee ke dauraan hone vaale seene ke darad se raahat milatee hai। esake saath hee yah teebee ke keetaaणoom ko maarane ka kaam bhee karatee hai। kaise karem upayog makakhan mem ath se das kaalee mirach pharaae karem। esamem ek chotakee heemg milaaem aur paaudar bana lem। es misharaण ko teem baraabar bhaagom mem bmt lem। kochh kochh ghmte ke mtaraal par esakee ek ek doj khaaem। 7. akharot (Walmut)- akharot teebee ke mareejom ko taakat deta hai, unakee emayuunitee baढ़aata hai aur jaladee theek hone mem bhee madad karata hai। kaise karem upayog akharot ke paaudar mem kochh kalee lahason kee milaakar kochal lem। esamem kalereephaaed makakhan (clarified butter) milaakar khaaem। akharot ko yuum bhee khaaya ja sakata hai ya esake paaudar ko salaad mem daalakar khaaem। 8. podeena (Mimt)- podeena mem maujuud emteebaikateeriyal (antibacterial) goणom ke kaaraण esamem bhee teebee ke rog ko theek karane ka adabhot goण hota hai। kaise karem upayog ek chamamach podeene ke ras mem do chamamach shahad milaaem, esake saath hee es ghol mem maalat vinegar (malt vinegar) aur adha kap gaajar ka juus milaaem। es ghol ko kochh kochh ghmtom par puure dim peeem। Disease: pharoज़n sholadar (Frozen Shoulder) Description: kmdhe ka darad ek bahot hee am shikaayat hai। isa maama jaata hai ki kmdhom ke asapaas joda़om mem suujan ane ke kaaraण yah darad hota hai। ise darad mem kabhee-kabhaar kmdhe sonan bhee pada़ jaate haim। yah sathiti kae baar maheenom tak rah jaatee hai। Symptoms: - kmdhom ka sonan pada़ jaana - kmdhom ko ghomaane mem asamarathata mahasuus hona - raat mem kmdhom mem teevar darad hona Reasons: - daayabiteej ke mareejom mem, haृday samasaya se garasit logom mem paarakisam beemaaree ke mareejom mem ho sakatee hai। - garadan mem hone vaalee saravaaekal disak kee samasaya bhee ise darad ka kaaraण ho sakatee hai। - vo mareeja, jinahem kmdhom par kisee parakaar kee chot lagee ho ya kmdhom kee kisee parakaar kee sarajaree hoe hai, unamem pharojan sholadar kee ashmka adhik hotee hai। Treatments: kmdhom kee jakaड़n mem akasar maalish ya semk se araam milata hai। agar esase araam naheem milata hai to niman upaay apanaame chaahie: - darad ko anadekha n karem। yah lagaataar ho to daॉkatar ko dikhaaem। - saamaanay kmdhom ke darad mem darad nivaarak davaaom se hee raahat mil jaatee hai। isa darad kmdhom mem suujan ke kaaraण hota hai, esalie suujan kam karane vaalee davaaem bhee raahat pahomcha sakatee haim। lekin darad kee davaaom ka parayog keval apaat sathiti mem hee karem। - kmdhom ko garam ya thmda sek dem। - darad se jalad araam ke lie ekayuupmkachar chikitasa ka sahaara le sakate haim। - pharojan sholadar kee chikitasa ka sabase achachha upaay phijiyotherepee (Physiotherapy) maana jaata hai। phijiyotherepee mem kmdhom mem khimchaav utapanan kar kmdhom ko dobaara gatimaan banaana hota hai। isa karane ke lie kmdhom ke vibhinan bimdoom ko vayaayaam davaara dheere-dheere saamaanay sathiti mem laane ka parayaas kiya jaata hai। - pharojam sholadar (Frozen Shoulder) kee chikitasa samay par naheem kee gae to mareej ko puura jeevan es samasaya ke saath bitaama pada़ sakata hai। Disease: saravaaekal sapaॉmadilaaetis (Cervical Sypondolysis) Description: umar ke saath hadadiyom mem ghisaav v badalaav  jaata hai। yah garadan kee hadadiyom mem bhee hota hai। hadadiyom mem ghisaava, anatar ho jaane ya enake joड़ vaale bhaag kee mmsapeshiyom mem suujan se garadan ka darad yaani saravaaekal sapmdaaelosis (Cervical Spondolysis) hota hai। yah sab garadam kee us hadadee mem hota hai jise saravaaekal sapaaem kahate haim। reeढ़ kee hadadee ka garadan vaala yah bhaag merodaणd (Spine) kee saat kasheruukaaom (Vertebrae) evm unake madhay kee disak se banata hai। garadan kee 85 paratishat gatividhiym opar kee do kasheruukaaom ke kaaraण hotee hai। garadan ke darad se hone vaalee pareshaamee esamem baadha pahomchaatee haim। saravaaekal sapmdaaelosis pahale 40 varash se adhik ayo ke logom ko hota tha kinato varatamaan samay kee jeevanacharaya evm ajeevika ne bachache aur baड़om sabhee ko garadan mem darad ka mareej bana diya hai। Symptoms: - garadan mem akada़na, - garadan ghomaame mem chat kee avaaj ana - garadam ghomaane mem dikakat - chakakar ana - darad v bhaareepan - nasom mem khimchaav se haathom mem kmpan adi lakashaण dikhate hai - sir ke peechhe bhaag mem darad - haathom ka soman paड़ jaanaa, jaan n rahana Reasons: - sote samay mote takie ka upayog esaka ek kaaraण hai। - baithane kee galat sathiti ke kaaraण, lmbe samay tak ek jaisee sathiti mem baithanaa। kmpayuutar par jayaada der tak kaam karane vaale vayakati, dmt chikitasaka, vaahan chaalaka, helamet dhaarak adi ko yah anay logom kee apekasha jayaada hota hai। - vidayaarathee evm ise vayakati jo bhaaree baig peeth ya kmdhe par latakaae rahate haim, ve esase peeड़it hote haim। - kisee chot ya pharaikachar ke kaaraण yah darad hota hai। - kochh anay rogom mem bhee yah darad parakat hota hai। - ek jaisee sathiti mem lagaataar teevee, kmpayuutara, veediyo gem adi ke upayog se hota hai। Treatments: - garadan evm kmdhe ka vayaayaam niyamit karem। - sahee sathiti mem baithem। - pair jameen par evm peeth korasee ke paृshath bhaag par seedhee rakhem। - jhokakar ya ek jaisee sathiti mem lagaataar kaam m karem। - beecha-beech mem kmdhe, garadan ko ghomaaem। - mote takie v masanad ka upayog kam ya bmd kar dem। - garadan ke darad vaale bhaag kee garam kapaड़e se sikaae karane ya baraph ghisane se darad theek ho jaata hai, phir bhee darad bana rahe to hadadee rog visheshajaञ se milem aur upachaar laabh lem। Home Remedies: saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis (cervical spondylosis) ko garadan kee gathiya (neck arthritis) ke maam se bhee jaana jaata hai। es rog mem garadan ke joड़ mem darad kee shikaayat rahatee hai। yah joड़ kaaratileja, otak aur saravaaekal sapaaem mem joड़e rahate haim। saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis adhikatar umar baढ़ne ke saath hone lagata hai lekin kae dapha garadan par dabaav paड़me, baithame-uthane ke galat poshachar se, dhuumarapaan karane, vajam ke bahot jayaada hone, jenetik kaaraणom aur alasee rahan sahan se bhee shoruu ho sakata hai। haalmki kochh ghareluu upaay apanaakar saravaaekal saponadeeloyasis ka upachaar smbhav hai। aee jaamate haim kochh ise hee upachaarom ke baare mem- 1. niyamit vayaayaam (Daily excersise)- niyamit vayaayaam n karana bhee saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis hone ka baड़a kaaraण hai। niyamit vayaayaam se garadan ke darad ko kam kiya ja sakata hai। (yadi kisee bhee tarah ke vayaayaam se darad baढ़ jaae to vayaayaam ko chhoड़ dem) 2. garam aur thmdee sikaae (Hot and cold fomentation)- garadam darad se nijaat ke lie garadan kee garam aur thmdee sikaae karane se bhee bahot araam milata hai। garam sikaae karane se rakat smchaar behatar hota hai vaheem thmdee sikaae se suujan aur chobham kam hotee hai। kaise karem upachaara- garam sikaae ke lie garam paanee kee botal ko tauliya mem lapet kar garadan kee sikaae karem। thmdee sikaae karane ke lie baraph (ice) ke tokaड़om ko tauliya mem lapetakara, us tauliya se sikaae karem। sikaae karate vakat kam se kam do se teen minat tak garadan kee lagaataar sikaae honee chaahie। 15 se 20 minat mem dobaara doharaaem। es vidhi ko araam hone tak din mem do baar karem। 3. lahason (Garlic)- yadi saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis ke lakashaण najar aem to lahason ka esatemaal behad achachhe pariणaam de sakata hai। esake aushadheey goण garadan ke darada, suujan aur jalan ko theek karate haim। kaise karem upachaara- lahason kee do kalee har sobah khaalee pet paanee ke saath khaaem। khaana banaane vaale kisee bhee tel mem lahason kee kochh kaliym daal kar bhuun lem। es tel ko gonagona hone tak thmda karem aur parabhaavit hisase kee maalish karem। es vidhi ko dim mem do baar kiya ja sakata hai। 4. haladee (Haldi)- haladee ke aushadheey goण kisee se chhipe naheem hai lekin achachhee baat yah bhee hai ki yah saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis ke darad mem bhee utanee hee parabhaavee hai। haladee rakat smchaar tej karake garadan ke darad se araam detee hai aur garadan kee akaड़n ko bhee kam karatee hai। kaise karem upachaara- ek chamamach haladee ko duudh mem daalakar ubaalem aur thmda hone par esamem shahad milaaem, ese dim mem do baar peeem। 5. til (sesame seed)- saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis ke upachaar ke lie ayoraved kee besat aushadhi hai tila। esamem kailashiyama, maiganeeshiyama, maiganeeja, kaॉpara, jimka, phaॉsaphoras aur vitaamin ke (vitamin k) tatha dee (vitamin d) parachor maatara mem paae jaate haim। esee kaaraण yah hadadiyom ke saath saath puure shareer ke lie phaayademmd hai। kaise karem upachaara- til ke tel ko gonagona karake lagabhag 10 minat parabhaavit hisase kee masaaj karem। es kariya ko dinabhar mem teem se chaar baar karem। garam seesam ke tel mem kochh buumde levemdar ke tel kee daalakar bhee masaaj kee ja sakatee hai। til ko halaka sa bhuunakar roj sobah chabaaem। esake alaava garam duudh mem bhone hoe til daalakar bhee peeya ja sakata hai। ek din mem lagabhag do gilaas duudh peeem। 6. adarak (Ginger)- saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis ke elaaj ke lie adarak bhee behatareen parabhaav dikhaata hai। yah rakat smchaar (blood circulation) ko tej karata hai jisase garadan ke darad se raahat milatee hai। kaise karem upachaara- ek din mem lagabhag teen kap adarak kee chaay peeem। adarak kee chaay banaane ke lie paanee mem adarak ubaalem aur thmda karake esamem shahad milaaem। es pey ko peeem। parabhaavit hisase kee adarak ke tel se masaaj bhee kee ja sakatee hai। 7. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb saaedar siraka bhee saravaaekal sapmdalaaetis se raahat dene mem bahot achachha asar dikhaatee hai। yah garadan ke darad aur suujan se raahat deta hai। kaise karem upachaara- kisee kapaड़e ko se saaedar siraka mem bhigokar parabhaavit sathaan par lapetem aur kochh ghmtom ke lie chhoड़ dem। din mem do baar es vidhi ko karem। do kap seb ke sirake ko gonagone paanee mem daalakar nahaaya bhee ja sakata hai। ek gilaas paanee mem kachacha seb ka siraka aur shahad milaakar peene se bhee laabh hota hai। Disease: vaakavikaar (Dyslexia) Description: disalekasiya koe beemaaree naheem hai aur n hee yah koe maanasik ayogayata hai। disalekasiya (Dyslexia) padha़me-likhane se smbmdhee ek vikaar hai, jisamem bachachom ko shabadom ko pahachaanane, padha़ne, yaad karane aur bolame mem pareshaanee atee hai। ve kochh (Gallstones) Description: pitataashay (Gall Bladder) pitat (Bile) bhmdaaraण ke lie ek chhotee see thailee hai (pitat jigar davaara utapaadit ek paachak ras hai jo khaane mem maujuud vasa ke tuutane nikaalana moshakil hai। ise mem yadi apako gaॉl baledar satom kee shikaayat hai to jaahir hai apane bhee ऑpareshan ka vichaar banaaya hogaa, lekin ऑpareshan se pahale kochh ghareluu upaay apanaakar dekhem, smbhav hai ki patharee gal jaae। kochh ghareluu upaay n keval patharee ko gala demge balaki paachan ko doruusat karake darad ko bhee theek kar demge। aee jaanate haim, ise hee ghareluu upaayom ke baare mem। 1. seb ka juus aur seb ka siraka (Apple and Apple cider vinegar)- seb mem pitat kee patharee ko galaane ka goण hota hai, lekin ese juus ke ruup mem seb ke sirake ke saath lene par yah jayaada asarakaaree hota hai। seb mem maujuud mailik esid (mallic acid) patharee ko galaane mem madad karata hai tatha seb ka siraka livar mem kolesataraॉl naheem banane detaa, jo patharee banane ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। yah ghol n keval patharee ko galaata hai balaki dobaara banane se bhee rokata hai aur darad se bhee raahat deta hai। upachaar ke lie- ek gilaas seb ke juus mem, ek chamamach upachaara- ek gilaas garam paanee mem, ek gilaas naashapaatee ka juus aur do chamamach shahad (honey) milaakar peeem। es juus ko ek din mem teen baar peena chaahie। 3. chokmdara, kheera aur gaajar ka juus (Beetroot, Cucumber and carrot juice)- juus therepee ko pitat kee thailee ke elaaj ke lie ghareluu upachaarom mem sabase jayaada esatemaal kiya jaata hai। chokmdar n keval shareer ka majabuutee ditaॉkaseephaae (detoxify) karatee hai। gaajar mem bhee vitaamin see aur uchach poshak tatav (high nutriemt) hone ke kaaraण yahee goण hote haim। upachaara- ek chokmdara, ek kheera aur chaar gaajar ko lekar juus taiyaar karem। es juus ko paratidin do baar peena hai। juus mem paratayek saamagaree kee maatara baraabar homee chaahie, esalie sabajee ya phal ke saaej ke hisaab se maatara ghataae ya baढ़aae ja sakatee hai। 4. podeena (Mint)- podeena ko paachan ke lie sabase achachhee ghareluu aushadhi (home remedy) maana jaata hai jo pitat vaahika tatha paachan se smbmdhit anay rasom ko baढ़aata mem jaruur shaamil karem। Disease: rebeej (Rabies) Description: rebeeज़ ek nayuuro enavesiv (Neuro-Invasive) vaayaral beemaaree hai। rebeeज़ ka vaayaras tmtarika tmtar yaani semtaral naravas sisatam v saabon se achachhee tarah dho dena chaahie। - dhome ke baad kaate gae sathaan par achachhee tarah se timchar ya povodeen ayodin lagaana chaahie। isa karane se kotate ya anay pashoom kee laar mem paae jaame vaale keetaaणo sirotaaepavan laayasa vaayaras kee gayaalakoparotin kee paratem ghol jaatee haim। esase rog kee maar ek baड़e had tak kam ho jaatee hai, jo rogee ke bachaav mem sahaayak hotee Home Remedies: raibeej vaayaras se phailane vaalee beemaaree hai jo ki manoshay ke dimaag aur sapaaenal korad (spinal cord) ko parabhaavit karatee hai। yadi raibeej ke lakashaण ubharane se pahale esaka elaaj n kiya jaae to vayakati kee maut bhee ho sakatee hai। ise jaanavar jo es vaayaras se aphekated (affected) hote haim, unake salaaeva (salaiva) ya dimaagee otakom (brain membrane) se yah vaayaras duusare logom mem phail jaata hai। yah beemaaree manoshayom ke saath hee anay anay satanadhaariyom mem bhee ho sakatee hai। jaanavarom ke kaatane, chaatane, kharomch lagaane ya kisee jakham laaparavaahee m karem। saabon aur paanee se dhone ke baad tormt chikitasak se milem। 2. akharot (walnut) akharot mem kotate davaara hone vaalee raibeej ke jahar ko maarane kee kashamata hotee hai। upachaar ke lie akharota, payaaj aur namak kee baraabar maatara lekar pees lem। es mitaraण mem thodaa़ shahad milaaem। parabhaavit hisase ya ghaav par yah lep lagaaem। 3. levemdar (lavamder) jaanavar ke kaatane ke sathaan par ya raibeej parabhaavit hisase par levemdar ko pees kar lep lagaane se bhee emphekashan se bacha ja sakata hai। 4. lahason (garlic) lahason mem paraakaृtik taur par emteebaayetik (antibiotic) goण hote haim। raibeej ke ghaav ko jaladee bharane ke lie din mem teen baar lahason kee kalee chabaaem। 5. jeera (cumin) kotate ke kaatane se phailane vaalee raibeej par bmdagobhee (cabbage), tamaatara, rasapabairee, tarabuuja, amaamaas (pine apple) aur paalak adi le sakate haim। esake alaava vitaamin bee ke sapaleememt lema bhee phaayademmd hota hai। nota- yah sabhee upachaar ghareluu haim। enamem se kochh upachaar jaanavar ke kaatane ke tormt baad daॉkatar ke paas pahomchane kee deree kee avasatha mem pahale kie ja sakate haim, taaki emphekashan jayaada n baढ़e ya avasatha ghaatak n ho। saath hee kochh upachaar elaaj ke dauraan lagaataar kie ja sakate haim। lekin raibeej hone kee sathiti mem chikitasak ke paas jaana jaruuree hai, ghareluu upachaar atirikat laabh ke lie haim। Disease: jokaam (Common Cold) Description: jokaam vishaaणoom (vaayarasa) davaara phailaaya jaane vaale smkaramaण hai jo khaasakar hamaare sms paraणaalee ke age vaale hisase ko ki paanee ya balagam naak se baahar ane lagate haim। - hamaare gale mem do tarah ke baikateeriya maujuud hote haim - kochh achachhe aur kochh bore। kabhee-kabhee saradee-garamee badha़ne, ekadam thmdaa-garam khaane, thmde se garam v garam se thmde maahaul mem jaane, thmda paanee jayaada peene ya baarish mem bheegane se gale ke bore baikateeriya sakariy ho jaate haim। ye baikateeriya hee gale vaayaras ke vibhinan parakaar ke kaaraणom se ho sakata hai। sir darada, maak bahanaa, khmsee, tej bokhaara, nkhom mem jalana, gale mem kharaash (Sore throat) aur shareer mem darad (Body pain) adi upayog - ek kap paanee mem lahason kee kalee, do chamamach neembuu ka rasa, ek chamamach shahada, aur adha chamamach laal mirach ya laal mirach paaudar milaaem। ese tab tak roj khaaem jab tak saradee emjaaem (enzyme) mem, uchach maatara mem baikateeriya aur vaayaras ko maarane ke goण hote haim। shahad se gale ka suukhaapam duur hota hai aur jokaam jaladee theek ho jaata hai। kaise karem upayog - kachacha shahad milaaem। jab tak baratan bhar n jaae tab tak parakariya ko doharaaem। katore ko dhak kar rakhem aur 12 se 15 ghmte ke lie chhoda़ dem। payaaj seerap kee tarah motee parat mem jam jaaegaa। 6. chikan ka suup (Chicken soup) - chikan suup kae mem kae avashayak poshak tatav vitaamim haim jo am saradee ke lakashaणom ke upachaar mem madad karate haim। chikan suup ke uchach Disease: bokhaar (Fever) Description: bokhaar ana ek behad am beemaaree hotee hai। vijaञaan ke amosaar yah bokhaar rog naheem balaki rog ka lakashaण hota hai। jaaniem bokhaar ke baarem mem visataar se: Reasons: - shavasan smsathaam vaale bokhaar jaise kee jokaama, phaluu, gale kee suujana, shavaasanalee shotha, nayuumoniyaa, tee.bee. adi। - tavacha ke smkaramaण (Infection) se hone vaale bokhaar jaise kee jakham mem peep honaa, phoड़e ya daane vaale bokhaara। - machachhar ya pisasuu se home vaale bokhaar jaise kee maleriya (Malari Fever), phaayaleriya (Flaria), demguu (Dengue), chikonagonaya (Chickengunia), masatishak javar (Menimgitis), paleg (Plague), adi। en sabhee bokhaarom mem pahale kmpakmpee hotee hai। - paachan smsathaan ke bokhaar jaise dasat ya pechisha, peeleeyaa, taayaphaॉed adi। pechish mem khuun aur balagam girata hai। taayaphaaed khuun ke jaॉmch se hee pata chalata hai। - parajanan aur muutar smsathaan ke bokhaar - esamem peshaab ke samay jalam hotee hai। - anay smkaraamak bokhaar jaise kee baroselaॉseesa, edasa, tapedik ke kochh parakaara, joड़om ka bokhaara। asmkaraamak bokhaarom mem jaise luu lagana aur ऍlarajee se hone vaale bokhaara। Treatments: bokhaar kee kmjee, saabuudaane kee kheer ya khichaड़ee, jau ka paanee adi dena chaahiye। - rogee ko achachhe havaadaar kamare mem rakhana chaahiye। - savachachh evm molaayam vasatar pahanaaem। - yadi javar 39.5 digaree se. ya 103.0 phairemahaaet se adhik ho ya phir 48 ghmtom se adhik samay ho gaya ho to daॉkatar se paraamarash lem। Home Remedies: jab bhee shareer ka taapamaan saamaanay se jayaada hota emphekashan hone par bhee bokhaar hota hai । etana hee naheem saapha- saphaae ka abhaav hone se bhee bokhaar home kee smbhaavana rahatee hai। bokhaar ke saamaanay lakashaणom mem sir darad (Headache), mmsapeshiyom mem darad (Muscle pain) , dihaadareshan (Dehydration) , kae dapha kmpakapee (Shivrimg) to kae baar paseena ana aur kamajoree ho sakate haim। yuum to bokhaar kochh din mem theek ho jaata chaahie। bokhaar ke lie ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies for Fever) thmda paanee (Cold Water) kisee kapaड़e ko thmde paamee mem bhigokar shareer ko pomchhe। esake alaava thmde paanee kee patatiym sir par rakhane se bhee laabh hota he aur shareer ka taapamaan kam hota hai। kapaड़e ko samaya-samay par badalate rahama chaahie। saamaanay bokhaar ke lie yah behad achachhee parakariya hai jo taapamaan ko baढ़ne naheem detee। tolasee (Basil) tolasee bokhaar mem shareer ke taapamaan ko kam karane mem bahot sahaayak hai। yah harab baajaar mem maujuud anay emteebaayotikas (Antibiotics) kee tarah hee kaaray hai kayomki esamem maujuud esid garamaahat ko shareer kee tavacha se baahar kar deta hai। saath hee esamem maujuud minaral shareer ko bokhaar se duur bhee rakhate haim। kisee kapaड़e ko ek bhaag siraka aur do bhaag paanee lekar usamem bhigoem। atirikat paanee ko michoड़ dem aur es patatee ko maathe aur pet par rakhem। ek patatee pair ke talavom par bhee rakhee ja sakatee hai। jaise hee kapaड़a garam ho jaae, dobaara solayuushan mem dobaaem aur parakariya ko doharaaem। lahason (Garlic) lahasom kee garam taaseer bhee shareer mem paseena laakara, shareer ka taapamaan kam kar sakatee hai। yah shareer se haanikaarak vishaakat padaarathom ko bhee baahar nikaalane mem sahaayak hai। etana hee naheem lahason emteephmgal (antifungal) aur emteebaikateeriyal goणom se bhara hai jo shareer ko emayuunitee chhaanakar alag kar lem। es juus mem adhe meembuu ka ras milaaem। mitaraण ko ek dim mem do baar peeem। adarak (Ginger) adarak mem shareer ke taapamaan ko niymtarit karane ke goण hote haim। yuum bhee milaakar es mikasachar ko piem। es mitaraण ko bhee din mem teen se chaar bar liya ja sakata hai। Disease: gale mem kharaash (Sore Throat) Description: mausam badalate hee gale mem kharaash hona am Home Remedies: saamaanayath gale kee mdaruunee parat mem smkaramaण ke kaaraण gale mem kharaash hotee hai। esake alaava kabhee kabhee mausam mem achaamak badalaav hone kee vajah se gale mem kharaash hotee hai aur kae baar tomsil (tonsil) ya gale mem kisee tarah ke emphekashan ke kaaraण bhee kharaash ho sakatee hai। vaise to gale kee kharaash teen chaar din mem theek ho jaatee hai, lekin kochh ghareluu upaayom se gale kee kharaash mem jaladee raahat milatee hai। aee jaamem gale kee kharaash duur karane ke ghareluu upaay 1. garam paanee aur namak ke garaare (Gargle of warm water and salt)- jab gale mem kharaash hotee hai to shaleshama jhilalee (mucous membrane) kee koshikaaom mem suujan ho jaatee hai। namak es suujan (swelling) ko kam karata hai jisase darad mem raahat milatee hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas gonagone paamee mem ek baड़a chamamach namak milaakar ghol lem aur es paanee se garaare karem। es parakariya ko din mem teen baar karem। 2. lahasom (Garlic)- lahason emphekashan (infectiom) paida karane vaale jeevaaणoom ko maar deta hai। esalie gale kee kharaash mem lahason behad phaayademmd hai। lahason mem maujuud eleesin (allicin) jeevaaणoom ko maarane ke saath hee gale kee suujan aur darad ko bhee kam karata hai। upachaar ke lie gaalom ke donom taraph lahason kee ek ek kalee rakhakar dheere dheere chuusate rahem। jaise jaise lahason ka ras gale mem jaaega vaise vaise araam milata rahegaa। lahason ka ras nikaalane ke lie beech beech mem dmtom se kochalate rahem। 3. bhaap lena (Steaming)- kae baar gale ke suukhame ke kaaraण bhee gale mem emphekashan kee shikaayat hotee hai। ise mem kisee baड़e baratan mem garam paanee karake tauliya se momh dhakakar bhaap lem। isa karane se bhee gale kee sikaae hogee aur gale ka emphekashan bhee khatam hogaa। es kariya ko din mem do baar kiya ja sakata hai। 4. laal mirach (Red chilli)- gale kee kharaash ko theek karane ke lie laal mirach bhee behad phaayademmd hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap garam paanee mem ek chamamach laal mirach aur ek chamamach shahad milaakar peeem। 5. bekimg soda (Baking soda)- gale kee kharaash duur karane ke lie bekimg soda kee chaay behad phaayademmd hai। kaaraण, bekimg soda mem emtee baikateeriyal (antibacterial) goण hote haim jo ki jeevaaणoom ko nashat kar dete haim। esake lie ek gilaas garam paanee mem bekimg soda aur mamak milaakar din mem teen baar garaare karem। 6. laumg (Laung or Clove)- laumg ka esatemaal upachaar ke lie sadiyom se hota  raha hai। gale kee kharaash ke upachaar ke lie laumg ko momh mem rakhakar dheere dheere chabaama chaahie। laumg emteebaikateeriyal goणom se bharapuur hotee hai jo gale ke emphekashan aur suujan ko duur karatee hai। 7. adarak (Gimger)- adarak bhee gale kee kharaash kee behad achachhee dava hai। adarak mem maujuud emteebaikateeriyal goण gale ke emphekashan aur darad se raahat dete haim। gale kee kharaash ke upachaar ke lie ek kap paanee mem adarak daal kar ubaalem। esake baad ese halaka gonagona karake esamem shahad milaaem। es pey ko din mem do se teen baar peeem। gale kee kharaash se araam milegaa। 8. masaala chaay (Masal Chay)- laumga, tolasee (basil), adarak aur kaalee mirach (black pepper) ko milata hai। Disease: ubakaae (Nausea) Description: ubakaae ana ulatee hone ka ehasaas maatar hai। kochh logom ko mitalee jayaada atee hai। visheshakar yaatara ke samay kochh logom ko ubakaae kee sathiti gmbhir ho jaay to daॉkatar se salaah lenee chaahie। Home Remedies: matalee ya jee michalaane kee pareshaanee moshan sikanes (Motion sickness), pet ke phaluu (Stomach flu) ya phir apake davaara ka parayaapat oraja naheem mil paatee aur vayakati eneemiya se garasat ho jaata hai। esake saath hee yadi shareer mem pholik esid aur vitaamin bee 12 kee kamee hai tab bhee vayakati eneemiya se garasat ho sakata hai। poruushom kee tolama mem mahilaaem jayaada eneemik paae jaatee haim। shareer ka jaladee thakanaa, chakakar anaa, tavacha mem peelaapana, lagaataar rahane vaala sir darad adi kochh eneemiya ke lakashaणom mem shaamil haim। aee apako bataate haim, eneemiya se raahat paane ke ghareluu upaay (Home remedies for anemia) 1. paalak (Spinach) paalak mem bharapuur lauh tatha vitaamin bee 12 hota hai। esake saath hee paalak pholik esid (Folic Acid) ka bhee uchach satarot hai। ise mem paalak khaane se khuun kee kamee puuree hotee hai। upachaar ke lie paalak ka suup banaakara, ya paalak ka saag adi ko apame roj ke khaane mem shaamil karana chaahie। 2. anaar (Pomegramate) anaar shareer mem heemogalobin (Haemoglobin) ko bahot tejee se baढ़aata hai। amaar mem paroteen aur kaarabohaaedaret kee uchach maatara hotee hai। esamem ayaran aur kailashiyam bhee hota hai। yah khuun mem heemogalobin kee maatara ko tejee se baढ़aakar rakat smchaar ko theek rakhata hai। eneemiya ke upachaar ke lie sobah khaalee pet anaar khaaem aur rojaana anaar ka juus peeem। 3. chokmdar aur seb ka ras (Beetroot and Apple Juice) chokmdar mem pholik esid uchach maatara mem hota hai jabaki seb mem lauh tatav hote haim, ise mem donom hee eneemiya kee kamee ko duur karate haim। upachaar ke lie ek kap chokmdar ke ras aur ek kap seb ke ras mem ek se do chamamach shahad milaakar din hai। rojaana ek se do kachache tamaatar jaruur khaaem। ek gilaas tamaatar ka ras bhee roj peeem aur khaana banaane aur salaad mem bhee tamaatar ka bharapuur upayog karem। 5. khajuur (Dates) khajuur bhee ayaran bahot achachha satarot hai। sau garaam khajuur mem 90 mileegaraam ayaran kee maatara hotee hai। do khajuur ko ek kap duudh mem raat bhar ke lie chhoड़ dem। en khajuur ko sobah khaalee pet chaba chabaakar khaaem। bache hoe duudh ko bhee pee lem। khajuur ko garam paanee mem do ya teen ghmtom ke lie bhigaakar us paanee ko peena bhee phaayademmd hota hai। jin logom ko lekatoj (lectose) se elarajee hai aur duudh naheem le sakate, unake lie yah behatar tareeka hai। 6. kishamish (Kishmish) kishamish bhee eneemiya kee behad achachhee ghareluu dava hai। kishamish mem ayarana, paroteena, phaaebara, sodiyam jaise uchach poshak tatav hote haim। upachaar ke lie ek kap paanee mem 10 se 15 kishamish raatabhar ke lie bhiga dem। sobah en kishamish ko shahad milaakar kha lem aur bache hoe paanee ko pee lem। 7. shahad (Honey) shahad bhee lauh aur vitaamim bee 12 ka uchach satarot hai। shahad ko rojaana khaane se bhee shareer mem emeemiya kee kamee puuree hotee hai। shahad ko phalom mem milaakara, duudh mem daalakar ya cheenee kee jagah shahad esatemaal karake bhee rakat kee kamee puuree kee ja sakatee hai। Disease: dimemshiya (Dementia) Description: dimemshiya (Dementia) vayakati ke paana - cheeज़om ko galata, anochit jagah par rakh chhodana (jaise ki ghadee ko, ya ऑphis phaael ko pharij mem rakh denaa) - chhotee chhotee samasayaaom ko bhee n solajha paana - chhotee-chhotee baat para, ya bina kaaraण hee baukhala jaanaa, chilalaanaa, ronaa, etayaadi - dimemshiya se parabhaavit vayakati mem, rog ke baढ़ne ke saath jayaada aur adhik gmbheer lakashaण naज़r ate haim। (yaad rakhem ki har vayakati mem alag alag lakashaण naज़r ate haim) - nmbar joड़ne aur ghataane mem dikakata, gimatee karane mem dikakat - bolate ya likhate hoe galat shabad ka parayog karanaa, ya shabadom ke arath n samajh paana - baड़ee rakam ko phaalatuu kee sakeem mem daal demaa, paise se samabmdhit ajeeb niraणy lenaa, laaparavaahee ya gairajimamedaaree dikhaana - yah bhuul jaana ki taareekh kaya hai, kaunasa maheena hai, saal kaunasa hai, vayakati kis ghar mem haim, kis shahar mem haim, kis desh mem Reasons: ​dimemshiya kae kaaraणom se ho sakata hai lekim esaka mokhay kaaraण anovmshik hee maana jaata hai। saath hee baढ़tee umar mem es beemaaree se peeड़it hone kee smbhaavana bhee baढ़ jaatee hai। esake aham kaarak niman haim: dimemshiya ke paramokh kaaraण (Causes of Dementi ​in Hindi) - anovmshika: agar parivaar mem koe bhee es beemaaree se peeda़it ho, to khatare kee smbhaavana ba़dh jaatee hai - baढ़tee umar mem es beemaaree ke khatare baढ़ jaate haim। - uchach rakatachaap se peeड़it rogiyom ko dimemshiya ke parati sachet rahana chaahie। - madhomeh aur motaape ko bhee esaka mokhay kaaraण maana jaata hai। - ja़yaada jmk phuud khaane se aur adhonik jeevanashailee se shareer se jaruuree poshak tatav naheem mil paate jis kaaraण dimemshiya (Dementia) hone kee smbhaavana baढ़ jaatee hai। Treatments: dimemshiya se bachaav aur esaka elaaj donom hee smbhav hai। jaruuree hai to keval sahee samay par esakee jaanakaaree honaa। dimemshiya ke dauraan niman baatom ka dhayaan rakhana jaruuree hai: - dimemshiya ka vayakati aur parivaar par kaya asar paड़egaa, yah samajhem aur saveekaarem। - dekhabhaal kae varashom tak chal sakatee hai, esalie yah jaamana jaruuree hai ki rogee kee dekhabhaal ke alaava aur kaya kaya jimamedaariym nibhaanee haim aur dekhabhaal ke lie samay aur paise ka emtajaam kis parakaar karemge। - esalie apanee jimdagee mem usee parakaar se badalaav laaem taaki rogee kee dekhabhaal ke saath saath ap apanee anay jimamedaariym bhee nibha sakem। esake lie jo bhee seekhana hai, vah seekhem, aur khoshee khoshee apane karatavay ka niravaah karem। Home Remedies: dimemshiya ya yaadadaashat ka jaana sabhee ke lie chimta ka kaaraण ho sakata hai। ham sabhee apane dimaag ko savasath rakhana chaahate haim। dimemshiya ke mareej kee yaadadaashat (memmory) jaane ke saath hee usake vayavahaar mem bhee parivaratan hota hai jisase n keval mareej balaki parivaar ke anay sadasay bhee parabhaavit hote haim। aee jaanem dimemshiya se bachane ke lie kochh ghareluu upachaara- 1. cheenee ko avaॉed karem (Avoid sugar) sabase pahale apane khaane se meetha (sweet), kaarabohaaedaret (carbohydrate) tatha riphaaemd kaarabohaaedaret (refined carbohydrate) sabhee ko alag kar dem। jab tak ki apaka vajan niymtarit naheem ho jaata hai, kaarabohaaedat vaalee cheejom ko khaane se bachem। bahot adhik cheemee kho se bhee dimaagee otak (brain membrane) kamajor hote haim jisaka asar yaadadaashat (memmory) par paड़ta hai। 2. haladee (Haldi) haladee mem maujuud tatav karakayuumin (curcumin) dimemshiya se sorakasha paradaan karata hai। haladee mem emteeऑkaseedemt (antioxidant) tatav bhee hote haim jo dimaagee vikaas ke lie jaruuree haim। ise mem bhojan mem haladee ka esatemaal jaruur karem। 3. naariyal tel (Coconut oil) naariyal tel mem khaana banaane se bhee dimemshiya ka upachaar smbhav hai। naariyal tel mem vasa kee maatara bahot jayaada naheem hotee aur yah dimaag ko bhee tej karata hai। 4. salaman machhalee aur mda (Salmon fish and egg) thmde paanee (cold water) mem rahane vaalee machhalee salaman aur mde kee jaradee (egg yolk) donom hee dimaag ko tej banaatee haim। ise mem bhojan mem donom ko shaamil kiya jaana behad jaruuree hai। ek din mem do mde jaruur khaaem। 5. adarak (Ginger) adarak bhee dimemshiya se bachaav ke lie behad phaayademmd hai। adarak kee chaay (ginger tea), khaane mem adarak ka parayog ya suukha adarak (dry ginger), kisee bhee ruup mem adarak khaana dimemshiya mem behad laabhadaayak hai। 6. gareen tee (Green tea) gareen tee bhee achachhe savaasathay v achachhe dimaagee vikaas ke lie behad jaruuree hai। gareen tee peene se shareer mem ऑkaseejan (Oxygen) ka smchaar hota hai aur jamee hoe vasa (Saturated fat) duur hotee hai। esase yaadadaashat baढ़tee hai aur bhuulane kee samasaya duur hotee hai। 7. baadaam (Almomd) baadaam bhee tej dimaag ke lie phaayademmd hota hai। baadaam ke tel mem vasa hotee hai jise khaane se charabee maheem baढ़tee aur dimaag ko anay poshak tatav (mutrient) bhee milate haim, jisase n keval shareer balaki dimaag bhee savasath hota hai। Disease: taaephaaed (Typhoid) Description: taaephaaed ya mt javar ek gmbheer beemaaree hai। es beemaaree mem rogee ko tej bokhaar ke saath ulatee aur dasat adi kee samasaya hotee hai। taaephaaed (Typhoid) ek jaamaleva beemaaree maanee jaatee hai। aeem jaanem esake vishay mem adhik jaanakaaree। Symptoms: - kabaj ya dasat hona - kabhee-kabhee shauch mem khuun ka ama - bokhaar shoruu mem halakaa, par dheere-dheere tej hota jaata hai - bhuukh kam lagana aur ulatiym ana - rog kee gmbheer sathiti mem behoshee bhee  sakatee hai - sira-darad aur badana-darad - suukhee khmsee ana aur pet mem darad Reasons: maana jaata hai ki taaephaaed adhikaatar gmdagee ke kaaraण phailata hai। shauch ke baad smkaramit vayakati davaara haath theek se n dhona aur bhojan banaana ya bhojan ko chhuuna bhee rog phaila sakata hai। kochh anay kaaraण miman haim: - un kashetarom mem kaam karana ya yaatara karana jahm yah beemaaree hai। - galat jeevana-shailee ke kaaraण shareer ke rog paratirodhak tmtar ka kamajor honaa। - peene ke paanee ka jeevaaणo se paraduushit honaa। - shauch ke baad saapha-saphaae ka dhayaan na rakhanaa। Treatments: taaephaaed ka upachaar (Treatment of Typhoid in Hindi) - daॉkatar ke paraamarash se balad tesat ke baad hee daॉkatar ke paraamarash ke anosaar hee chikitasa karaaem। - taaephaaed kee dava ko beech mem n chhoड़em। bokhaar mem peraaseetaamol ka esatemaal karem। - rogee ke shareer mem paanee kee kamee m hone paae, esake lie rogee ko paanee aur anay taral padaarath parayaapat maatara mem dem। - rogee ke asapaas saapha-saphaae ka vishesh dhayaan rakhem। Home Remedies: taaephaaed ka bokhaar paachan tmtar aur baladasatareem (blood stream) mem baikateeriya ke emphekashan ke kaaraण hota hai। salomonela taaephee (salomonel typhi) naam ka yah baikateeriya (bacteria) paanee, kisee pey ya khaane ke saath hamaare shareer ke mdar paravesh karata hai aur paachan tmtar mem jaakar yah baikateeriya baढ़ jaate haim। yah baikateeriya shareer ke bheetar ek jagah se duusaree jagah jaise, livara, sapaleena, gaॉlabaledar adi jagahom par ghuumate rahate haim। taaephaaed ka bokhaar adhikmshat duushit paanee (polluted water) peene se hota hai। taaephaaed ke lakashaणom mem sir mem darad (headache), pet mem darad (pain im stomach) aur bokhaar ka hona hai lekin taaephaaed ke bigaड़ne par ulatee (Vomiting), daayariya (diarrhea), mal mem khuun ana (blood im stool), livar ka baढ़na (enlargement of liver) adi bhee ho sakate haim। taaephaaed mem laaparavaahee maheem baratanee chaahie tatha esaka koras puura kiya jaama bhee jaruuree hai kayomki esake dobaara hone ke chmses bhee rahate hai। taaephaaed se nijaat ke lie yahm ham apako kochh ghareluu nosakhom ke baare mem bataaemge jinahem apanaakar ap taaephaaed se raahat pa sakate haim। 1. thmda paanee (Cold water) kisee kapaड़e ko thmde paanee mem bhigokar shareer ko pomchhe। esake alaava thmde paamee kee patatiym sir par rakhane se bhee laabh hota he aur shareer ka taapamaan kam hota hai। kapaड़e ko samay samay par badalate rahana chaahie। saamaanay bokhaar ke lie yah behad achachhee parakariya hai jo taapamaan ko baढ़ne naheem detee। nota- esake lie baraph ya baraph ke paanee kee esatemaal n karake, taaje paanee ka esatemaal karem। 2. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar) seb ka siraka bhee bokhaar ke lie behad sasatee aur parabhaavee dava hai। esase bokhaar ko tejee se duur hota hai kayomki esamem maujuud esid garamaahat ko shareer kee tavacha se baahar kar deta hai। saath hee esamem maujuud minaral shareer ko bokhaar se duur bhee rakhate haim। kaise karem upayog kisee kapaड़e ko ek bhaag siraka aur do bhaag paanee lekar usamem bhigoem। atirikat paanee ko nichoड़ dem aur es patatee ko maathe aur pet par rakhem। ek patatee pair ke talavom par bhee rakhee ja sakatee hai। jaise hee kapaड़a garam ho jaae, dobaara ghol mem dobaaem aur parakariya ko doharaaem। 4. lahasom (Garlic) lahason kee garam taaseer bhee shareer mem paseena laakara, shareer ka taapamaan kam kar sakatee hai। yah shareer se haanikaarak vishaakat padaarathom ko bhee baahar nikaalane mem sahaayak hai। etana hee naheem lahasom emteephmgal (antifungal) aur emteebaikateeriyal (Antibacterial) goणom se bhara hai jo shareer ko emayuunitee (Immunity) deta hai। kaise karem upayog lahason kee ek kalee ko peesakar garam paanee mem milaaem। 10 mimat dhak kar rakhem। paanee ko chhaan lem aur ghuumt ghuumt karake dheere dheere peeem। ek din mem es pey ko do baar peeem। agale hee din ap bokhaar se raahat mahasuus karemge। do chamamach ऑliv ऑyal (olive oil) mem do kalee lahason kee daalakar bhuunem। es tel ko thmda karake pair ke talavom (sole of feet) mem lagaaem। 5. tolasee (Basil) tolasee bhee taaephaaed ke bokhaar ke lie utatam aushadhi hai। esake emteebaikateeriyal (Antibacterial) aur emteebaayotik (Antibiotic) goण baikateeriya ko khatam karate hai, jisase bokhaar jaladee bhee theek hota hai। kaise karem upayog podeene kee bees patatiyom mem ek chhotee chamamach adarak (Ginger) ko kadaduukas karake ek kap paamee mem ubaal lem। es paanee ko gonagona rahane tak emtajaar karem। esake baad ese chhaanakar esamem shahad milaakar peeem। es pey ko din do se teen baar le sakate haim। 6. laumg (Laung or clove) laumg mem taaephaaed ko theek karane ke goण hote haim। laumg ke tel mem emteebaikateeriyal (Antibacterial) goण hote haim jo ki baikateeriya ko maar dete haim। kaise karem upayog ath kap paanee mem 5 se 7 laumg daalakar ubaal lem। jab paanee adha rah jaae ese chhaam lem। es paanee ko puura din peeem। es upachaar ko ek haphate lagaataar karem। Disease: juun (Lice) Description: juum (Head Lice) til ke akaar kee ek chhotee parajeevee hai jo manoshay ke shareer mem paida ho jaatee haim। saamaanayata: yah baalom mem paaye jaate haim। ye bada़ee tejee se chal sakatee haim। es kaaraण baalom ke beech enahem khojana kathin ho jaata hai। ye sabhee umar tatha parajaatiyom ke logom ko smkaramit karatee haim। Symptoms: - sir mem khojalee homa Reasons: joem tejee se, ek vayakati se duusare vayakati tak phail sakatee haim। yah behad tejee se chalatee haim। joom ke phailame ke kochh kaaraण niman haim: joem phailane ke kaaraण (Cause of Head Lices in Himdi) - haita, sakaarapha, kmghee, barasha, heyar kalip athava baireta, heyar baimda, helamet athava kapada़om, ka adala-badalakar esatemaal karate haim। - ek hee bisatara, palmg athava kaaleen ka parayog karate/karatee haim। - bahot nikat rahakar khelate haim। - ise alamaaree athava laॉkar mem rakhee gae, vasatoom ka parayog karate haim, jin mem joem athava unake mde maujuud hote haim। Treatments: kaise roke juum ko phailane se (Treatment of Head Lice in Hindi) - saamaanay shaimapuu se baal saaph karem। kmdeeshamar ka parayog n karem। esake kaaraण joom kee dava ka parabhaav samaapat ho sakata hai। - garam paanee se baal dhokar unahem tauliye se sokha lem। es tauliye ka dobaara parayog tab tak n karem, jab tak yah dho n liya jaae। - baalom par saphed siraka lagaaem - yah us ‘gomda’ ko dheela karane mem sahaayak hota hai, jo ‘leekhom’ ko baalom se chipakaae hoe hai। - baalom ko maheen kmghee se saaph karem, jisase ye mde nikal aem। baalom ko edhara-udhar karake kmghee karana upayogee ho sakata hai। - sabhee mdom ka hataaya jaana avashayak hai। esamem 2 athava 3 ghmte ya adhik samay lag sakata haim, tatha yadi kmghee kaam naheem karatee hai to apako haathom sm mde chomane pada़ sakate haim। - parivaar mem jitane logom ko juumem haim sab ka upachaar ek saath ho। - kapaड़e bisatar adi dhuup mem rakhem ya garam paanee mem dhoem। - ruusee - ruusee - baalom ka jhaड़na Home Remedies: juun ek chhota parajeevee (parasite) hai jo baalom kee jaड़om aur baalom ke nichale hisase par chipake rahate haim, jahm yah sir kee tavacha se khuun ko peekar jimda rahate haim। bachachom mem juun hone kee samasaya am hai। yadi ap juun vaale kisee vayakati ke smparak mem ate haim to yah apako bhee ho sakate haim। saath hee emphekated vayakati ka saamaan jaise kmghee aur kapaड़e adi esatemaal karane se bhee juun hone kee smbhaavana rahatee hai। sir mem juun hone ka sabase am lakashaण hai sir mem khojalee hona aur sir kee tavacha par laal chakatate paड़naa। yah bahot tejee se baढ़te haim esalie enahem jaladee khatam karana bahot moshakil hota hai। kochh ghareluu upachaar ke davaara juun se mijaat paae ja sakatee hai। aee apako bataaem ise hee kochh ghareluu upachaar ke baare mem- 1. lahason (Garlic)- lahason kee tej mahak joom ka dam ghotatee hai aur unahem maar detee hai। kaise karem upayog ath se das lahason kee kaliyom ko peesakar esamem neembuu ka ras milaaem aur baalom kee jaड़om mem lagaaem। adhe ghmte baad baalom ko garam paanee se dho lem। lahasom kee kaliyom ko peesakara, usamem khaane vaala tel milaaem। esake baad esamem shaimpuu ya kmdeeshanar mem milaakar baalom mem lagaaem। adhe ghmte ke lie baalom ko yuum hee chhoड़ dem aur dho dem। 2. bebee ऑyal (Baby oil)- bebee ऑyal mem kapaड़e dhone vaala ditarajemt aur kochh siraka milaakar baalom mem lagaane se bhee juun ka elaaj smbhav hai। bebee ऑyal bhee juun ka dam ghomt deta hai jisase vah mar jaatee haim। kaise karem upayog bebee ऑyal ko baalom mem lagaakara, patale dmtom vaalee kmghee se baal kaaढ़em। juun giranee shoruu ho jaaemgee। esake baad baalom ko ditarajemt aur garam paanee se dho lem। sone jaane se pahale baalom mem siraka lagaaem aur baalom ko shaavar kaip se dhak lem aur puuree raat yuum hee chhoड़ dem। sobah saamaanay shaimpuu se baal dho lem। shaimpuu ke baad kmdeeshanar karem। 3. ऑliv ऑyal (Olive oil)- ऑliv ऑyal bhee juun maarane mem bahot parabhaavee hai। kaise karem upayog baalom mem kisee bhee parakaar ka ऑliv ऑyal sone se pahale lagaaem। shaavar kaip lagaakar raat bhar tel ko baalom mem yuum hee chhoड़ dem। sobah mem baalom ko kmghee karem, juun baahar nikal aemgee। esake baad baalom ko shaimpuu kar lem। adha kap ऑliv ऑyal mem adha kap kmdeeshanar milaakar esamem kochh likavid saabon milaaem। ese baalom kee jaड़om mem lagaakar ek ghmta chhoड़ dem aur baal dho lem aur kmghee karake juun baahar nikaal dem। ese ek haphate baad dobaara doharaaem। 4. namak (Salt)- namak bhee juun nikaalane mem behad asarakaaree hai। kaise karem upayog ek chauthaae kap namak mem etana hee siraka milaakar es ghol ko baalom mem sapare karem। sapare kie hoe geele baalom par shaavar kaip pahanem aur do ghmte yuum hee chhoड़ dem। esake baad baal dho lem aur baalom par kmdeeshanar karem। har teesare din es parakariya ko doharaaem। 5. petaroliyam jelee (Petrolium jelly)- petaroliyam jelee remgane vaale (roaming around) joom ko tormt maar detee hai। kaise karem upayog sone se pahale baalom kee jaड़om mem petaroliyam jelee lagaaem। esake baad kapaड़e se baalom ko bmdh kar so jaaem। sobah bebee ऑyal se jelee hataaem aur kmghee karake juun ko baahar nikaalem। 6. naariyal ka tel (Coconut oil) naariyal ka tel remgane vaale joom par asar dikhaata hai saath hee enakee smkhaya ko baढ़ne se rokata hai। kaise karem upayog sabase pahale baalom ko seb ke sirake (Apple cider vinegar) se dhoem। baalom ko puuree rah sokhaakar jaड़om mem naariyal ka tel lagaaem। chhah se ath ghmtom ke lie baalom ko yuum hee chhoड़ dem। esake baad baalom ko shaimpuu karake kmghee karem aur juun nikaalem। 7. saphed siraka (White vinegar) saphed sirake mem maujuud eseetik esid juun ko maarata hai। yah juum ko maarane ka sorakashit aur sasata tareeka hai। kisee tel mem saphed siraka milaakar baalom mem lagaakar kochh ghmte chhoड़ dem aur phir shaimpuu karem। Disease: kabaj (Constipation) Description: kabaj ek behad am beemaaree bam chokee hai। mal tayaag ek paraakaृtik kariya hai। lekin jab mal tayaag karane mem agar pareshaanee atee hai to us samasaya ko kabaj (Kabj) kahate haim। aniyamit khaanapaan aur galat jeevamashailee ke kaaraण yah beemaaree lagaataar baढ़tee ja rahee hai। Symptoms: - imthan ho, darad ho, pet phuul jaae ya matalee ho - isa mahasuus ho ki apakee mtaड़iym puuree tarah se khaalee maheem hoe ho - mal tayaag ke lie ज़or lagaana paड़e Reasoms: - ise ahaar jinamem charabee aur shakakar jayaada hom aur reshe kam hom। - kaaphee maatara mem taral padaarath n lenaa। - nishakariy rahanaa। - jab ap ko mal tayaag kee echachha ho tab shauchaalay n jaanaa। Treatmemts: kaise duur karem kabaज़ (Treatment of Constipation in Hindi) - din mem kam se kam 8-10 gilaas paanee peena chaahie। gonagone ya garam paanee se apakee ntom ko asaamee se kaam karane mem madad mil sakatee hai। - barain siriyala, hol garen bareda, kachachee sabajiym, taaje ya sokhaaye hoe phala, suukha meva aur paॉpakaॉran jaisee adhik reshe vaalee cheejem khaaee। reshe shareer se mal ko nikalane mem madad karate haim। - cheeज़, chaॉkalet aur aणkadem adi kam khaana chaahie kayomki enase kabaj (Kabj) baढ़ sakatee hai। - mal ko naram karane ke lie aluu bokhaare ya seb ka ras peejie। - apanee ntom ko theek se kaam karane mem madad karane ke lie kasarat keejie। - kabaj mem paidal chalane se laabh hota hai। - jab ap ko mal tayaag karane kee echachha ho, shauchaalay jaaem। - eneema ka upayog karane se pahale apane chikitasak kee salaah lem। Home Remedies: - ek chotakee kaala mamak gomagone paanee mem daalem aur use sobah khaalee pet peekar 15 minat tak chahalakadamee karem, kabaज़ mem avashay hee raahat milegee। - apane bhojan mem mote anaaj (Bran) ka samaavesh karem। mausam ke anosaar upalabadh salaad ko shaamil karane se kabaj aur pet kee duusaree tamaam samasayaaom se sathaae ruup se chhotakaara paaya ja sakata hai। - alasee ke beej (Flaxseed) ka sevan bhee kabaज़ se araam dilaata hai। alasee ke beej ko sobah kaॉranaphalekas (Cornflax) ke saath milaakar kha sakate haim ya phir motathee bhar alasee ke beej ko garam paanee ke saath sobah kha sakate haim। - kishamish phaaebara(Fiber) se bharapuur hotee hai aur paraakaृtik jolaab kee tarah kaam karatee hai। १०-१२-kishamish ko raat mem paanee mem bhigokar rakh dem aur sobah khaalee pet khaaem। garabhaavasatha (Pregnancy) mem mahilaao ko akasar kabaज़ kee shikaayat rahatee hai, garabhavatee mahilaaom (Pregnant Females)ke lie yah bahot laabhakaaree upaay hai। - amaruud (Gauva) bhee kabaज़ mem bahot raahat pahomchaata hai। ek gilaas gomagone paanee mem neembuu (Lime) aur namak (Salt) milaakar sobah khaalee pet peene se bhee kabaज़ mem kaaphee araam milata hai। Disease: uchach rakatachaap (High Blood Pressure) Description: haae balad pareshar ya uchach rakatachaap kee samasaya ajakal behad am hotee ja rahee hai। uchach rakatachaap ke dauraam mareej ke shareer mem rakat ka paravaah behad tej ho jaata hai। es rahama - chakakar ana - tmgom mem darad - tanaav hona - maak se khuun ama - meemd n ana - lagaataar siradarad homaa, sir chakaraana - sms lene mem kathimaae - sir ke peechhe v garadan mem darad -
