mahatavapuuraण hai aseen jeevamashailee। shaareerik sharam kee kamee ke kaaraण bhee kae baar yah beemaaree logom ko pareshaan karatee hai। uchach rakatachaap ke kae amay kaaraण niman haim: uchach rakatachaap ke kaaraण (Reason for High Blood Pressure) - dhuumarapaan - motaapa - nishakariyata - namak ka jayaada sevan - sharaab peena - tanaav - baढ़tee umar - anovmshikata - paarivaarik etihaas - poraanee kidamee kee beemaaree - thaaeroed disaऑradar Treatments: rakatachaap (Blood Pressure) baढ़ne par kis tarah apana dhayaan rakhana esakee jaanakaaree homa behad jaruuree hai। saath hee samaya-samay par daॉkataree jmch es beemaaree se bachaane mem bahot kaaragar hotee hai। uchach rakatachaap se bachame ke kochh paramokh upaay niman haim: - paratidin ek ghmta halaka ya tej kisee parakaar ka vayaayaam jaruur karem। - khaane mem haae phaaebar vaale cheejem lenee chaahie। - khod ko ekativ rakhane ka adhik se adhik parayaas karana chaahie। - samaya-samay par daॉkatar kee salaah lenee chaahie। Home Remedies: uchach rakatachaap (High Blood Pressure) yuum to jeevanashailee se smbmdhit ek saamaanay beemaaree hai lekin yahee kae anay baड़ee bimaariyom kee shoruuvaat ya vajah bhee hai। kae baar uchach rakatachaap se vayakati kee maृtayo tak smbhav hai। dil kee bimaariym (Heart Disease), enajaaena (Engina) aur satarok (Stroke) adi sabhee samasayaaem uchach rakatachaap ke kaaraण hotee haim yahm tak kee kae baar shogar ke lie bhee uchach rakatachaap jimamedaar hota hai। haalmki yadi apane savaasathay ka dhayaan rakha jaae to kae ghareluu upaayom se bhee uchach rakatachaap ko theek kiya jaana smbhav hai। aee jaanate haim kochh ise hee ghareluu upachaarom ke baare mem। uchach rakatachaap ke lie ghareluu nosakha़e (Home Remedies for High Blood Pressure) lahason (Garlic) lahason ko khaalee pet sobah kachacha hee khaaem। lahason mem rakat ko patala karane ke goण hote haim jo ki rakat ka thakaka jamane se bhee rokata hai। chikitasak se paraamarash lekar lahason kar parayog shoruu kar sakate haim। shahajan kee phalee (Drum Sticks) shahajan mem paroteena, vitaamin aur anay poshak tatav maujuud hote haim jo ki shaareerik savaasathay kee daृshati se behad jaruuree haim। shahajan ka upayog karane ka asaan tareeka hai ki esakee phaliyom ko daal ke saath banaakar khaaya jaae। esase bhee uchach rakatachaap naॉramal hota hai। mvala (Indian Gooseberry) mvala mem vitaamim see kee uchach maatara hotee hai jo ki shareer se kolesataraॉl (cholesterol) kee maatara ko kam karatee hai। esase dil savasath rahata hai aur uchach rakat chaap niymtarita। muulee (Radish) rasoeghar mem parayog hone vaalee am sabajee hai muulee, lekin esamem uchach rakatachaap ko miymtarit karane ke goण hote haim। muulee ko salaad ke ruup mem kachacha ya dahee ke saath milaakar khaaya ja sakata hai। til (Sesame) til daayasatolik aur sisatolik (Diastolic and Systolic) , donom tarah ke rakatachaap ko niymtarit karata hai। til ke tel mem sisamin (Sesamim) aur sisaminaॉl (Sesaminol) donom hote haim jo ki shareer ke tanaav ko kam karane mem aham bhuumika nibhaate haim। til ka khaane mem parayog karane se uchach rakatachaap ko niymtarit kiya ja sakata hai। til ke ladaduu ya til ka paaudar salaad ya daal sabajee mem opar se chhida़kakar khaame se laabh hota hai। alasee ke beej (Flex Seed) alasee ke beej omegaa-3 phaitee esid mem se ek hai jisase esamem alapha linolenik esid (Alf Limolenic Acid) maamak yaugik kee uchach maatara hotee hai। yah uchach rakatachaap ko miymtarit karane ke saath hee kelaॉsataraॉl kee maatara bhee ghataata hai jisase haृday bhee savasath banata hai। Disease: dmt ka darad (Toothache) Description: dmt hamaare shareer ka mahatavapuuraण hisasa haim। baat mosakoraane kee ho ya kochh khaane kee bina dmt sab bekaar hai। lekin kisee bhee kaaraण yadi dmtom mem darad ho jaae to vayakati baichen ho jaata hai। dmtom ka darad yuum to ek am samasaya hai, lekin esaka darad asahaneey hota hai। Symptoms: - chabaane mem darad hona - bokhaara, siradarad - sms lene mem kathimaae Reasons: dmtom mem darad ke kae kaaraण ho sakate haim। dmtom kee theek se saphaae n karanaa, dmtom mem kaivitee hona ya atayadhik meetha khaanaa। esake saath hee chaay kaaphee jayaada peenaa। esake saath hee kochh anay kaaraण bhee haim jaise: dmtom mem darad ka kaaraण (Causes of Tooth Pain) 1. masuuड़om mem emphekashana- yadi kisee bhee kaaraण se masuuड़om mem emphekashan hai to yah dmt darad ka kaaraण ho sakata hai। esake kaaraण tuuth enemal (Tooth Enamel) kee samasaya bhee hotee hai। esase dmtom mem thmda garam laganaa, momh ka savaad bigaड़naa, garadan kee galaimd mem suujan anaa, masuuड़om mem suujan anaaadi samasayaaem  sakatee haim। 2. kaiviteeja- esake kaaraण dmtom kee oparee parat nashat ho jaatee hai। kaॉrabohaaedaret vaala khaama jisamem bareda, soda kek ya kaimdee adi dmtom par chipak jaae aur achachhee tarah se saaph n ho to kaivitee (Cavity) ho sakatee hai jisaka pariणaam hota hai dmtom mem darada। 3. dmt mem keeड़aa- esase dmt puuree tarah khokhala ho jaata hai aur unamem khaana bhar jaata hai। jo ki darad ka kaaraण banata hai। darad ke kaaraण dmt kaam naheem karata aur un par ek parakaar kee gmdagee jamane lagatee hai। 4. tuute dmta- kochh khaate vakat ya kisee anay kaaraण se yadi dmt tuut gae haim to ise dmtom mem darad kee shikaayat akasar rahatee hai। ise dmtom ke ememal kamajor ho jaatee hai jisase ye semsitiv ho jaate haim। 5. philimga- yadi dmtom mem philimg (Tooth Filling) karaae gae ho to yah bhee kae baar yah dmt darad ka kaaraण ho sakatee hai। Treatments: ​dmt darad hone par thmde paanee se kolala karana phaayademmd hota hai lekin agar esase puuraण araam naheem mil paae to nimam upaay karane chaahie: - koe penakilar lem। - aes paik ya taॉvel mem aes lapetakar use gaalom par kochh der ke lie rakhem। agar gaalom mem suuja़m  jaae aur darad ho to pharoja़en peeja़ ko aesapaik kee jagah lagaaen। ye chehare ke akaar ke anosaar badal sakate haim। - agar do dinom mem darad maheem jaata to denatisat (Dentist) ke paas jaaen। ho sakata haim ja़yaada kaॅvitee ya karaik kee vajah se darad ho। - dmt ka daॉkatar apake momh kee jmch karega aur ekasa-re legaa। phir dmt ka daॉkatar dmt ko theek karega ya nikaal degaa। apako darad nivaarak davaaem ya emteebaayotik leme ke lie kaha ja sakata hai। daॉkatar kee bataae gae davaaem lem। Home Remedies: dmtom ka darad vaise to ek saamaanay samasaya hai, lekin esaka darad asahaneey hota hai। yadi apako bhee kabhee dmt mem darad ho to ghabaraaem naheem, kochh ghareluu upaay apanaakar ap es takaleeph se bach sakate haim। 1. laumga- yadi dmt mem darad ho to laumg ka tel ruue mem bhigokar dmt par lagaaee। koshish keejie ki tel masuuड़om par n lage kayomki esase halakee jalan mahasuus ho sakatee hai। 2. elakohala- jee hm apane theek paढ़a elakohala। ek sip elakohal se kolala karane par bhee darad mem araam milata hai। esase darad vaala hisasa sonan ho jaata hai। lekin sathaae yah elaaj naheem hai। 3. vikasa- vikas ko apane chehare ke us hisase kee taraph lagaaee jis taraph dmt mem darad ho। esake baad chehare ko dhmk lem। esase darad mem araam milata hai। 4. aesa- baraph ke tokaड़e se sikaae karane par bhee dmt darad mem behad araam milata hai। 5. kaalee miracha- kaalee mirach ke paaudar ko masuuड़om par ragaड़me se bhee darad ka hisasa sonan ho jaata hai aur darad mem araam milata hai। 6. kachachee payaaja- kachachee payaaj ko 3 minat tak darad vaale hisase par ragaड़em, esase bhee darad mem bahot araam milata hai। 7. lahasona- lahason kee kalee ko chabaakar usake ras ko laar ke saath milakaar kolala karem। kochh hee sekemd mem darad mem araam milegaa। 8. kolala karem। lekin dhayaan rahe ese kabhee nigalem naheem। esase bhee dmt darad mem araam milata hai। Disease: demguu (Dengue) Description: demguu, maada edeej (Female Aedes) machachhar ke kaatane se Water) mem panapate haim। demguu ke dauraan rogee ke joड़om mem tej darad (Pain in Joimts) hota hai tatha sir mem bhee darad (Headache) kaaphee tej hota hai। baड़om ke mokaabale yah bachachom mem chaar baar lee ja sakatee hai। papeete kee patatee (Papay Leaves) papeete kee patatiym, demguu ke bokhaar ke lie sabase asarakaaree dava kahee jaatee hai। papeete kee patatiyom mem maujuud papen Treatments: maleriya ka paraathamik upachaar (Treatment of Malari in Hindi) - maleriya mem kalorokavin jaisee emtee-maleriyal dava (Chloroquine- Anti malarial medicine) dee jaatee hai। en davaaom ke saaed - ephekatas ho sakate haim, esalie enahem daॉkatar kee salaah ke bina m lem। - mareej ko puura araam karane dem। use har chhah ghmte mem pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol in Malaria) dem aur baara- baar paanee aur taral cheejem ( neebuu paanee , chhaachh , naariyal paanee adi ) pilaaem। - maleriya bokhaar ke dauraan bachachom ka khaas khayaal rakhem। - bachache naajok hote haim aur unaka emayuun hadadiyom ke dhmche ko sorakashit rakhate haim। baadaam ka duudh (Almond Milk) baadaam ke duudh mem kailashayim kee uchach maatara hotee hai। esalie baadaam ka duudh ऑsatiyoporosis ke behad achachha upachaar hai। baadaam ke duudh mem hadadiyom ke lie jaruuree tatav maiganeeshiyama, maiganeej aur pauteshiyam bhee shaamil hote haim। ise mem roj ek gilaas baadaam vaala duudh niyamit ruup se peeem। til ke beej (Sesame Seeds) apane bhojan mem til ke beej shaamil karame se hadadiyom kee kamajoree duur hotee hai। til mem bhee kailashiyam kee uchach maatara hotee hai, jo ki hadadiyom ke savaasathay ke lie sabase jaruuree poshak tatav hai। esake saath hee til mem maiganeeshiyama, phaॉsaphorasa, maimganeeja, tmba (Copper), jasata (Zinc) aur vitaamin dee bhee hota hai। upachaar ke lie ek motathee bhone hoe til chaba kar duudh peeem। esake alaava khaane banaane mem bhee bhone hoe tilom ko opar se daalakar khaaya ja sakata hai। anaanaas (Pine Apple) anaanaas mem ऑsatiyoporosis ko rokane ke lie jaruuree maimganeej shaamil hai। maimganeej kee kamee se hadadiyom ka ghamatav kam aur hadadiym patalee ho sakatee haim, ise mem amaanaas khaane se maimganeej kee kamee puuree hotee hai। upachaar ke lie har roj khaana khaane se pahale ek kap anaanaas ko khaaem। esake saath hee anaanaas ka juus bhee piya ja sakata hai। dhaniya ke beej (Coriander Seed) dhamiya ke patate aur beej donom mem hee maigameeshiyama, ayarana, kailashiyama, poteshiyam aur maimganeej adi poshak tatav hote haim। dhamiya ke beejom ko garam paanee mem ubaalakar kochh der dhak kar rakhem usake baad gomagona rahane par usame shahad milaakar peeem। khaane ke chhaumk mem bhee dhaniya ke beejom ka esatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। hare dhamiya ka esatemaal bhee khaana banaane aur chatanee ke ruup mem karana chaahie। Disease: baresat kaimsar (Breast Cancer) Descriptiom: maanav shareer ke avayav aur otak koshikaaom (sela) se bane hote haim। kaimsar en koshikaaom ka ek rog hai। baresat kaimsar doniya mem tejee se phailame vaalee khataranaak beemaariyom mem se ek hai। baresat kaimsar (Breast Cancer) ya satan kaimsar kee adhikatar rogee mahilaaem hotee haim। poroshom ko bhee satan kaimsar ho sakata hai, lekin esakee smbhaavana bahot kam hotee hai। Symptoms: - satanom ke baare mem jaan lene ka saral tareeka hai T L C yaani T - TOUCH Your Breasts (apane satanom ko chhoem) kaya apako kochh asaamaanay lagata hai? kaya ap satan mem, chhaatee ke oparee hisase mem, ya bagalo mem koe gnth (Lump) mahasuus karatee haim? kaya apako satanom ke opar koe parat mahasuus hotee hai jo hatatee naheem? kaya satanom mem saadhaaraण sa darad hai। L - LOOK for changes (kochh badalaav to nahee lagataa) kaya satanom ke akar ya banaavat ( shape or texture) mem koe badalaav hai? kaya satanom ke akar ya akaृti (size or shape) mem koe badalaav hai (koe ek satan duusare ke mokaabale chhota ya baड़a haim)? satanom kee tavacha kee banaavat mem koe badalaav jaise फ़tee फ़tee see ya koe gadada sa paड़ jaanaa? rmg mem badalaav jaise kee nipapalas ke asapaas sorakh laal rmga.ho jaanaa? kaya nipapal kee disha sahee hai, kaheem vah mdar kee taraph to mahee moड़ gaya hai? kisee bhee nipapal se taral padaaradh ka risanaa? nipapal ke as paas kisee paradaarath ka risana ya papaड़ee ka jamanaa? C - CHECK any unusual findings with your doctor (kochh asaamaanay sa mahasuus ho to tormt hee daॉkatar se salaah lem) kaya apako kochh asaamaanay ya alag sa mahasuus ho raha hai? agar isa hai to tormt hee daॉkatar se salaah lem। samay samay par apane satanom kee jmch savaym karate rahem isa karane se ap umame saamaamay taur par ane vaale badalaavom aur asaamaanay badalaav ke baare mem jaan jaayemge, akasar maasik dharam (Menses) ke samay satamom mem kochh badalaav avashay ata hai। lakashaणom ke ubharane ka emtaज़aar n karem, niyamit ruup se satanom kee jmch karavaaem। yah saravavidit hai ki rokathaam elaaज़ se behatar hai Reasons: baresat kaimsar ke kaaraण (Reason for Breast Cancer) kae log maamate haim ki baresat kaimsar anovmshik hota hai jo puuree tarah sahee tathay naheem hai। satan ya baresat kaimsar ke kochh aham kaaraण niman haim: - ayo-satam kaimsar home ka jokhim ayo ke saath badha़ta hai। - yadi apako pahale kaimsar ya satan ka koe anay rog ho ho। - paarivaarik etihaas - keval 5–10% satan kaimsar hee amovmshik ruup se paraapat jeen ke kaaraण hote haim। satan kaimsar ka khatara kin mahilaaom ko jayaada hota hai? - adhik umar kee mahilaaem। - jin mahilaaom kee mm, bahan ya betee ko satan kaimsar ho ho - janam ke samay se hee karomoज़om (goणsuutaro) mem badalaav ho। - mahila jise bachache na hoe hom, ya 30 saal kee umar ke baad bachache hoe hom। - jise 12 saal kee umar se pahale hee peeriyadas shoro ho gae hom। - jis mahila ko 50 saal kee umar ke baad menopaॉj (rajonivaृtati) hoe ho। - jis mahila kee satan ke otak kaaphee ghane hom। apakee memogaraaphee karake daॉkatar ye jaanakaaree de sakate hai। - jo mahila garabh nirodhak goliyom ka lmbe arase se esatemaal kar rahee ho। - jo mahila din mem 2 se 5 baar sharaab ka sevan karatee ho। - jis mahila ko memopaॉj ke baad jayaada motaapa  gaya ho। - jis mahila ne haaramon ripalesamemt therepee esatemaal kee ho। - jo mahilaaem apane bachachom ko satanapaan naheem karavaateem। haaramon smbmdhee kaarak esatarojam aur parojesatarojan naamak haaramon se lmbe samay tak samaparak mem ane se apaka satan kaimsar ka jokhim baढ़ sakata hai। jeevanashailee smbmdhee kaarak lamabe samay tak paratidin do peg se jayaada sharaab peena tatha dhuumarapaan se apaka satan kaimsar ka jokhim baढ़ sakata hai| vajan jayaada hona bhee satan kaimsar ka kaaraण bam sakata hai। Treatments: - agar apako thoड़a sa bhee smshay ho to tormt daॉkatar kee salaah leejiye। - chhote satan Home Remedies: satan kaimsar (Breast cancer), sabase am kaimsar mem se ek hai। satan kaimsar ek kmpalekas beemaaree (Complex disease) hai jisake hone ke lie kae phaikatara, jaise anovmshik (Heredity), khaana-paam aur jeevan shailee jimamedaar hote haim। chikitasa visheshajaञom kee maanem to ane vaale samay mem satan kaimsar se peeड़it rogiyom kee smkhaya aur bhee tejee se baढ़gee। haalmki jeevan shailee mem badalaav karake satan kaimsar se kaaphee had tak bacha ja sakata hai। jaamie satan kaimsar se bachaav ke ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies for Breast Cancer): 1. gareem tee (Green tea)- ek gilaas paanee mem harabal gareen tee ko adha hone tak ubaalem aur phir use peeem। yah phaayademmd hotee hai aur esase satan kaimsar ka khatara kaaphee kam ho jaata hai। 2. mguur aur anaar ka juus (Grapes and pomegranate juice)- rojaana mguur ya anaar ka juus peene se satan kaimsar se bacha ja sakata hai। en donom phalom ke juus mem kaimsar ke selas ko maarane kee kashamata hotee hai, jisase satan kaimsar ka khatara kam ho jaata hai। 3. lahasom (Garlic)- lahason mem phalevonas (flavons) aur phalevonolas (flavonols) jaise emtee baikateeriyal tatav hote haim। roj lahason ka sevan karane se satan kaimsar kee smbhaavana ko roka ja sakata hai। 4. haladee (Turmeric)- haladee mem karakayuumin (curcumin) naam ka tatav hota hai jo ki vibhinan tarah ke kaimsar ko theek karane mem sakasham hai। haladee ke sevan se kaimsar sel baढ़ne kee smbhaavana kam hotee hai tatha kaimsar theek hota hai। 5. tamaatar (Tomato)- tamaatar khaane se bhee mahilaaem satan kaimsar se bachee rah sakatee haim। tamaatar mem laayakopeen (lycopene) hota hai jo ki ek shakatishaalee emteeऑkaseedemt hai aur kaimsar ko baढ़ne se rokata hai। 6. paalak (Spinach)- paalak mem emteeऑkaseedemt layuutin (lutin) hota hai jo kaimsar se bachaane mem sahaayak hai। haphate mem do se teen baar paalak khaama chaahie jisase satan kaimsar se bacha ja sakata hai। 7. barokalee (Broccoli)- barokalee mem kaimsar se laड़ne vaale tatava, emdola-3-kaarabinol (indole-3-carbinol) hota hai jo ki satan kaimsar ke selas kee garoth ko kam kar dete haim। barokalee ke niyamit sevan se kaimsar se bacha ja sakata hai। barokalee ke saath patata gobhee aur gobhee ko milaakar khaama chaahie। 8. akharot (Wallnut)- akharot mem bahot se poshak tatav hote haim jo satan kaimsar kee garoth ko kam kar dete haim esalie akharot ka rojaana sevan karana chaahie। 9. baluuberee (Blueberries)- baluuberee vitaamin aur mimaral se bharapuur hotee haim। enamem emteeऑkaseedemt elejik bhee hote haim jo satam kaimsar se bachaav karate haim। baluubairee ke saath sataraॉberee aur balaikaberee bhee behad phaayademmd hotee hai। Disease: siradarad (Headache) Description: siradarad ek am samasaya hai। sir ke kisee bhee hisase mem darad ho sakata hai aur yah darad keval lakashaण hota hai jo ki sir kee kisee beemaaree ko darashaata hai। kae baar bahot jayaada tanaav lene, thakaavat home, bhuukhe rahane, garamee tej hone ya kisee am shaareerik samasaya jaise ki bokhaar ya jokaam ke kaaraण bhee sir darad ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - uchach rakat chaap hona - kabaj ya dasat hona - jayaada sharaab peena - tanaavagarasat hona - pet theek n hona Reasons: sir darad ke kaaraण- (Cause of Headache) sir ka darada, dimaag mem rakat koshikaaom (blood vessels) aur shiraaom (nerves) ke apas mem takaraane se hota hai। darad ke samay rakat koshika kee ek nishachit sira aur sir kee mmsapeshiym sakariy hotee haim aur dimaag ko darad ka siganal bhejatee haim। jisase sir darad mahasuus hota hai। sir darad ke anay kaaraण (Other Reasons of headache) 1. jab vayakati kisee cheej ko lekar khod par dabaav mahasuus karata hai ya kisee sathiti ya parisathiti ko lekar asammjas mem hota hai। ise mem usaka man ashmt ho jaata hai aur dimaag par jayaada gahara parabhaav paड़ta hai jisake kaaraण tanaav hota hai aur sir darad hone lagata hai। 2. dimaag kee rakat vaahiniyom mem badalaav hone se home vaale darad ko maaegaren ka darad kaha jaata hai। es tarah ke sir darad mem sir ke kisee ek hisase mem chobhan bhara darad hota hai aur darad ke saath jee michalaane, gais aur ulatee jaisee samasayaaem bhee hotee haim। etana hee naheem vayakati photophobiya (roshanee se pareshaanee) aur phonophobiya (shor se pareshaanee) se bhee pareshaanee mahasuus karata hai। parayaapat neemd n lene, bhuukhe rahane ya kam paanee peene se maaegaren ho sakata hai। 3. kochh mahilaaem haaramon mem badalaav ke dauraan gmbheer sir darad mahasuus karatee haim। yah sathiti monopoja, maasik sataraava, ovelayuushan adi ke dauraan bhee ho sakatee hai। maasik sataraav mem utaara chaढ़aav se bhee es tarah ka sir darad bana rah sakata hai। 4. kochh khaas tarah kee davaaeyom ka jayaada dim tak lene ke kaaraण ribaaumd siradarad kee samasaya ho ho sakatee hai। kae beemaariym isee hotee haim jinamem davaaeym lmbe samay tak chalatee haim, ise mem yah masatishak ko parabhaavit kar sakatee haim। es tarah ka sir darad davaaem bmd hone ke saath khod hee bmd ho jaata hai। 5. dmt darad se bhee sir kee nasem parabhaavit hotee haim। dmt aur sir kee nasem jabaड़e par jaakar milatee haim jisase dmt aur sir ek duusarem ko kanekat karate haim। jisase dmt mem kisee bhee tarah kee takaleeph hone se sir mem darad hone lagata hai। 6. chaay aur kaॉphee ke adi logom ko yadi samay par chaay n mile to bhee unahem sir darad kee shikaayat ho sakatee hai। 7. kochh logom ko sobah uthate hee siradarad kee shikaayat hotee hai jabaki kochh der baad yah apane ap theek ho jaata hai। kae baar raat mem achachhee neemd n lene ya bhuukhe pet some ke kaaraण sobah sobah sir darad ho sakata hai। 8. mkhom mem kisee tarah kee samasaya hone, mkh kamajor hone, chashama n pahanane ya kmtekat laims mem gaड़baड़ee hone se sir darad ho sakata hai। isee koe bhee samasaya jisase mkhom par tamaav paड़ta ho, sir darad hone kee vajah ho sakata hai। ise mem yadi koe vayakati sir darad se pareshaan hai to use apanee mkhom ko bhee jaruur chaik karaana chaahie। 9. kochh logom ko aesakareem ya bahot thmdee cheejom ko khaane se bhee sir darad kee shikaayat ho sakatee hai। aesakareem ya bahot thmdee cheejem khaane ke baad maathe ke beech mem bhaareepan mahasuus hota hai jisase sir darad shoruu ho jaata hai। es tarah ka darad aesakareem khaane ke tormt baar shoruu ho jaata hai। Treatments: sir darad se raahat ke lie tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Headache) Home Remedies: ajakal kee tej bhaagatee jimdagee aur vayasat jeevanashailee mem tanaav aur saradarad ek am beemaaree ho gae hai। saradarad ke kae kaaraण hote haim। sir mem rakat pahomchaane vaalee naada़iyom mem smkochana, samaayo tmtar kee asamaanay gatividhi, jayaada dhuumarapaan karamaa, jayaada alakohal lemaa, shareer mem paanee kee kamee, jayaada der tak bevajah sonaa, darad nivaarak davaaom ka jayaada sevan karanaa, saradee-jokaama, bokhaar samet ise kae vajah haim, jisase saradarad hotee hai। yahm yah jaanana jaroree hai ki saamaanay saradarad aur maaegaren ke saradarad mem mtar hai। maaegaren mem saradarad kaaphee pareshaanee vaala hota hai aur yah ek gmbheer beemaaree bhee hai। saradarad ya kisee bhee tarah ke saradarad mem jaladee elopaithik darad nivaarak dava khaana sehat ke lie nokasaanadeh hota hai, kayomki jayaada pen kilar khaane se kidamee aur livar daimej hote haim। elopaithik davaaom se behatar hai ki ham ise kochh ghareluu upachaar ko ajamaaem, jisase saradarad mem n siraph araam milata hai balaki yah jada़ se khatam bhee hota hai, bina koe saaed ephekata। saradarad ke ghareluu nosakha़e (Home Remedies for Headache) sarasom tel (Mustard Oil) saradarad mem sarasom tel kaaphee asaradaar hota hai। maathe ke jis hisase mem darad ho raha ho us taraph vaale maak mem sarasom ke tel kee kochh buumdem daal deejie aur usake baad jor se smsom ko opar kee taraph kheemchie। esase saradarad se kaaphee raahat milegee। dhayaan rahe saradarad hone par bisatar par letakar darad vaale hisase ko bed ke neeche lataka kar naak mem tel lena chaahie। daalacheenee (Cimamon) daalacheenee ko paanee ke saath maheen peesakar maathe par patala lep lagaane se saradarad mem kaaphee raahat milatee hai। lep suukh jaane par use hata leejie। teena-chaar baar lep lagaane par saradarad hona bmd ho jaata hai। poshakar muul (Pushkar Mool) poshakar muul ek kodaratee jada़ee buutee hai। ese chmdan kee tarah ghisakar lep bana lem aur sir par lagaaem। esake lep ko maathe par lagaane se saradarad mem kaaphee raahat milata hai। molethee (Mulethi) molethee saradarad mem kaaphee kaam karata hai। molethee ko peesakar chuuraण bana leejie। es chuuraण ko naak ke paas le jaakar suumghem। esase saradarad chhuu-mmtar ho jaaegee। saumpha-peepala-molethee (Saunf, Peepal and Mulethi) peepal ke patate, somtha, molaithee aur saumph sabako peesakar chuuraण bana leejie। usake baad es chuuraण mem ek chamamoch paanee milaakar gaadha lep bama bana leejie। es lep ko maathe par lagaaee। saradarad khatam ho jaaegaa। masaaledaar chaay (Spicy Tea) masaaledaar chaay saradarad ke lie ek raamabaaण kee tarah kaam karata hai। ese ghar mem bhee asaanee se banaaya ja sakata hai। yah ek uta‍tejak pey padaarath hai jo dimaag ko sachet karata hai। chaay mem thoda़ee adarakha, laumg aur elaaechee mila kar ubaal dem। ho gaya garamaagaram masaaledaar chaay taiyaara। masaaledaar chaay ko garamaagaram hee peena chaahie। esase apaka saradarad to gaayab hoga hee saath mem ap tarotaaja़a bhee mahasuus karemge। tel maalish (Oil massage) saradarad mem tel kee maalish bahot asaradaar hotee hai। maalish se sir kee rakat dhamaniyom mem rakat paravaah sahee se hone lagata hai aur saradarad tormt chhuu-mmtar ho jaatee hai। dhayaan rahe sir kee maalish harabal tel se hee karem aur saradarad hone par tel ko halaka garam kar lema chaahie taaki yah jaladee asar kare। neembuu paanee (Lemom Water) kaaphee maatara mem sharaab peene se akasar logom ko haimgaovar ho jaata hai। haimgaovar mem kaaphee tej saradarad hota hai। isee sathiti mem neembuu paanee kaaphee kaam karata hai। sharaab jayaada peene se shareer mem paanee kee kamee ho jaatee hai aur neembuu paanee peeme se shareer mem paanee kee kamee bhee duur hotee hai aur saradarad bhee theek hota hai। Disease: baromkaaetis (Bronchitis) Description: jab shavaasanalee tatha esakee shaakhaaom mem smkaramaण ya elarajee ke kaaraण suujam ane ke kaaraण shavaas smbmdhee samasaya hotee hai to us sathiti ko baromkaaetis (Bronchitis) kahate haim। yah saradiyom kee ek am samasaya hai। Symptoms: - khmsee ke saath bahot gaadha़a v hare rmg ka balagam ana - naak bahana ya bmd hona - badan darad hona - baara-baar chhaatee mem jalan - bokhaar ya thmd lagana - lagaataar kaaphee der hona - sms phuulana - sms lete samay chhaatee mem gharagharaahat kee avaaj hona Reasons: - seene mem sathit shavms nalee aur usakee shaakhaaom mem baara-baar home vaala emphekashana। - nayuumomiya bhee baromkaaetis ka mokhay kaaraण hotee hai। - tee.bee. ka emphekashan bhee esaka ek paramokh kaaraण hota hai। agar shoroat mem hee tee.bee. emphekashan ka samochit elaaj ho jaae to baromkaaetis se bacha ja sakata hai। - kochh logom mem yah rog janamajaat hota hai। - esake alaava imteetaripasin naamak emjaaem kee kamee, rayuumetaaed ऑratharaaetis aur anay atoemayuun beemaariym bhee baromkaaetis ka kaaraण banatee haim। - baikateeriya ya vishaaणo ka smkaramaण bhee baromkaaetis ka kaaraण ho sakata haim। - dhuumarapaan aur vaayo paraduushaण ke kaaraण bhee yah beemaaree ho sakatee hai। - vaayo mem kisee cheej se elarajee jaise paraag kaण etayaadi bhee baromkaaetis ka kaaraण ho sakate haim। Treatmemts: baromkaaetis se bachaav ke lie shareer ko thmdee se bachaana chaahie। saath hee niman baatom ka bhee khayaal rakhana chaahie: - dhuumarapaan chhoda़ dem। - vaayo paraduushaण, v dhuul se bachem। - saradee aur phaluu se karem bachaava। - balagam patala rakhane ke lie khuub paanee piem। - sote samay sir bisatar se omcha rakhame ke lie takie ka parayog karem। - yadi bokhaar badha़ jaae aur thmd lagane lage to tormt kisee chikitasak se smparak karem। Home Remedies: baromkaaetis naak aur phephada़e ke beech sms lene vaalee nalee mem suujan ke vajah se hotee hai। yah paraay vaaeral emphekashan se hota hai। gale mem khichakhicha, kmto jaisee chobhan aur darad hona esake lakashaण haim। mausam mem badalaav aur elarajee se bhee baromkaaetis kee shikaayat hotee hai। esamem kabhee-kabhee bokhaar kee bhee shikaayat hotee hai। baromkaaetis mem kharaash ya darad hone se khaana khaane, paanee peene ya thuuk nigalane tak mem takaleeph hotee hai। esase nijaat paane ke lie daॉkatar kee madad lene se behatar hai ki kochh ghareluu elaaj kie jaane chaahie jo kaaphee asaradaar bhee hota hai। baromkaaetis mem kharaash ke ghareluu elaaja(Home remedies for Bronchitis) shahad (Honey) shahad mem emtee vaayaral aur emtee baikateeriyal goण hota hai। gale mem kharaash hone par shahad ya shahad vaalee chaay peene se suujan kam hotee hai aur gale ko kaaphee araam milatee hai। gale mem kharaash mem yah kaaphee phaayademmd hota hai। adarak (Ginger) saradee, kaph aur gale kee kharaash mem adarak gale ko kaaphee araam pahomchaata hai। adarak mem emtee emphalaametaree goण hota hai। adarak ka rasa, adarak kee chaay peene ya adarak chuusane se gale kee suujana, kharaash mem kaaphee araam milata hai। harabal chaay (Herbal Tea) kaalee miracha, tolasee v laumg se banee chaay peene se gale mem kharaash se nijaat milatee hai। en kodaratee jada़ee-buutiyom se banee garam chaay kee chosakiyom se gale ko kaaphee raahat milatee hai। vaise harabal chaay kae beemaariyom mem bhee kaam ata hai। haladee (Turmeric) thoda़ee see haladee daalakar duudh mem ubaal lem। duudh tab tak ubaalem jab tak haladee pak na jaaem. phir ese kap mem lekar chaay kee chosakiym lete hoe piem। esase gale ke darad mem aur kharaash mem kaaphee raahat milegee। garaara (Gargil) gale mem kharaash kee shikaayat hone par garam paanee mem namak daalakar garaare karem। namak mila garam paanee apake gale mem emphekashan kee vajah se ae suujam ko kam karata hai aur araam pahomchaata hai। behatar hoga ki jaladee raahat ke lie ap har teen ghmte mem garaare karem। taral padaarath (Liquid) ap thoda़ee-thoda़ee der mem kochh garam taral padaarath lete rahem। kochh bhee naheem to ap thoda़ee-thoda़ee der mem garam paanee peete rahem। esase apake gale kee sikaae hogee aur apako araam milegaa। lahason (Garlic) lahason mem emtee-baayotik aur emtee vaayaral goण hote haim। gale kee suujan aur kharaash mem yah kaaphee asaradaar hota hai। lahason ke do-teem tokada़e ko paanee ke saath chaba kar sobah khaaem ya phir duudh mem ubaal kar bhee pee sakate haim। yuukilipatas tel (Eucalyptus Oil) gale kee kharaash mem bhaap lena kaaphee phaayademmd hota hai। garam paanee mem agar yuukilipatas ke tel ko mila kar bhaap lem to yah kaaphee asaradaar hota hai। gale kee suujan aur kharaash ko kam karata hai। Disease: ebola vishaaणo rog (EVD) (Ebola) Description: ebola vaayaras rog ya ebola hemoraahaijik bokhaar ebola vishaaणo ke kaaraण hota hai। ebola vishaaणo rog (EVD) ya ebola hemoraahaijik bokhaar (EHF) mem shareer mem nasom se khuun baahar ana shoruu ho jaata hai, jisase shareer ke mdar rakatasaraav shoruu ho jaata hai aur esase 90% rogiyom kee maृtayo ho jaatee hai। Symptoms: - armbhik lakashaण mem javara, phonasee, sar darada, michalee, ulatee aur pet mem darada, puure shareer mem gathiya ka darada, gale mem darada, dasat sakata hai - es rog ka emkayuubeshan pireeyad (Imcubation Period) ek haphate ka hota hai। usake baad rogee mem armbhik lakashaण najar ate haim - jananmg mem suujan hotee hai - tavacha mem darad ka anobhav hota hai - netarashaleshamalaashoth (kmjemgavaaetisa) hai - puure shareer par phomshiyom najar ane lagatee haim - monh ka taalo laal ho jaata hai - monha, kaana, naak se rakatasaraav hota hai - rog ke vikasit avasatha mem yah lakashaण bhee najar ate hai Reasons: ebola se bachaav ka sabase behatar aur ekamaatar upaay hai esase parabhaavit rogee ke samaparak mem ane se bachamaa। kisee rogee ke smparak mem ane se yah rog aur tejee se phailata hai। Treatments: ​ebola ka abhee tak koe thos elaaj naheem mila hai। bachaav hee es beemaaree ka sabase behatareen upaay maana jaata hai। abhee tak ebola se peeditom ke kes mem niman kadam uthaae jaate haim: - es beemaaree ke lie koe vishishat upachaar maheem hai; smkaramit logom kee sahaayata kee koshishom mem unahem oral rihaaedareshan therepee (peene ke lie thoda़aa-sa meetha aur namakeen paanee denaa) ya emtaraavenas phalodas dena shaamil hai। - akasar es vaayaras ke smkaramit hone vaale 50% se 90% tak log maut ke shikaar ho jaate haim। - esake lie teeka vikasit karane ke parayaas jaaree haim; haalmki abhee tak isa koe teeka maujuud naheem hai। Disease: luu lagana (Heat Stroke) Description: garamee mem sabase baड़ee samasaya hotee hai luu laganaa। mgarejee bhaasha mem ese heet satarok (Heat Stroke) aur sanasatarok (Sum Stroke) bhee kahate haim। garamee mem uchach taapamaan mem jayaada der tak rahane se ya garam hava ke jhomkom se smparak mem ane par luu (Loo) lagane ka dar adhik hota hai। Symptoms: - nkhem bhee jalatee haim - esase achaanak behoshee v mtath rogee kee maut bhee ho sakatee hai - bokhaar kaaphee badha़ jaata hai - baladapareshar bhee lo ho jaata hai aur livar - kidanee mem sodiyam potaishiyam ka smtolam bigada़ jaata hai। ise mem behoshee bhee  sakatee hai। esake alaava lo beepee , baren ya haarat satarok kee sathiti bhee ban sakatee hai - luu lagane par shareer mem garamee , khoshakee , siradarad , kamajoree , shareer tuutana , baar - baar momh suukha.na , ulatee , chakakar , tej bokhaar sms lene mem takaleeph , dasat aur kae baar nidhaal ya behoshee jaise lakashaण majar ate haim। pahomch sakatee hai। vaise to luu ka shikaar akasar pachaas se opar kee umar ke log hote haim lekin kae savasath khilaada़ee bhee esaka shikaar asaanee se ho jaate haim। kam umar ke logom mem semtaral sakata hai। kae sathitiyom mem mareeja़ kee maृtayo bhee ho sakatee hai। garamee mem vibhinan davaaeyom ka sevan karane vaale vayakatiyom ko bhee luu lagane ka dar hota hai। isee davaaem jo rakat karem। garamee ke kaaraण shareer ka taapamaan baढ़ jaata hai। chhaaya mem laane se shareer ka taapamaan saamaanay ana shoro ho jaata hai। - usako namak shakakar aur paanee ka ghol momh se pilaayem, usake kapaड़e nikaalakar siraph mdaruunee vasatar rakhem। shareer par halaka sa garam paamee chhiड़kem। - geelee chaadar mem lapetakar taapamaan kam karane ka parayaas karem। - haath pair kee maalish karem jisase rakat smcharaण parabhaavit hota hai। - smbhav ho to baraph ke tokaड़e kapaड़e mem lapetakar garadana, bagalom aur jmghom par rakhe। esase garamee jaladee nikalatee hai। - dhuup mem ghar se baahar nikalem to chhataree ka esatemaal karem। nmge badan aur nmge pair dhuup mem na khada़e hom। - neembuu paanee, am panaa, chhaachha, lasasee, naariyal paanee, bel ya neembuu ka sharabata, khas ka na jaaem। - din mem do baar nahaaem। - haree sabajiyom ka sevan adhik karem। - kheeraa, kakada़ee, laukee, tauree jaruur khaaem। - thmde vaataanokuulit kamare mem rahem। - emalee ke guude ko haath honaa, tavacha laal ho jaanaa, chakakar anaa, ulatee, kaaphee paseena ama jaise lakashaण jab dikhane lage to samajh jaaee ki yah heet satarok ya luu ka ataik hai। heet satarok ya luu lagane ke baad Description: adhikatar mahilaaem chhote ya bada़e satanom kee samasaya ko lekar pareshaam rahatee haim। sodaृढ़ aur poshat satan (Breast) sataree kee sonadarata mem chaar chnd lagaate haim। Reasons: mem kodaratee chamak bhee atee hai। baal ka jhada़na rokane ke lie ghareluu nosakha़e (Home Remedies for Hair fall) memhadee aur mvala (Rosemary and Amla) memhadee aur mvala kee baraabar maatara lekar Symptoms: - agar apako teem haphate se adhik se khmsee hai - kabaj aur ख़raab pet : kochh adhayayamom se yah pata chalata hai ki kabaj aur ख़raab pet hone kee vajah se bhee rosee hotee hai - daimdaraph se sir mem khojalee rahatee hai aur baal girane lagate haim। yah jayaadaatar saradiyom mem hotee hai - baalom ka girana : amataur par hamaare roज़ 20 se 50 baal girate haim। sar mem rosee hone se bhee baal jhaड़te haim, agar esase jayaada baal jhaड़te hai to rosee bhee kaaraण ho sakatee hai - sar kee suukhee tavacha : sar kee suukhee tavacha rosee hone ka ek paramokh kaaraण hai - sar mem khojalee: jab rosee hona shoruu hotee hai to sabase pahale sar mem khojalee hona shoruu ho jaatee hai Reasons: baalom mem rosee hone kee mokhay vajah (Top Reason For Dandruff In Hindi) baalom kee sahee dekhabhaal na karanaa, sahee daaet na lena ya anay kae vajahem hotee haim jinakee vajah se sar mem rosee (Rusi) ho sakatee hai। en paramokh vajahom mem se kochh miman haim: 1. mausam mem badalaava- atayadhik garam ya atayadhik thmda mausam donom hee sir kee tavacha ko nokasaan pahomchaate haim। jis tarah mausam ka utaar chaढ़aav hamaare shareer ko parabhaavit karata hai usee parakaar sir kee tavacha ko bhee, jisaka nateeja daimdaraph ho sakata hai। 2. haaejeena- baalom kee theek se saphaae n karane ya sir se smbmdhit upakaraणom ko saaph n rakhane jaise kmghee, tauliyaa, heyar barash adi esake saath hee kisee aur ke davaara esatemaal kie gae kmghee ya tauliya ko esatemaal karane se bhee ruusee hone kee samasaya ho sakatee hai। 3. sahee daaeta- shareer mem poshak tatavom ka sahee smtolan n home se bhee sakailap se ruusee noma papaड़ee utarane lagatee hai। daaet mem daala, duudha, taaज़a phal aur haree sabajiyom (Diet for Dandruff) ka esatemaal jaruuree hai। esake alaava baalom mem sahee maatara mem tel n lagaane se bhee daimdaraph shoruu ho jaata hai। 4. ऑyal galaimd ka bmd honaa- kae baar kisee beemaaree ya haaramonal asmtolan ke kaaraण ऑyal galaimd bmd ho jaate haim jisase ruusee hone lagatee hai। 5. smkaramaण- baalom kee sataaelimg ke lie kemikal ka parayoga, heyar kalar ka esatemaala, baalom ko nechoral ruup se n suukhane denaa, geele baalom ko hee bmdh lena hota hai jo ki sakailap par ruusee ko janam deta hai। heyar kalar ka esatemaal ekasaparat se raay lekar hee karana chaahie aur achachhe kisam ke heyar kalar ka esatemaal karana chaahie। 7. paseena aur dhuula- garamiyom ke dinom mem sir kee tavacha par jama paseena jab dhuul ke smparak mem ata hai to sakailap par gmdagee jama hona shoruu ho jaatee hai। jo ki dheere dheere daimdaraph ka kaaraण ban jaatee hai। 8. elarajee- kae baar ham jo tela, shaimpuu, heyar sataaelimg paraॉdakat ya heyar kalar esatemaal kar rahe hote haim vah hamem suut naheem karataa, nateeja elarajee ho jaatee hai jo daimdaraph home ka baड़a kaaraण hai। Treatments: paraathamik satar par rosee kee dekhabhaal (First Level Treatment in Himdi) - apane sar kee satah ko rokha hone se bachaane ke lie sar aur baalom mem jarorat naheem hai। heyar taraasapalmt ya phir sarajaree mem laakhom ropaye kharach karane se behatar hai ki agar ap kochh ghareluu aur kodaratee nosakhom (Herbal and Home Remedies for Baldness) ko Oil) armdee ka tel gmjaapan ko duur karane ka sabase kaaragar dava hai। yah ek adararak yaami maॉsacharaaejimg ejemt kee tarah kaam karata hai। yah baal aur tavacha kee kae aur samasayaaom mem kaam baalom kee jada़om par phaila kar laga lem। kaaphee asar hogaa। 6. memthee ke beej (Methee) memthee ke beej bhee gmjepan ko duur karane mem kaaphee kaaragar hote haim। memthee ke beej ko kuut kar pesat bana lem aur sir mem jahm baal naheem hai vahm laga lem। ek ghmta tak pesat laga ho chhoda़ dem। baad mem sir ko paanee se dho lem। kaaphee asar hogaa। 7. meembuu (Lemon) neembuu bahot saare baalom kee pareshaamee mem kaam ata hai। masalana, baalom ke jhada़me-girane mem, rosee ko khatam karane mem, daraae heyar mem। gmjepan se lada़ne ke lie neembuu ke ras ko kae tarah ke telom mem mila kar lagaaem aur sir kee maalish karem to kaaphee asar dikhegaa। 8. chokmdar ke patate (Beetroot Leaves) chokmdar ke patate gmjepan ko duur karane kee achuuk dava hai। chokmdar ke patate ko paanee mem ubaal lem। jab vah kaaphee molaayam ho jaae to usamem memhadee ke patate mila dem aur phir ese garaaemdar masheen mem pees kar pesat bana lem। es pesat ko sir par laga kar kochh der ke lie chhoda़ dem। baad mem gonagone paanee se sir dho lem। kaaphee asar dikhegaa। 9. payaaj (Omion) payaaj mem maujuud salaphar sir mem rakat ke paravaah ko tej karata hai। jisase gmjapan kee beemaaree theek ho sakatee hai। kochh nahee bas payaaj ko kaat kar usaka juus nikaal lem aur usamem kochh shahad mila lem। aur phir ese baalom kee jada़om par laga lem। yah baalom kee jada़ mem rakat smchaar ko to badha़aaega hee saath hee phmgas aur baikateeriya ko bhee maaregaa। 10. dahee (Curd) baalom ke lie dahee kmdeeshanar ka kaam karata hai। yah baalom ke gmjepan ko duur karame mem kaaphee kaam karata hai। baalom ko jhada़ne-girane se bhee rokata hai। baalom mem dahee ka maasak lagaaem kaaphee behatar nateeje aemge। Disease: deehaaedareshan (Dehydration) Description: deehaaedareshan yaani nirajaleekaraण। mamoshay shareer mem paanee ke kam ho jaane kee avasatha ko deehaaedareshan (Dehydration) kahate haim। vaijaञaanik bhaasha mem deehaaedareshan ko haaepohaaedaraishan (Hypohydration) kahate haim। shareer mem paanee kee kamee (Pani ki Kami) ke kaaraण shareer se khanij padaarath jaise ki namak aur shakakar kam ho jaate haim। deehaaedareshan ke dauraana, shareer kee koshikaaom se paanee suukhata rahata hai jisake kaaraण shareer ke kaaray karane ka smtolan asaamaanay ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - ghabaraahat ya kmpakmpee - kabaj - chakakar ana - momh ka baar baar suukh jaana - suukhee tavacha - payaas na bojhana - sir mem darad - sosatee - mmsapeshiyom mem imthan - kamaja़oree Reasoms: - shareer mem paanee kee gmbheer samasaya kae baar jaanaleva bhee ho sakatee hai। - shareer se pmch paratishat darav khatam hone par kamaja़oree, payaasa, ubakaae, chida़chida़aapan hota hai। - shareer se das paratishat darav khatam hone par sir darada, chakakar aur mgom mem sanasanaahat paida ho sakatee hai। shareer kee tavacha neelee pada़ne lagatee hai aur shareer kamaja़or ho jaata hai। - shareer se pmdarah paratishat darav khatam hone par dekhane aur sonane kee shakati par asar pada़ta hai। jeebh mem suujan ho jaatee hai aur khaana nigalane mem dikakat hotee hai। - shareer se pmdarah paratishat se jayaada darav khatam home par emsaan kee maृtayo bhee ho sakatee hai। - dasat ke kaaraण shareer mem hoe deehaaedareshan se mamoshay kee maृtayo ke asaar jayaada hote haim। gmbheer deehaaedaresham (Pani ki Kami) kee vajah se manoshay ka baren daimej yaani usake masatishak ko haami bhee pahomch sakatee hai। saath hee haaepovolemik shaॉk ka khatara bhee rahata hai jisamem shareer ke kae mgom ko haani pahomch sakatee hai। - yadi apako chakakar  rahe haim, ya ap kisee bhee kaaray ko karane mem khod ko asamarath pa rahe haim to ise samay mem daॉkatar ko dikhaama behad avashayak hota hai। do din se jayaada kabaj ya bokhaar rahane par tormt daॉkatar se samaparak karem। Treatments: deehaaedaresham ke upaay (Treatment for Dehydration) - jitana ho sake jayaada se jayaada paanee piem। - navajaat bachachom mem deehaaedareshan ke upachaar (pani ki kami k ilaj) ke lie bachache ko mm ka duudh v paanee pilaate rahem। paanee mem oaraes ka ghol milaakar pilaaem। - jayaada bhaagadauda़ vaala kaam na karem aur jitana ho sake araam karem। - dhuup mem ghar se baahar na nikalem aur thmdee jagah par baithe rahem। - duudha, kaॉphee, pharuut juus jaise padaarathom ka sevan karane se bachem। - elekatarolaaetas se yokat saporatas darimkas ka sevan avashay karem। Home Remedies: apake shareer kee har koshika theek dhmg se kaam kare esake lie ऑkaseejan (Oxygen) ke saath saath paanee kee bhee avashayakata hotee hai। jab shareer mem paanee kee kamee hotee hai to yah sathiti dihaaedareshan ya nirajaleekaraण kahalaatee hai। momh suukha lage, homthom par papaड़ee jam jaae, thakaan ho, taॉyalet kam jaana ho, chakakar aem to enahem dihaaedareshan ke paraarmbhik lakashaण samajhakara, pey padaarath adhik maatara mem lena shoruu kar dena chaahie। dihaaedareshan kee samasaya ko gmbheerata se n lene par esake ghaatak pariणaam ho sakate haim। aee apako bataate haim ki dihaaedareshan kee samasaya ko ghareluu nosakhom se kis tarah theek kiya ja sakata hai। dihaaedareshan ke lie ghareluu nosakha़e (Home Remedies for Dehydration) paanee peene kee maatara baढ़aaem (Increase Water Intake) dihaaedareshan se nipatane ka sabase pahala kadam hai ki paanee kee maatara badhaaem। puure dim mem takareebam das gilaas paanee peena bahot jaruuree hai। yadi apako payaas m bhee lag rahee ho tab bhee paamee jaruur piem। saada paanee peena achachha n lag raha ho to paanee mem neembuu ya elekataraॉl adi daalakar bhee paanee piya ja sakata hai। dahee (Yogurt or Curd) ulatee, dasat adi ke kaaraण hoe dihaaedareshan ke lie dahee ek achachha upachaar hai। yah elekatarolaaetas (Electrolytes) ka bhee achachha satarot hotee hai, esalie pet ke lie phaayademmd hotee hai aur asaamee se pach bhee jaatee hai। upachaar ke lie dahee ko saada ya dahee mem kaala namak aur bhona jeera daalakar bhee khaaya ja sakata hai। raseele phal aur sabajiym (Watery Fruit and Vagetable) yadi dihaaedareshan kee shoruuat hai to raseele phal aur sabajiyom ke sevan se bhee araam smbhav hai। em phal aur sabajiyom mem tarabuuja, kharabuuja, mguura, smtaraa, sataraॉberee, kheeraa, kakaड़ee, papeeta muulee, paalaka, toree aur tamaatar adi haim। kela (Banana) shareer mem dihaaedareshan kee shikaayat potaishiyam jaise khanij kee kamee ke kaaraण hotee hai। kele mem potaishiyam bharapuur hota hai, ise mem yah shareer kee dihaaedareshan kee samasaya se nipatane ka asaan upaay hai। upachaar ke lie din mem do kele khaae ja sakate haim ya kele kee samuuthee banaakar bhee pee ja sakatee hai। naariyal paamee (Coconut Water) naariyal paanee ka ek gilaas dihaaedareshan se nipatane mem kaaphee kaaragar hai। naariyal paanee mem uchach elekatarolaaetas hote haim jo ki naariyal paanee ko haaedaretimg pey banaate haim। esamem cheenee kee apekasha kailoree bhee bahot kam hotee hai। chhaachh (Butter Milk) yadi ap dinabhar dhuup mem kaam karate haim ya apako kinaheem kaaraणom se adhik paseena ata hai to bhee apako dihaaedareshan kee samasaya ho sakatee hai। es tarah kee samasaya se nipatane ke lie chhaachh ek parabhaavee nosakha hai। upachaar ke lie din mem ek se do gilaas chhaachh piem। suup (Soup) dihaaedaresham se nipatame mem sabajiyom ke suup bhee parabhaavee asar dikhaate haim। esake lie suup mem ajavaayana, muulee aur toree jaisee sabajiym daalakar suup taiyaar karem। din bhar mem kam se kam ek baar suup jaruur piem। neembuu paanee (Lemon water) neembuu paanee n siraph shareer ko haaederat rakhata hai balaki shareer ke taॉkasin bhee baahar nikaalata hai। meembuu paanee peene se taajagee ka ehasaas hota hai। neembuu paanee banaane ke lie cheenee kee jagah shahad ka esatemaal karem aur ek chotakee kaalee mirach bhee daalem। jau ka paanee (Barley Water) jau ka paanee bhee shareer ko haaedaret rakhane ka achachha upaay hai। jau ke paanee se dihaaedareshan ke dauraan shareer mem hoe poshak tatavom kee kamee kee bharapaae hotee hai। yee asaanee se pach jaata hai aur shareer ko thmda rakhata hai। upachaar ke lie 4 kap paanee mem ek kap jau bhiga dem। usake baad es paanee ko lagabhag 45 minat dhakakar ubaalem। jab achachhee tarah ubal jaae to es paanee ko chhaanakar gonagona rahane tak thmda karem aur esamem shahad milaakar piem। savaad baढ़aane ke lie neembuu ka ras bhee milaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: ghamauriym (Prickly Heat) Description: ghamauriyom ko mgarejee mem parikalee heet (Prickly Heat) kahate haim। garamiyom ke mausam mem ghamauriym hona am baat hai। garamee ke mausam mem shareer se paseema adhik maatara mem bahata hai। yadi samay rahate es paseene ko saapha़ na kiya jaae to yah shareer kee tavacha mem hee suukh jaata hai jisake kaaraण paseene kee garmthiym bmd ho jaatee haim aur shareer mem ghamauree home lagatee haim। Symptoms: - shareer mem khojalee hona - shareer mem jalan ya kmte see chobhan mahasuus hona - shareer par laala-golaabee, chhote daanom ka ubharana - adhik paseena ana - kapada़om se chobhan hona - thakaavat mahasuus hona Reasons: ghamauree ke dauraam shareer mem khojalee, halakee suujan aur chobhan mahasuus hone lagatee hai। ghamauree ke daane dhuup ke seedhe smparak mem ane se badha़ jaate haim। amataur par ghamauree kochh dinom mem apane ap sahee ho jaatee hai lekin kochh logom mem yah haphatom aur maheenom tak ke lie ho sakatee hai। esalie ek haphate tak ghamauree ke theek ma hone par daॉkatar se jaruur paraamarash lena chaahie। ghamauree (Prickly Heat) ke kaaraण logom mem thakaavat (Heat Exhaustion) aur dhuup mem chida़chida़aahat kee shikaayat bhee hotee hai। ghamauree ke kaaraण luu lagama ka khatara bhee paida ho sakata hai। ghamauriym bhee kae parakaar kee hotee haim jaise milieriya karisatalaaen (Miliari Crystallina), milieriya ruubara (Miliari Rubra) aur milieriya paraॉphmda (Miliari Profunda)। milieriya paraॉphomda mem sabase adhik khatara rahata hai aur ese vaaeladaphaayar (Wildfire Rash) bhee kahate haim। Treatmemts: ghamauriyom se bachaav ka sabase behatar upaay hota hai garamee se bachakar rahanaa। esake alaava ghamauriyom (Ghamoriyan) se bachaav ke kochh aham upaay nimam haim: - simthetik phaibarik se bane vasatarom ko na pahanem। - suutee aur dheele dhaale kapada़e pahanem। - khuub paanee piem aur nahaaem। - baahar se ghar lautane ke kochh der baad sanaan karem। - shareer ke hisasom ko taaज़a hava lagane dem। - masaaledaar bhojan se bachem। saada bhojan hee khaaem। - baarish ke paanee se sanaan karane se shareer par nikalee phomsiym aur daanem duur hote haim। - rojaana sobah neem kee chaara-pmch patatiym chabaaem। - shareer par molataanee mitatee ka lep lagaaem। - neem kee patatiyom ko paanee mem ubaalakar es paanee se sanaan karem। - naariyal ke tel mem kapuur milaakar es tel se puure shareer kee maalish karem। - kailaamaaen loshan ka parayog karem। - geele shareer par paaodar na lagaaem। jaruurat se jayaada paaodar ka parayog karane se bhee bachem। Home Remedies: garamiyom mem ghamauriyom kee samasaya am hai। jayaada paseena ane ya garamee mem rahane par baड़om, bachachom, yahm tak ki navajaatom (Infants) mem bhee ghamauree kee samasaya ho jaatee hai। ghamauree hone par chhote-chhote chobhane vaale daamem peetha, garadan tatha shareer ke amay hisasom par nikal ate haim। kae baar baikateeriyal emphekashan (Bacterial Infection) aur shareer ka vajan jayaada hone se bhee ghamauree nikalane kee samasaya hotee rahatee hai। yuum to mausam mem badalaav hote hee ghamauree kee samasaya khod b khod theek ho jaatee hai lekin kae dapha samasaya etanee baढ़ jaatee hai ki mausam mem badalaav hone tak ka samay kaatana bhee moshakil hota hai। ise mem kochh ghareluu upachaarom se ghamauriyom se nijaat smbhav hai। ghamauriyom se raahat ke lie ghareluu nosakha़e (Home Remedies for Prickley Heat) otameel (Oatmeal) ghamauriyom se mijaat ke lie otameel bahot baढ़iya nosakha hai। otameel se ghamauriyom mem home vaalee jalan (inflammation), chobhan aur khojalee (itching) se raahat milatee hai। upachaar ke lie thmde paanee se bhare hoe tab mem ek kap otameel daalem। jab tak paanee duudhiya rmg ho tab tak emtajaar karem aur es paanee mem takareeban adha ghmta baithem। es upaay ko har roj do baar karem। thmda upachaar (Cold Compress) ghamauree parabhaavit sathaan par thmdee sikaae karane se bhee tormt araam milata hai। baraph ke kochh tokaड़om ko kapaड़e mem lapetakar parabhaavit sathaan par sikaae karem। lagaataar takareeban 10 minat tak isa karem। har chaar se chhah ghmte par isa karem। esase ghamauriym theek ho jaaemgee। chmdan ka paaudar (Samdalwood Powder) chmdan ke paaudar kee thmdak bhee ghamauriyom se nijaat dilaane mem parabhaavee hai। upachaar ke lie chmdan ke paaudar mem paanee milaakara, lep banaaem aur parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। esake alaava paaudar kee tarah chmdam paaudar ko ghamauriyom par chhiड़ka bhee ja sakata hai। bekimg paaudar (Baking Powder) bekimg paaudar bhee ghamauriyom se raahat deme ka achachha upaay hai। yah maृt tavacha ko hataakara, gmdagee ko saaph karata hai jo ki khojalee aur jalan ka kaaraण hote haim। upachaar ke lie ek kap thmde paanee mem ek chamamach bekimg soda milaakar usamem ek saaph kapaड़a bhigaakar nichoड़ lem। es kapaड़e ko parabhaavit sathaan par takareeban 10 minat tak rakhem। ek haphate tak har roj 5 se 6 baar isa karem। molataanee mitatee (Fuller’s Earth) molataanee mitatee bhee ghamauree se nijaat dilaane ka ek achachha ghareluu nosakha hai। molataamee mitatee ghamauree kee jalan se nijaat dilaatee hai aur khojalee bhee mitaatee hai। upachaar ke lie 5 chamamach molataamee mitatee mem golaab jal milaakar lep banaaem aur es lep ko parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। es upaay ko paratidin ek baar karem। elovera (Aloevera) elovera bhee ghamauree se nijaat ke lie behad achachha satarot hai। elovera ke jaate patatom ka guuda lekar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। takareeban 20 minat laga rahane dem aur usake baad dho dem। paratidin do baar isa karane se ghamauriym theek ho jaaemgee। besan (Gram Flour) besan shareer ka tel sokh leta hai jisase ghamauree ke daane jaladee suukh jaate haim। yah maृt tavacha ko bhee saaph karata hai aur jalan se raahat deta hai। upachaar ke lie besan kee kochh maatara mem paanee milaakar lep banaaem। es lep ko parabhaavit sathaan par 10 se 15 minat ke lie lagaakar chhoड़ dem। es upaay ko har roj ek baar karem। ek sapataah mem ghamoriym theek ho jaaemgee। kachache am (Raw Mango) kachacha am shareer kee garamee ko thmda karane mem behad parabhaavashaalee haim। ise mem kachache am ka pana (ek parakaar ka peya) banaakar peene se garamee mem raahat milatee hai। pana banaane ke lie kachache am ko ubaalakar usaka guuda alag karem aur thmde paanee mem mila lem। es paanee mem savaadaanosaar cheenee, kaala namak aur bhona jeera milaaem। ese har roj do baar peeem। kheera (Cucumber) kheere mem shareer ko thmda rakhame ka goण hote haim jo ki ghamauree se bhee bachaate haim। upachaar ke lie kheere ke patale-patale tokaड़e kaatakar neembuu mile hoe thmde paamee mem kochh der bhigaakar rakhem। esake baad en tokaड़om ko parabhaavit sathaan par kochh der rakhem। isa karane se bhee ghamauriym jaladee theek ho jaatee haim aur khojalee tatha jalan se bhee raahat milatee hai। Disease: sakaravee (Scurvy) Description: yah rog bhojam mem vitaamin see (Vitamin C) jise esakorabik esid (Ascorbic acid) bhee kaha jaata hai, kee kamee se hota hai। manoshayom mem kolaajen ke bamane aur ayaran ke avashoshaण ke lie vitaamim see kee avashayakata hotee hai jo ki hamem vibhinan phalom aur sabajiyom se milate haim, lekin vitaamin see kee kamee hone se shareer mem rakat kee bhee kamee ho jaatee hai। Symptoms: - masuuड़om mem khuun ana - suukhe aur do momhem baal - pairaalaayasis jaisa mahasuus karana - vajan ka n baढ़na - sakin disaऑradar Reasons: sakaravee ke kaaraण (Reasons of Scurvy) sakaravee ka pahala kaaraण bhojan mem parayaapat vitaamin see (Deficiency of Vitamim C) ka n hona ya shareer ko parayaapat vitaamin see m milana hai। esake alaava shareer par parayaapat dhayaam n dena ya samapuuraण bhojan n karane kee vajah se bhee yah rog ho sakata hai। vitaamin see kee kamee sabase pahale samodar ke jariye vayaapaar karane vaale vayaapaariyom mem dekhane ko mila tha jo lmbe samay tak ghar se baahar rahate the aur unahem paraॉpar khaana naheem mil paata thaa। vitaamin see paanee mem gholanasheel hai yaani shareer n to ese bamaata hai aur n hee sator karake rakhata hai esalie behatar savaasathay ke lie samay samay par esaka shareer mem pahomchama jaruuree hai। anay kaaraण jinase sakaravee rog ho sakata hai, nimanalikhit haim- - bachachom ko gaay ka duudh theek tarah se ubaalakar n pilaane se bhee sakaravee ho sakata hai। - khaane mem phal aur sabajiyom kee parachor maatara n hone par vitaameen see shareer ko naheem mil paataa। - dhuumarapaan ya sharaab ka jayaada sevan karane par bhee es rog se khatara rahata hai। - garabhavatee hone ke dauraan khaane peene ka dhayaan n rakhane par bhee sakaravee ho sakata hai। Treatments: sakaravee ka upachaar (Treatment of Scurvy) kee jmch karega aur rog se smbmdhit kochh savaal puuchhegaa। yah bahot jaruuree hai ki daॉkatar davaara bataae gae disha miradeshom ka paalan kiya jaae aur bataae gae davaaom ko bhee niyamit samay par khaaya jaae। esake upachaar ke dauraan apake shareer mem vitaamin see kee maatara ko naॉramal kiya jaata hai। apake lie vitaamin see kee parachor maatara se smbmdhit jaamakaaree daॉkatara, apakee umara, jemdar aur apake savaasathay ko dhayaan mem rakhakar degaa। esee ke amosaar apako apana daaet chaarat banaana hogaa। bahot see cheejem haim jinaka dhayaan rakhakar sakaravee hone se bacha ja sakata hai ya sakaravee hone ke khatare ko kam kiya ja sakata hai। -dhayaan rahe ki daaet mem vitaamin see kee parachor maatara ho jisamem, beree, khatate raseele phal jaise neembuu, mausamee, smtara adi , haree miracha, haree patatedaar sabajiym, tarabuuj aur kharabuuj adi shaamil hom। -daaet mem kae tarah ke paushatik cheejem shaamil honee chaahie, jisase shareer ko smpuuraण vitaamin mil sakem। -dhuumarapaan ko chhoड़na Home Remedies: sakaravee rog vitaamin see se joड़a ho hai। vitaamin see (esakorabik esid or Ascorbic Acid) kee kamee hone par sakaravee rog hota hai। sakaravee rog hone ka duusara kaaraण hai tmtarika mem tanaav yaani ki naravas temshana। sakaravee rog mem masuudom se khuum anaa, thakaavat aur shareer mem kamajoree homa adi kochh lakashaण najar ate haim। aee jaanate haim kaun se ghareluu nosakhom se sakaravee rog se nijaat paae ja sakatee hai। sakaravee se bachaav ke lie ghareluu nosakhe (Home Remedies for Scurvy) haree mirach (Green Chillie) haree mirach mem vitaamin see kee uchach maatara hotee hai। haree mirach khaana sakaravee rog se bachane ka sabase achachha upaay hai। sakaravee ke lie laal mirach ka parayog n karem kayomki laal mirach haree mirach ke samaan parabhaavee naheem hai। keevee (Kiwi) keevee mem bhee vitaamin see kee uchach maatara hotee hai। keevee ko salaad ke ruup mem esatemaal karake vitaamin see kee bharapaae kee ja sakatee hai। mvala (Indian Gooseberry) mvala mem bhee vitaamin see hota hai। mvala kee suukhee kaimdee ya mvala ka ras bhee sakaravee rog mem phaayada deta hai। etana hee (Erectile Dysfunctioms) Description: smbhog ke samay limg mem erekashan athava tanaav khatam ho jaane ko erekataael disaphmkashan (Erectile Dysfunctions) arathaat satmbhanadosh kaha jaata hai। jabaki vaasatav mem isa naheem haim। edee haaeparatemshana, daayabiteej v avasaad adi ke kaaraण bhee hota hai। erekataael disaphmkashan shaareerik aur maanasik kaaraणom se bhee ho sakata hai। yadi erekashan smbhog ke alaava kisee vishesh samay jaise sobah sokar uthane para, peshaab karate samaya, hasatamaithon ke dauraan ya sekas ke baare mem sochane par hota hai to ye maanasik kaaraणom kee ephekat bhee naheem hota hai। balad sapalaae (Blood Supply) limg mem dhamaniyom mem kisee parakaar kee rokaavat kee vajah se rakat ke paravaah mem kamee  jaatee hai, to iese mem davaaom kee madad se (Reason of Pellagra) yadi pilaagara ka elaaj samay par na ho to 4 se 5 saalom mem mareej kee maut bhee ho sakatee hai। kae kaarak ise bhee haim jo pilaagara ke risak ko baढ़a sakate haim, jaise: * (Rickets), vitaamin dee kee kamee se hota hai। yah bachachom mem hone vaala rog hai jisamem bachachom kee hadadiym molaayam ho jaatee haim। kae baar hadadiym etamee kamajor ho jaatee haim ki hai। Symptoms: - hadadiyom mem darad Reasons: riketas beemaaree ka ek mokhay kaaran vitaamin dee kee kamee (Deficiency of Vitamin D) hai। ahaaranalee se kailashiyam aur phaasaphoras ke shoshaण mem sarakal - akhom ke neeche ke kaale ghere (Dark Circle) Description: kisee ne sach hee kaha hai ki mkhem bina bole bhee bahot kochh kah jaatee haim। ise mem mkhom ke neeche ke kaale ghere ya daarak sarakal bhee apake savaasathay ko baym karate haim। mkhom ke neeche kaale gherom kee samasaya baढ़tee ja rahee hai। keval mahilaaem hee naheem balaki poruush aur teenej bachachom mem bhee daarak sarakal kee samasaya ho rahee hai। kae baar mkhom ke neeche ke kaale ghere kisee beemaaree ke kaaraण ho sakate haim lekin kae baar isa asavasath jeevamacharaya ke kaaraण bhee hota hai। daarak sarakal (Dark Circle) n keval mkhom kee khuubasuuratee ko kam kar dete haim balaki esase chehara bhee beemaar najar ata hai। mkhom ke neeche kee tavacha bahot patalee hotee hai jisase nasem najar atee haim। jab en nasom mem rakat ka bahaav tejee se hota hai to yah baahar se gaharee najar atee haim jisake kaaraण kaale ghere (Aankhon ke Kale Ghere) majar ate haim। kochh logom mem mkhem mdar kee or dhmsee hoe hotee hai, ise logom mem bhee daarak sarakal najar ate haim। yadi apakee mkhom ke neeche suujan ya badarmg tavacha dikhaae de jo samay ke saath baढ़ rahee ho to chikitasak ko jaruur dikhaaem। samasaya kis kaaraण se hai, yah pata lagaane ke baad daॉkatar asaanee se kaale gherom ka elaaj kar sakata hai। Symptoms: - mkhom ke neeche kaale ghere, - mkhom ke neeche suujan ya badarmg tavacha homge। Home Remedies: samasaya baढ़me par lej tareetamemt ya kemeekal peel therepee kee ja sakatee hai lekin kae baar keval ghareluu nosakhom se bhee daarak sarakal ko hataaya ja sakata hai। haalmki paraakaृtik galo bhee milegaa। yogaa- (yoga) daarak sarakal ka mokhay kaaraण tanaav maana jaata hai ya anaheladee laaephasataaela। ise mem niyamit yog karane se shaareerik aur maanasik sokuun milata hai। yog karane se man shmt rahata hai jisase kaale ghere hone ke chmses kam ho jaate haim। yog karane se shareer ke sabhee mg sochaaruu ruup se kaaray karane lagate haim। Disease: echimg ya khojalee (Itching) Description: tavacha ke kisee bhee hisase mem tavacha ko khorachane kee anobhuuti hona hee khojalee hai। khojalee mem ek shareer mem ek tarah ka senaseshan hota hai jo ki tavacha ko nomchane (Scratch) ya khojalaane par majabuur kar deta hai। Symptoms: - khasara jaisee beemaaree home ke chhah sapataah ke mdar dasat homa Reasons: - garamiyom mem paseena ata rahata hai। baahar se ghar lautane par saara shareer paseene se bheega hota hai, lekin pmkhe v kuular kee thmdee hava se kochh der mem paseema suukh jaata hai। shareer par paseena suukh jaane se khojalee hone lagatee hai। - baajaar mem kholee rakhee cheejem n khaaem। - ghee, tel v makakhan se bane khaaday padaarathom ka sevam n karem। - duushit jal se n nahaaem। - paseene se duushit kapaड़e n pahanem। Home Remedies: emphekashan (Infection), elarajee (Allergy), kisee keeड़e ke kaatane se (Insect Bite), tavacha ke shoshak hone se (Dry Skin), dhuup meom bahot jayaada rahane adi kaaraणom se shareer mem khojalee kee jaatee hai। aee jaanem khojalee se nijaat ke ghareluu nosakhe (Home remedies for Itching) 1. naariyal ka tel (Cocomut oil)- tavacha ke shoshak hone ya kisee keeड़e ke kaatame se, khojalee kisee bhee kaaraण se ho, naariyal ka tel behad phaayademmd hota hai। naariyal ke tel ko khojalee vaale sathaan par lagaakar halake haath se maalish karem। etana hee naheem naariyal tel ko puure shareer par bhee lagaaya ja sakata hai। 2. petaroliyam jailee (Petroleum jelly)- yadi tavacha behad smvedanasheel (sensitive skin) hai to khojalee se mijaat ke lie petaroliyam jailee behad achachha upaay hai। esamem koe bhee rasaayam naheem hota aur tavacha par behad parabhaavee bhee hotee hai। esake esatemaal se m keval khojalee balaki tavacha kee anay samasayaaem bhee hal ho jaatee haim। 3. neembuu (Lemon)- neembuu mem vitaamin see (vitamin c) uchach maatara mem paaya jaata hai। khojalee se nijaat ke lie neembuu behad achachhe upaayom mem se ek hai। neembuu mem maujuud volaataael (volatile) tavacha kee suujan aur jalan ko duur karate haim। parabhaavit tavacha par neembuu ke ras ko ruue kee sahaayata se lagaaya ja sakata hai। 4. bekimg soda (Baking soda)- teen hisase bekimg soda mem ek hisasa paanee milaakar ek pesat banaayem। es pesat ko parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se khojalee kee samasaya se raahat milatee hai। lekin tavacha katee-phatee ho to bekimg soda lagaane se bachana chaahie। 5. tolasee (Basil)- tolasee mem thaayamaॉla, yuujeenaॉl aur kaimphar uchach maatara mem hote haim jo khojalee aur jalan se raahat dete haim। tolasee kee kochh patatiyom ko achachhee parakaar dhokara, parabhaavit sathaan par ragaड़ne se khojalee aur jalan se raahat milatee hai। 6. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ke sirake ka esatemaal ruusee se nijaat ke lie kiya jaata hai, usee parakaar khojalee mem bhee yah laabhadaayak hai। seb ke siraka mem emteesepatik aur emteephmgal goण hote haim jo ki tavacha smbmdhee samasayaaom se nijaat dilaate haim। seb ke siraka mem ruue ko bhigaakar parabhaavit sathaam par lagaane se khojalee kee samasaya se raahat milatee hai। 7. elovera (Aloevera)- elovara maॉeshacharaaejar se bharapuur hota hai jisase ruukhee tavacha se hone vaalee khojalee mem yah asarakaaree hai। elovera jel parabhaavit tavacha par lagaane se khojalee, jalan aur suujan duur hotee hai। tavacha par elovera lagaane ke lie esakee ek patatee ko chaakuu se beech se cheer kar usake mdar se jailee ko baahar mikaalem aur shareer par halake haathom se masaaj karem। 8. neem (Neem)- neem kee patatiyom ko paanee mem daalakar ubaalem। esake baad es paanee ko gomagona rahame par nahaayem। neem mem paraakaृtik taur par emteesepatik goण hote haim jo khojalee ko duur karate haim। esake alaava yadi rakat mem kisee parakaar kee ashodadhi ke kaaraण khojalee hotee hai to sobah sobah meem ke chhote ya kachache patate chabaayem। nibauree chabaane se bhee rakat saaph hokar khojalee duur hotee hai। Disease: gale mem darad (Throat Ache) Description: gale mem darad (Throat ache) saamaanay saradee ka smket bhee ho sakata hai aur vokal korad mem emphekashan ya satarep tharot (strep throat) jaisee kisee gmbheer samasaya ka lakashaण bhee। esamem gale mem chobhan ya chhila ho kharaash mahasuus hotee hai - jabaड़a kholane mem pareshaanee hona - kae baar kaan mem bhee dikakat hona - gale mem chobhan hona Reasons: 1. saamaanay saradee jo vaayaral emphekashan se ho sakatee hai। Disease: javaaemt pena- joड़om mem darad (Joint Paim) Description: javaaemt pena- joड़om mem darad Symptoms: - joड़om ko moड़ne mem pareshaamee hona - joड़om ka laal hona - joड़om mem khimchaav mahasuus hona - joड़om par kathorata hona - chalame- phirane mem dikakat hona - joड़om mem akaड़n ana - joड़om mem suujam aur darad - joड़om mem kamajoree hona Reasons: kaaraण (cause of joint pain) - umar baढ़ne ke saath - hadadiyom mem rakat kee apuurati mem ruukaavat ana - rakat ka kaimsar hona - hadadiyom mem mimaral yaani kee khanij kee kamee homa - joड़om par bahot jayaada dabaav paड़na - joड़om mem emphekasham hona - hadadiyom ka tuutana - moch ana ya chot lagana - hadadiyom mem tayuumar adi kee shikaayat homa - aratharaaetis - barasaaetis - ऑsatiyokomdaraaetis - kaaratilej ka phatana - kee muuvamemt hotee rahanee chaahie। lmbe samay tak ek hee sathiti mem rahame se bhee joड़om mem kathorata mahasuus hotee hai। 2. joड़om ko chot se bachaaem (Prevent joimts from injury) joड़om par lagee chota, hadadee ko toड़ bhee sakatee hai, esalie joड़om ko chot se bachaakar rakhem। jab bhee koe isa khel khelem jisamem joड़om par chot lagane ka dar ho, to javaaemt sephatee pedas (Joint safety pads) pahamem। tenis aur golaph khelate samay bhee bareses (braces) pahanem। 3. vajan ko miymtarit rakhem (Maintain your weight) yadi apaka vajan niymtaraण mem rahega to apake joड़ bhee savaasathay rahemge। shareer ka jayaada vajan ghotanom aur kamar par adhik dabaav daalata hai, jisase kaaratilej (cartilage) ke tuutane ka dar rahata hai। ise mem vajan ko niymtaraण mem rakhana behad jaruuree hai। 4. shoruu karane kee jagaha, esase pahale vaaram ap vayaayaam (warm up exercise) karem। 5. duudh peeem (Drink milk) joड़om ko majabuut rakhane ke lie duudh jaruur peeem। duudh se hadadiyom ko kailashayim aur vitaamin dee milata hai jisase hadadiym majabuut banatee haim। yadi duudh pasmd n ho to duudh se bane anay khaaday padaarath jaise paneera, dahee adi bhee khaae ja sakate haim। 6. sahee poshachar banaae rakhem (Maintain right posture) joड़om ke darad se raahat ke lie sahee poshachar mem uthanaa, baithana aur chalana behad jaruuree hai। sahee poshachar garadan se lekar ghotanom tak ke joड़om kee rakasha karata hai। 7. vayaayaam (Exercise) joड़om ke savaasathay ke lie vayaayaam ko dainik dinacharaya ka hisasa banaaem। tairaakee (swimming) bhee joड़om ke darad se raahat ke lie achachha vayaayaam hotee hai। Home Remedies: joड़om ka darad (Joint Pain) shareer ke kisee bhee bhaag mem ho sakata hai, ghotane, kmdhe ya kamara। kae baar gathiya joड़om ke darad ka kaaraण hota hai jo kae baar tanaav lene, parabhaavit hisasom par jayaada dabaav paड़ne, moch ane ya kisee anay parakaar kee chot lagane ke kaaraण bhee isa ho sakata hai। joड़om ke darad mem parabhaavit hisasa laal ho sakata hai aur vahm suujan bhee  sakatee hai। aee ham apako bataate haim ki kaun se ghareluu upaay apanaakar ap joड़om ke darad mem raahat pa sakate haim। joड़om ke darad ke lie ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies for Joint Paim) maalish (Massage) maalish se shareer ke darad mem behad araam milata hai, yahee parakariya joड़om ke darad mem bhee laaguu hotee hai। naariyala, jaituuna, sarasom ya lahason ke tel se parabhaavit ke lie garam aur thmdee sikaae karane se bhee bahot araam milata hai। garam sikaae karane se rakat smchaar behatar hota hai vaheem thmdee sikaae se suujan aur chobhan kam hotee hai। garam sikaae ke lie garam paanee kee botal ko tauliya mem lapet kar garadan kee sikaae karem। jabaki, thmdee sikaae karane ke lie baraph ke tokaड़om ko tauliya mem lapetakara, us tauliya se sikaae karem। sikaae karate vakat kam se kam do se teem minat tak garadan kee lagaataar sikaae honee chaahie। yah puuree parakariya 15 se 20 minat mem doharaaem। es vidhi ko araam hone tak din mem do baar karem। lahason (Garlic) yadi joड़om mem darad hai to lahason ka esatemaal behad achachhe pariणaam de sakata hai। esake aushadheey goण garadan ke darada, suujan aur jalan ko theek karate haim। lahason kee do kalee har sobah khaalee pet paanee ke saath khaaem। khaana banaane vaale kisee bhee tel mem lahason kee kochh kaliym daal kar bhuun lem। es tel ko gonagona hone tak thmda karem aur parabhaavit hisase kee maalish karem। es vidhi ko din mem do baar kiya ja sakata hai। haladee (Turmeric) haladee ke aushadheey goण kisee se chhipe naheem hai lekim achachhee baat yah bhee hai ki yah joड़om ke darad mem bhee utanee hee parabhaavee hai। haladee rakat smchaar tej karake joड़om ke darad se araam detee hai aur garadan kee akaड़m ko bhee kam karatee hai। adarak (Ginger) joड़om ke darad ke elaaj ke lie adarak bhee behatareen parabhaav dikhaata hai। yah harab bhee goणom se bharapuur hai jo ki rakat smchaar ko tej karatee hai jisase garadan ke darad se raahat milatee hai। ek din mem lagabhag teem kap adarak kee chaay piem। adarak kee chaay banaane ke lie paamee mem adarak ubaalem aur thmda karake esamem shahad milaaem। es pey ko piem। parabhaavit hisase kee adarak ke tel se masaaj bhee kee ja sakatee hai। hone se hote haim। kae baar mtom davaara taral padaarath ko theek tarah se avashoshit (absorb) m kar paane ya mtom se mal ke tejee se nikalane ke kaaraण bhee isa hota hai। dasat hone kee do sathitiym ho sakatee haim, jisamem se ek mem saamaanay se kochh jayaada baar shauch jaate haim jabaki duusaree sathiti mem lagaataar chhaha- saat ya usase jayaada baar shauch jaate haim। yah shauch har baar ekadam patalee hotee hai। yah dasata, paachan smbmdhee samasaya ke kaaraण haate haim। jeevaaणoom davaara smkaramaण tatha taॉkasin adi phailaame se dasat hone shoruu ho jaate haim। kae baar tanaav ya
