Banana) kela mem potaishiyam aur kaarabohaaedaret kee uchach maatara hotee hai jo shareer ko tormt oraja detee hai। rojaana sobah ek gilaas garam duudh ke saath ek kela khaane se vajan baढ़ta hai। duudh mem cheenee bhee milaaem। muumgaphalee ka makakhan (Peanut Butter) muumgaphalee ke makakhan mem uchach kailoree aur paushatik tatav hote haim। am makakhan kee jagah naashate mem muumgaphalee ka makakhan khaane se bhee vajan baढ़ta hai। es makakhan ko phalom ke saath milaakar bhee khaaya ja sakata hai। meva (Dry Fruit) muumgaphalee, baadaama, kaajuu, akharota, kishamish aur mjeer jaise mevom ko bhuunakar khaane se bhee vajan baढ़ne mem madad milatee hai। sabhee meve vasaa, phaaebara, vitaamin aur khanij se bhare hote haim jo ki vajan ko smtolit banaate haim। vajan ko baढ़aane ke lie har roj har roj duudh mem suukhe meve ubaalakar piem। aluu (Potato) aluu bhee kaarabohaaedaret se bhara hota hai। aluu ko yadi makakhan mem talakar khaaya jaae to vajan baढ़aane mem sahaayak hai। aluu ke chipas aur pharaimch pharaaej khaane vaale logom ka vajam bhee tejee se baढ़ta hai। dopahar mem sona (Nap in Afternoon) dopahar ke sone se bhee vajan baढ़ta hai। dopahar ko khaane ke baad takareeban 45 minat se ek ghmte kee neemd lem। isa karame se bhee vajan baढ़egaa। vayaayaam (Excersise) rojaana vayaayaam karane se apakee bhuukh kholatee hai। jisase ap bhojan kee achachhee maatara khaate haim jo ki vajam baढ़aane mem sahaayak hai। Disease: esiditee ya amalapitat (Acidity) Descriptiom: esiditee (Acidity) Symptoms: - kabhee-kabhee chhaatee mem darad ho sakata hai। - khatatee dakaarem anaa, - khaana ya khatata paanee (esida) momh mem  jaanaa, - chhaatee mem jalan hona - pet mem gais banana - matalee aur ulatee Reasons: kaaraण (Cause of Acidity) ham jo bhee khaate haim, usaka paachan (Digestion) behad jaruuree hota hai। bhojan ke paachan ke lie amaashay mem kae tarah ke paachan rasaayanom ka sataraav hota hai jaise ki haaedarokalorik esid (Hydrochloric acid) aur pepasin (Pepsin)। saamaanay ruup se yah donom esid amaashay mem hee rahate haim aur khaane kee nalee ke beech mem naheem ate kayomki amaashay aur khaame kee nalee ke beech mem mmsapeshiym hotee haim jo ki smkochanasheelata ke kaaraण amaashay aur bhojan nalee ka raasata bmd rakhatee haim। yah raasata tab hee kholata hai jab ham kochh khaate ya peete haim lekim kabhee- kabhee kisee vikaृti ke kaaraण yah raasata apane ap khol jaata hai jisase amaashay mem maujuud haaedarokalorik esid aur pepasin khaane kee malee mem  jaate haim। jab yah kariya baar baar hone lagatee hai to vayakati ko esiditee kee samasaya ho jaatee hai jisake baढ़ne par alasar tak ho sakata hai। esiditee ke anay kaaraण niman haim (Other Reason & Causes of Acidity) - khaana-paan mem aniyamitata - khaane ko theek se n chabaana - parayaapat maatara mem paanee n peema - masaaledaar khaana jayaada khaana - dhuumarapaan aur sharaab ka jayaada sevam Treatments: - paamee jayaada se jayaada se peeem - chaaya-kaॉphee kam se kam peeem - koladadarimk ya anay aratiphishiyal pey n lem - khaana samay se khaaem aur khaakar kochh der tahalem, tormt soem naheem - jayaada talaa-bhona ya masaaledaar khaana n khaaem - bhojan banaane mem heemg ka parayog karem Home Remedies: pet mem paachan ras kee jayaada ya kam maatara nikalane par esiditee kee pareshaanee hotee hai। esiditee hone par pet mem darad (Stomach Pain), gais (Gas), momh se badabuu (Mouth Odour) aur jee michalaane (Nausea) jaisee samasayaaem ho sakatee haim। jo log akasar esiditee se pareshaan rahate haim unake lie samasaya gmbheer ho sakatee hai। esiditee masaaledaar khaana khaame, aniyamit khaane (Irregular Eating) kee adatem ya bahot jayaada satares lene se bhee hotee hai। etana hee naheem jayaada sharaab peene aur chaaya-kaॉphee peene vaalom ko bhee esiditee kee dikakat hotee hai। aee apako bataate haim ki kaun se ghareluu nosakhe apanaakar ap asaanee se esiditee se raahat pa sakate haim। esiditee se bachaav ke lie ghareluu nosakha़e (Home Remedies for Acidity) tolasee ke patate (Basil Leaves) tolasee ke patate apako tormt esiditee, gais aur ulatee se raahat de sakate haim। upachaar ke lie kochh tolasee ke patate chaba kar khaaem। esake alaava tolasee ke kochh patate paanee mem ubaalakara, us paanee ko chhaan lem। gonagona rahane par shahad milaakar piem। yah bhee esiditee ke lie achachha upaay hai। daalacheenee (Cinnamom) daalacheenee ek paraakaृtik emtaasid (Antacid) hai jo paachan shakati ke lie behad achachhee hai aur gais ko duur rakhatee hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap paanee mem adha chamamach daaleecheenee paaudar daalakar ubaalem। es paanee ko ek dim mem do se teen baar piem। esake alaava suup ya salaad mem bhee daalacheenee paaudar daalakar khaaya ja sakata hai। chhaachh (Buttermilk) chhaachh peene se bhee esiditee mem bahot raahat milatee hai। chhaachh mem pet kee amalata ko smtolit karame ke lie laikatik esid hota hai। upachaar ke lie methee ke daanom ko paanee ke saath milaakar pesat bana lem। es pesat ko ek gilaas chhaachh mem milaakar piem। esase pet ka darad bhee theek hoga aur gais se bhee raahat milegee। saath hee, esiditee bhee khatam hogee। savaad baढ़aame aur behatar pariणaam ke lie es chhaachh mem kaala namak aur kaalee mirach bhee milaae ja sakatee hai। seb ka siraka (Apple Cider Vinegar) seb ka siraka bhee esiditee ko theek karane ka asaan tareeka hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap paanee mem do chamamach kachacha seb ka siraka milaakar din mem do baar piem। khaana khaane se pahale bhee ese piya ja sakata hai। laumg (Cloves) laumg khaane se pet mem haaedarokalorik esid kee maatara baढ़ jaatee hai jisase pet kee amalata kam hotee hai aur esiditee se raahat milatee hai। raahat ke lie khaane ke baad do se teen laumg ko momh mem rakhakar halaka halaka chabaakar chuusem। jeera (Cumin) jeera bhee ek behatareen esid nayuutaraalaaejar (Acid Neutralizer) hai jo esiditee ko kam karata hai। esake saath hee paachan shakati ko baढ़aakar pet darad se bhee raahat deta hai। upachaar ke lie jeera ko bhuunakar usaka paaudar bamaaem। es paaudar ko khaana khaane ke baad ek gilaas paanee mem milaakar piem। jeera paaudar ko chhaachh mem milaakar bhee piya ja sakata hai। adarak (Ginger) adarak mem pet kee amalata se laड़me ke goण hote haim jo esiditee se raahat dete haim। upachaar ke lie khaane ke baad adarak ka ek chhota tokaड़a momh mem rakhakar chabaaem। ya phir ek kap paanee mem adarak ko kochalakar daalem aur ubaalem। es paamee ko chhanakar piem। goड़ (Jaggery) goड़ mem paachan ke lie behad achachhee khaaday saamagaree hai saath hee goड़ khaane se pet kee amalata bhee kam hotee hai jisase esiditee se raahat milatee hai। upachaar ke lie har roj khaane ke baad ek tokaड़a goड़ ka khaaem। haalmki yah upaay shogar rogiyom ke lie theek naheem hai। thmda duudh (Cold Milk) duudh pet mem esid ke niramaaण ko rokata hai saath hee gaisatarik esid ko sathir karake esiditee kee samasaya hone se bachaata hai। haalmki esiditee kee samasaya hone par siraph thmda duudh hee peena chaahie। garam duudh utana laabhakaaree naheem hotaa। saumph (Fennel) saumph khaane ko pachaane mem sahaayata karatee hai aur gais ko duur rakhatee hai। har roj khaana khaane ke baad saumph ko momh mem rakhakar chabaaem। saumph ke saath misharee bhee milaae ja sakatee hai। isa karane se esiditee se raahat milatee hai। Disease: elarajee (Allergy) Description: elarajee (Allergy) kisee bhee cheej ke parati atismvedanasheel hona hee elarajee hai, jise savaasathay kee bhaasha mem etopee (atopy) bhee kahate haim। elarajee kisee se bhee ho sakatee hai, mausam mem badalaav se, kisee khaane kee cheej se, paalato jaanavar se, dhuul se, dhoem se, saumdaray parasaadhanom se ya davaaom adi se। elarajee mem shareer ka emayuun sisatam kochh khaas cheejom ko saveekaar naheem kar paataa। en cheejom ke parati emayuunitee ayogay tarah se paratikariya detee hai। emayuunitee davaara dee jaane vaalee paratikariya hee elarajee hotee hai। yuum dekha jaae to adhikatar elarajee khataranaak naheem hotee lekin kabhee kabhee samasaya gmbheer ho jaatee hai। elarajee ko roka ja sakata hai, lekin esake lie elarajee paida karane vaale kaaraणom se puuree tarah duur rahana hogaa। yuum to elarajee phailane vaalee beemaaree naheem hai phir bhee yadi kisee ko naak bahane aur mkhom se paanee ane vaalee elarajee ho to usase smparak banaakar rakhane mem hee behataree hai। smbhav ho to usake davaara esatemaal kie gae saamaan ko bhee esatemaal n karem। Symptoms: - mkh mem khojalee hona aur mkh ka laal ho jaana - mkh se paanee ana - egajima aur garamiyom mem bokhaar - gale mem khojalee hona - tavacha par khojalee hona - tavacha par pitat uthana - tavacha par laal chakatate aur daane hona - maak ke mdar baara- baar daane nikalana - naak mem baara-baar khojalee hona - naak se paanee ana Reasons: elarajee ke kaaraण- (cause of allergy) 1. dhuul (Dust) dhuul ke kaण bahot chhote jeev hote haim jo hamaare- as paas kee jayaadaatar vasatoom par rahate haim। yah kaण uchach adarata mem pamapate haim jo maृt tavachaa, baikateeriya aur phmgas adi se apana khaana paraapat karate haim। 2. keet (Insect) keetom se elarajee vaale logom ko keetom ke kaatane se dmk lagane se tavacha ekadam laal hokar phuul jaatee hai। etana hee naheem unahem ulatee, chakakar ana aur bokhaar bhee ho sakata hai। 3. khaana (Food) kochh logom ko rojamarara mem khaayee jaane vaalee cheejom se bhee elarajee hotee hai, jaise muumgaphalee, duudh aur mda adi। khaaday padaarath se elarajee vaale logom ko khaane ke baad jee michalaane, shareer mem khojalee hone ya daane nikalane kee samasaya ho sakatee hai। 4. rabaड़ (Latex) rabaड़ se bana koe bhee utapaada, elarajee ka kaaraण ho sakata hai। kochh logom ko rabaड़ se bane utapaad bhee mokasaan pahomchaate haim, jaise dasataane, kmdoma, medikal upakaraण adi ke esatemaal se jalana, naak bahanaa, chheemkanaa, sms kee ghabaraahat aur khojalee kee samasayaaem ho sakatee haim। 5. khoshabuu (Fragrance) achachhee khoshabuu bhale achachhee lagatee ho lekim yah bhee kochh logom kee elarajee ka kaaraण ho sakatee hai। paraphayuuma, khoshabuu vaalee momabatatiym, kae tarah ke bayuutee paraॉdakat adi kee khoshabuu se sir darada, jee michalaane aur naak kee elarajee ho sakatee hai। 6. jaanavar (Pets) paalato jaanavar bhee kae logom kee elarajee ka kaaraण hote haim। jaanavarom ke baala, unake momh se nikalame vaalee laara, ruusee adi se kae gmbheer pareshaaniym ho sakatee haim। 7. ghaas (Grass) kae baar ghaasa, peड़ aur phuul bhee elarajee ka kaaraण hote haim। yah sab mausamee elarajee ka kaaraण hote haim, jinase khojalee, mkhom mem jalama, lagaataar chheemk ana aur khojalee adi kee samasaya ho sakatee hai। Treatments: elarajee se nijaat paane ke lie upaay (Tips to Prevent Allergy) - dhuula, dhom aur gmdagee se bachakar rahem। - kochh davaaom jaise esapireena, nimosalaaed adi ke sevan mem saavadhaanee baratem। - khatatee cheejom, jaise achaar adi ka esatemaal kam karem। - ise khaaday padaarath jinahem khaane se elarajee hai, unahem n khaaem। - gmdagee se elarajee vaale logom ko samaya-samay par chaadara, takiye ke kavar aur parade adi badalate rahane chaahie। Home Remedies: dhuul (Dust), gmdagee (Dirt), mausam mem parivaratan (Climate change), seelana, adi kochh ise kaaraण haim jinase vayakati ko elarajee (Allergy) ho sakatee hai। parayaavaraण mem maujuud cheejom ke lie alaga-alag smvedanasheelata hotee hai jisake chalate hamaara shareer paratikariya karata hai। ise mem vijaateey padaarathom kee shareer mem asaveekaarata elarajee hai। kochh logom ko khaane kee cheejom se elarajee ho sakatee hai। adhik chheemkem amaa, sms lete samay avaaj honaa, shareer mem kisee tarah kee suujana, khojalee, chakakar anaa, jee ghabaraanaa, pet mem maroड़ hona adi elarajee ke kochh lakashaण haim। aee apako bataate haim elarajee se bachane ke kochh ghareluu upaae (Home remedies of Allergy): 1.shahad (Honey)- shahad shareer kee rog paratirodhak kashamata ko baढ़aata hai। rojaana do chamamach shahad ka esatemaal shareer ko kaaphee laabh pahomchaata hai। ek gilaas gonagome paanee mem shahad mila kar peene se ya duudh mem shahad mila kar peene se kaaphee laabh pahomchata hai। 2. seb (Apple)- rojaana ek seb khaane se emayuum sisatam (immune system) behatar hota hai aur ap elarajee se duur rahate haim। seb ka juus bhee peeya ja sakata hai। 3.haladee (Turmeric)- elarajee se bachaane mem haladee bhee kaaphee parabhaavashaalee hai। haladee mem taakatavar emtee ऑkaseedemt paae jaate haim jo elarajee se laड़ne mem madad karate haim। ek gilaas garam duudh mem ek chamamach haladee milaakar peene se kaaphee laabh pahomchata hai। 4. lahasuun (Garlic)- lahasuun bhee ek emtee elarajee khaaday padaarath hai jise apanee daaet mem shaamil karana avashayak hai। yah ek emtee baॉyotika, emtee ऑkaseedemt aur emayuunitee baढ़aane vaala khaaday padaarath hai। lahasuun ko sabajee mem daalakar ya sobah khaalee pet ek do kalee paanee ke saath nigalame se kaaphee phaayada hota hai। 5.neembuu (Lemom)- neembuu mem uchach maatara mem vitaamin see aur emtee ऑkaseedemt paaya jaata hai। neembuu emayuun sisatam baढ़aata hai aur elarajee se duur rakhane mem kaaphee phaayademmd saabit hota hai। 6. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ke sevan se sms kee beemaaree mem araam milata hai। ise mem yah asathama se smbmdhit elarajee mem kaaphee araam pahomchaata hai। rojaana adarak ka sevan karane se elarajee se raahat paae ja sakatee hai। daॉkatar kee salaah par adarak ke sapaleememt bhee lie ja sakate haim। 7. gareen tee (Green tea)- gareen tee mem maujuud emteeऑkaseedemtas shareer kee rog paratirodhak kashamata ko baढ़aate haim। esamem maujuud thiyaaneen bhee elarajee se bachaane mem madad karata hai। yadi kisee ko gareem tee pasmd n ho to balaik tee bhee pee ja sakatee hai। 8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam mem vitaamin bee, e, maiganeeshiyama, jimka, seleniyam (selemium) tatha anay savaasathayavaradhak vasa paae jaatee hai। jis kaaraण yah tanaav se to raahat dete hee haim saath hee elarajee se bachaane mem bhee madad karate haim। rog paratirodhak kashamata ko tej kar shareer aur dimaag ko majabuutee dete haim। baadaam ko bhuun kar ya kachacha bhee khaaya ja sakata hai। yadi ise khaana smbhav n ho to baadaam ka paaudar banaakara, duudh ke saath khaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: motiyaabimda- keterekat (Cataract) Description: keterekat ya motiyaabimd (Cataract) motiyaabimd mkh ke lems mem ubhara saphed rmg ka dhababa hai, jo ki mkh kee daृshati ko parabhaavit karata hai। motiyaabimd hone se vayakati ko koe bhee vasato dhomdhalee najar atee hai। motiyaabimd jayaadaatar bojoragom ko hota hai। motiyaabimd keval ek mkh ya donom mkhom mem bhee ho sakata hai, yahm tak ki yah ek mkh se duusaree mkh mem bhee phail sakata hai। Symptoms: - mkhom ke lems par saphed parat ka jamana - ek mkh se do cheejem najar ana - kae dapha halakee roshamee bhee bahot tej parateet hona - kisee bhee vasato ka rmg halaka najar ana - koe bhee vasato dhomdhalee najar ana - chashame ka nmbar baara-baar badalana - tej roshanee se pareshaanee hona - raat kee laaet mem chhalale moma akaृti najar ana - raat ko gaaड़ee chalaane mem dikakat homa - shaam hote hee mkhom kee roshanee aur bhee kamajor hona Reasons: mkh ke mdar ka lems kaimare kee tarah kaam karata hai। yahee retina par laaet ko phokas karata hai jisase cheejem saaph najar atee haim। lems paamee aur paroteen se milakar bamata hai। paroteen es tarah se lems ke saath joड़ee rahatee hai ki yah lems ko saaph rakhatee hai jisase ki roshanee ara-paar ja sake। umar baढ़ne ke saath kae baar kochh paroteen ek jagah ekatathee ho jaatee hai aur lems ke ek hisase par jama ho jaatee hai। ise mem motiyaabimd mkh ke lems mem atayadhik paroteen ke banane ke kaaraण hota hai jo lems ko dhomdhala bama deta hai। yah lems ke jarie roshanee ko puuree tarah jaane maheem deta jisase mkh se saaph dikhaae naheem detaa। ise mem sabhee nae lems selasa, lems ke baahar kee or jama ho jaate haim jabaki sabhee poraane lems selasa, lems ke beechom beech ek jagah ekatatha ho jaate haim, jise motiyaabimd ya keterekat kahate haim। motiyaabimd hone ke anay kaaraण (other reason & causes of cataract) - mkhom mem kisee tarah ka anay rog honaa, jaisa galuukoma adi - janamajaat mkh mem motiyaabimd hona - daayabiteej hona - shareer mem kisee pareshaamee, jaise asathama ke lie sateraॉed lema - achaamak se tej roshanee ke smparak mem ane se ya lagaataar tej roshanee mem rahane se - dhuumarapaan ya sharaab adi ka jayaada sevam karane se Treatments: motiyaabimd ke upaay (tips to prevent cataract) - dhuup ya tej roshamee se khod ko bachaaem, mkhom par chashama aur sir par topee pahan ke rahem - kisee bhee tarah ka koe nasha n karem - paushatik khaana khaaem - samaya-samay par mkhom kee jmch karavaaem - tanaav se duur rahem - daayabiteej niymtaraण mem rakhem Home Remedies: jab mkhom kee baat ho to samasaya ko gmbheerata se lena chaahie, kayomki yadi mkhom kee roshanee ek baar chalee gae to dobaara naheem paae ja sakatee। motiyaabimd (Cataract) bhee isee hee gmbheer samasaya hai, jisamem mkhom ke lems par ek dhababa (spot on the eye lens)  jaata hai। jisase ap jo bhee cheej dekhate haim vah apako dhomdhalee najar atee hai aur vahm apako dhababa jaisa najar ata hai। yuum to motiyaabimd ko sarajaree ke davaara hataaya ja sakata hai lekin kochh ghareluu nosakhom kee madad se bhee motiyaabimd ka elaaj smbhav hai। yadi shoruuat mem sachet hokar yah apanaae jaaem to smbhav hai apako sarajaree ya ऑpareshan n karavaana paड़e। motiyaabimd ke lie ghareluu mosakha़e (Home Remedies for Cataract) lahason (Garlic) lahason ke asmkhay savaasathay laabh haim aur yah mkhom ke lie bhee samaan ruup se laabhakaaree hai। lahason kee do se teen kaliym (2 to 3 clove) rojaama khaame se mkhom se ekadam saaph dikhaae deme lagega aur kochh hee dinom mem dhababe kee shikaayat duur ho jaaegee। paalak (Spinach) paalak khaane se motiyaabimd kaaphee had tak theek ho jaata hai। paalak mem beeta kairoteen (Bet Carotene) or emteeऑkaseedemt (Antioxidents) goण hote haim। paalak ko rojaana khaane se mkhom ka motiyaabimd kochh din mem hee khatam ho jaata hai aur mkhem pahale jaisee ho jaatee haim। duudh aur baadaam (Milk amd Almond) motiyaabimd se pareshaan logom kee mkhem jayaadaatar laal rahatee haim aur samasaya se nipatana aur bhee moshakil hota hai। ise mem duudh aur baadaam mkhom ko laabh dete haim। upachaar ke lie baadaam ko raat bhar duudh mem bhigaakar chhoड़ dem। es duudh ko sobah chhaanakar esakee buumde mkhom mem daalem aur baadaam ko chaba kar kha lem। gareen tee (Green Tea) gareem tee se mkhom kee roshanee tej ho sakatee hai। gareen tee saamaanay mkhom kee samasaya mem bhee laabhakaaree hai। rojaana teen se chaar baar gareen tee peeme mkhom ko savaasathay laabh hota hai। gareem tee mem maujuud emteeऑkaseedemt (Antioxident) mkhom ko nae saradee aur kaph (Cough And Cold) Description: saradee aur kaph (Cough and Cold) naak bah rahee hai, ya bmd hai jisase ki sms lene mem takaleeph ho rahee hai, gale mem darad mahasuus ho raha hai ya gale mem chobhan aur chhila (scratchy throat) jaise mahasuus ho raha hai aur khmsee ke saath balagam (muscus) pareshaan kar raha hai to samajh leejie ap saradee- jokaam aur kaph se pareshaan haim। Symptoms: - mkhom se khuub paanee ana aur jalan hona - avaaj bhaaree hona - khaane mem savaad aur khoshabuu mahasuus n hona - gala chhila ho ya darad mahasuus hona - chheemk ama - naak ka bmd hona - naak se khuub paanee girana - naak se gale kee or balagam ka girama - mmsapeshiyom mem darad ya khimchaav hona - sir bhaaree mahasuus hona ya halaka darad hona Reasoms: kaaraण- (Cause of Cough amd Cold) saradee hinovaayaras (rhinovirus) se phailatee hai jo ki 10 se 40 paratishat tak saradee ko shareer mem paravesh karaata hai। vaheem koronaavaayaras (coromavirus) lagabhag 20 paratishat saradee ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। emake alaava resapeeretaree simseetaayal vaayaras (respiratory syncytial virus) aur pairaaemphaluuemja vaayaras (parainfluenz virus) 10 pheesadee tak saradee ke lie jimamedaar hote haim। saradee, smkaramaण se bhee phailatee hai। ek smkaramit vayakati ya usake davaara esatemaal kie gae saamaan ke smparak mem ane se duusare ko bhee saradee kee samasaya ho sakatee hai। yah vaayaras shareer ke mdar pahomchakar vayakati kee rog kashamata ko parabhaavit karate haim aur kaaphee maatara mem balagam banaana shoruu kar dete haim, jisase gala aur naak puuree tarah parabhaavit ho jaate haim। etana hee naheem smkaramit vayakati ke chheemkane (sneezing), usase haath milaane se bhee saradee ke baikateeriya duusare vayakati ko parabhaavit kar sakate haim। saradee aur kaph ke lie kae amay kaaraण (Other causes of Cough and Cold) - kamare mem seelan ya ghotan ho - tej dhuup se ane ke baad tormt thmda paanee peena - shareer kee paratirodhak kashamata kamajor hona kiya ja sakata hai। esase bmd naak kholegee aur raahat milegee। - garam paanee mem namak daal kar garaare karate rahem। - khaane-peene se pahale apane haath achachhee tarah dhoem। - smkaramik vayakati ke smparak mem n aem, jaise ki haath milaane kee jagah namasate kee ja sakatee hai। - yadi ap khod smkaramit haim to bheeड़ vaalee jagahom par jaane se bachem aur apanee cheejem jaise ruumaal adi duusarom se duur rakhem। - thmdee aur baahar kee cheejem khaane se parahej karem। Home Remedies: mausam mem parivaratana, sarada-garam hone ya paraduushaण aur elarajee (Allergy) ya smkaramaण (Infection) ke kaaraण saradee-khmsee kee samasaya ho jaatee hai। kae baar smkaramaण bhee esaka kaaraण hota hai। aee jaanate haim, saradee khmsee se bachaav ke ghareluu nosakhe (Home Remedies for Cough and Cold): 1. haladee (Turmeric)- adha kap garam paanee ko ubaal lem phir usamem ek chamamach kaalee mirach paaudar (black pepper powder), ek chamamach haladee paaudar aur ek chamamach shahad milaaem। ab es misharaण ko do se teen minat tak ubaal lem aur niyamit taur par kaaढ़e kee tarah peeem। 2. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ko ghisakar ya chhote-chhote tokaड़om mem kaatakar ek kap paanee mem daalakar ubaal lem। din bhar mem teen se chaar baar es ghol ko peeem। shahad aur neembuu ko adarak ke ras mem milaakar peene se bhee kaph kee shikaayat duur hotee hai। 3. meembuu (Lemon)- ek chamamach shahad mem do chamamach neembuu ka ras milaakar garam kar lem। din bhar mem kae baar es ghol ko dava kee tarah lete rahem। 4. lahasom (Garlic)- laumg ke tel aur shahad mem lahason kee do se teen kalee ko pees kar mila lem। din bhar mem kae baar thoड़ee thoड़ee maatara mem esaka sevan karate rahem। 5. payaaj (Onion)- ek chamamach shahad mem adha chamamach payaaj ka ras lem aur esako milaakar din bhar mem kam se kam do baar avashay sevan karem। kaph aur gale kee kharaash se raahat milegee। 6. garam taral padaarath peeem (Drink warm liquids)- garam paanee peeem ye gale kee suujan (throat sweeling) ke lie phaayademmd hai। ap chaahem to koe anay garam padaarath bhee pee sakate haim। 7. shahad (Honey)- shahad gale ko araam pahomchaane ke lie ek paarmparik upaay hai। ek gilaas garam paanee mem shahad aur neembuu ka ras milaakar din mem teen baar peene se khnsee se raahat milatee hai। 8. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ka siraka har tarah kee khnsee ke lie achachha hai। 2 baड़a chamamach siraka 10 tola paanee mem milaakar garam karem। esamem ek chamamach shahad daalakar peeem। khmsee mem raahat paane ka kaaragar upaay hai। 9. tolasee ke patate aur shahad (Honey and basil leaves)- dhole hoe tolasee ke kochh patatom ko kuut kar usaka ras nikaalem aur usame shahad milaaem। ab ese chamamach mem garam karake din mem 3-4 baar lem, es ghareluu upaay se khmsee mem jaladee araam milata hai। Disease: titanas (Tetamus) Description: titanas (Tetanus) mamoshayom ke ghaav (Wound) mem smkaramaण home se titamas hota hai jisaka kaaraण kalosatareediyam titaanee baikateeriya (Clostridium Tetani Bacteria) hai। yahee jeevaaणo ghaav ya chot mem vish paida karata hai jisase titamas ho jaata hai। dheere-dheere yahee jahar puure shareer mem phailane lagata hai jisase sathiti ghaatak ho jaatee hai। titamas ke kaaraण kae baar vayakati kee maृtayo bhee ho sakatee hai। titanas mem shareer kee mmsapeshiyom mem imthan mahasuus hotee hai aur ruuk ruuk kar darad hota hai। haalmki kisee chot ke lagane ke baad yadi tormt titanas ka teeka lagavaaya jaae to esase hone vaalee pareshaaniyom se bacha ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - uchach rakatachaap - garadan mem imthan hona - chiड़chiड़aapan - chehare kee mmsapeshiyom ka jakaड़ jaana - jabaड़e ka bmd ho jaana - nigalane mem dikakat hona - paseena khuub ama - mmsapeshiyom mem imthan aur akaड़n mahasuus hona - sms lene mem takaleeph hona - kalosatareediyam titaanee titanas rog ke lie jimamedaar jeevaaणo hai। yah baikateeriya do ruupom mem paaya jaata hai, pahala dorammt ya nishakariy ruup mem duusara sakariy ruup mem jo jeevaaणoom kee smkhaya ko aur bhee baढ़a deta hai। kisee bhee tarah kee chot mem titanas ho sakatee hai। - ghaav se - sarajaree mem - parasav ke dauraan - koe phoड़a hone par - soe ya emjekashan se nasha karane vaalom ko - kisee poraane jmg lage lohe se chot lagane se Treatments: titanas se bachane ke lie tipas (Tips to Prevent Tetanus) - koe bhee isa ghaav jisase tavacha phat gae ho, use tormt paanee aur saabon se saaph kiya jaana chaahie। - ghaav ko kabhee khola n chhoड़em। khole ghaav ke smkaramaण ka khatara jayaada hota hai। - yadi ghaav se khuun bah raha ho to to us par suutee aur suukha kapaड़a bmdhem। - rakat ko rokane ke lie ghaav ke opar dabaav daalem, jisase rakat bahana ruuk jaae। - ghaayal vayakati ko tormt titamas ka teeka lagavaama chaahie। titanas ke amay upachaar (Treatmemt of Tetanus) - ghaav ko garam paanee se dhoem aur koe emteesepatik kareem ya paaudar lagaaem। - taarapeen ke tel se shareer kee maalish karem, esamem paira, jabaड़e aur garadan par halake haath se dabaav daalate hoe maalish karem। - ghaav ke opar tel ko garam karake usamem haladee milaakar lagaaem - momabatatee ke mom ko pighalaakar bhee ghaav par lagaaya ja sakata hai - kate sathaan par neem ka tel lagaane se bhee titanas ka dar naheem rahata Disease: moch (Sprains) Description: moch (Sprains) shareer ke joड़ ke ligaamemt (ligament) ya sanaayo jab kisee chot ke kaaraण jaruurat se jayaada khimch jaate haim to es avasatha ko moch (Sprains or Moch) kaha jaata hai। jayaada khimchaav ke kaaraण peshiyom ke phaaebar phat jaate haim aur ligaamemt mem ghaav ho jaata hai। ligaamemt ek hadadee ko duusaree hadadee se joड़ne (connect) ka kaaray karate haim। Symptoms: - chot vaalee jagah par asahaneey darad - chot vaalee jagah par sonanapam hona - parabhaavit sathaan ko moड़ne ya chalaane mem pareshaanee hona - parabhaavit sathaam par neela ya kaala dhababa ana - parabhaavit sathaan par suujan ana - bina sahaare ke chalane phirane mem dikakat hona Reasons: moch ke kaaraण- (Causes of Sprains) moch shareer ke alaga-alag hisasom mem alaga-alag kaaraणom se  sakatee hai। moch saamaanay ya karonik bhee ho sakatee hai। 1. emkal mem moch (Ankle Sprains)- omchee-neechee jagah par chalane ya dauड़ne se emkal mem moch  sakatee hai। kae baar haae heel pahanane se pair achaanak se moड़ta hai, yah bhee pair mem moch ka kaaraण ho sakata hai। 2. ghotane mem moch (Knee Sprains)- bhaagate- bhaagate achaamak gir jaane ya koe bhaaree vasato uthaakar chalane se ghotanom mem moch  sakatee hai। kae baar chalate chalate achaanak ghotana moड़ jaata hai। yah bhee ghotane mem moch ka kaaraण ho sakata hai। 3. kalaae mem moch (Wrist Sprains)- girane ke dauraan haath ke moड़ne, kisee ke davaara haath ko galat tareeke se kheemchane, khel ke dauraan adi sathitiyom mem kalaae mem moch  sakatee hai। 4. kamar mem moch (Waist Sprains)- kae baar seeढ़iym chaढ़ne utarane mem dikakat hone yaa, kisee omchee jagah se kamar ke bal girane se ya jaruurat se jayaada bhaaree cheej ko jhokakar uthaane se kamar mem moch  sakatee hai। 5. mguuthe mem moch (Thumb Sprains)- kae tarah ke khel khelame ya kaheem mguutha dab jaame ke kaaraण chot lagane se mguuthe mem moch  sakatee hai। 6. garadan mem moch (Neck Sprains)- achaamak se garadan mem jhataka lagame, jayaada omcha takiya lagaane, kisee parakaar se garadam mem chot lagane kee sathiti mem garadan mem moch  sakatee hai। anay kaaraण (other causes & reason of sprains) - kae baar vayaayaam karane se pahale vaaramaap n hona aur achaanak se kathin vayaayaam shoruu kar dena bhee moch ane ka kaaraण ho sakata hai। - pair mem paraॉpar photaviyar n hone se bhee pair ke moड़ne ya chot lagane ka khatara baढ़ jaata hai jisase moch kee smbhaavana rahatee hai। Treatments: moch se nijaat ke lie upaay (Treatment of Sprain Pain) - moch se nijaat ke lie parabhaavit sathaan par chane bmdh dem। em chanom ko baara- baar bhigaate rahem। jaise jaise chane phuulemge, moch theek hotee jaaegee। - moch vaale sathaan par ermd ke patatom ko halaka sa semk kar us par sarasom ka tel lagaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par bmdh dem। - til ke tel mem apheem milaakar moch vaale sathaan par bmdh dem। - moch vaale sathaan par haladee, chuuna aur shahad ko milaakar lagaane se chot theek ho jaatee hai। - moch se nijaat ke lie tejapatata aur laumg ko peesakar lep lagaaem। - sarasom ke tel mem ajavaayan aur lahason ko garam karake, es tel se moch vaale sathaan kee maalish karem। - paam ke patate par sarasom ka tel lagaakar use halaka garam karem aur moch vaale sathaan par bmdhem । - tolasee patatom ke ras mem sarasom ka tel milaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। tormt araam milegaa। - akharot ke tel se maalish karane par bhee chot mem araam milata hai। - namak ko garam karake, kisee mote kapaड़e mem bmdhakara, chot vaale sathaan par bmdh dem। araam milegaa। - namak aur haladee ko milaakar chot vaale sathaan par lagaane se bhee araam milegaa। - paan ke patate ya am ke patate par tel lagaakara, us par namak lagaaem aur garam karake chot vaale sathaan par bmdh dem। isa karane se bhee moch theek ho jaaegee। - moch aur suujam mem elovera lagaane se bhee araam milata hai। Home Remedies: omchee eड़ee ke juute-chapapal pahaname, pair omche neeche paड़ne, vayaayaam bahot jayaada ya galat tarah se karane, bahot jayaada chalame, galat tarah se uthane baithane adi ise kochh kaaraण haim, jinase shareer mem moch (sprain) kee sathiti ban jaatee hai। kae dapha darad asahaneey bhee ho sakata hai aur parabhaavit jagah par laal ya neela nishaam aur suujan bhee  sakatee hai। yadi khimchaav kee pareshaamee ho to pairom ko thaणd se bachaayem aur ise kapaड़e ka chonaav karem jo thaणd ke dinom mem apake pairom ko hava n lagane dem। aee jaanem moch se raahat ke ghareluu upaay (Home remedies for sprain): 1. garam aur thmda semk (Hot and cold compress)- shareer ke darad vaale hisase par karam se garam aur thmde paanee ka sek karem, ye tamaavagarasat mmsapeshiyom ko araam pahomchaaegaa। ese kae tareeke se kar sakate haim jaise ki tauliye ko garam paanee mem dobaayem aur tamaavagarasat mmsapeshee par laga sakate haim। tanaavagarasat mmsapeshee mem araam ke lie gonagone paanee se nahaaya ja sakata hai ya bhaap le sakate haim। baraph lagaakar bhee araam pa sakate haim। 2. mmsapeshee ko kheemchana (Stretch your muscle)- din paratidin kee saamaamay shaareerik parakariya ke liye jaane se pahale, mmsapeshiyom ko kheemchana mahatavapuuraण hota hai। esake lie halakee halakee satarechimg karem। agar apako raat mem sote samay pairom mem khimchaav hota hai, to achachha hoga ki ap mmsapeshiyom ko kheemchane ka abhayaas karem। 3. taral padaarath lete rahem (Take enough liquid)- taral padaarath ke saath paanee ko niyamit mtaraal par lekar shareer mem namee banaayem rakhem। 8 gilaas paanee peene ke saath apako phalom ka juus bhee peena chaahiye। parayaapat maatara mem taral lena apake mmsapeshiyom mem kam maroड़ paida karega aur araam degaa। 4. kela (Banana)- kele mem parayaapat maatara mem potaishiyam hota hai। yah shareer ke liye behad achachha hota hai। agar naashate ya bhojan ke baad paratidim ek kela khaate haim to yah mmsapeshiyom ko maroड़ se duur rakhega aur khimchaav se raahat degaa। 5. garam paid se sikaae (Hot pad)- ek samay isa tha jab log garam paanee ko paid par daalakar phir esatemaal karate the aur shareer par lagaakar sabhee parakaar ke darad se duur rahate the। lekin ab baaज़aar mem bijalee se chalane vaale garam paid maujuud haim। en paid se sikaae karane se mmsapeshiyom ka khimchaav duur hota hai aur darad se raahat milatee hai। 6. maalish (Massage)- parabhaavit hisase kee maalish karama bhee behad raahat deta hai। kisee bhee tel ko thoड़a gonagoma karake, usamem lahason kee kochh kaliym daalem। kochh der es tel ko aur garam karem aur gonagona rahane par parabhaavit hisase kee halake haathom se maalish karem। kochh hee der mem pairom mem khimchaav kam hoga aur darad mem bhee araam milegaa। Disease: niman rakatachaap ya lo baladapareshar (Low Blood Pressure) Description: niman rakatachaap ya lo baladapareshar (Low Blood Pressure) lo baladapareshar ya nimam rakatachaapa, ऑkaseejan (oxygen) ko dimaag tak jaane se rokata hai। keval ऑkaseejan hee nahee balaki anay poshak tatav bhee dimaag tak naheem pahomch paate। baladapareshar ko savaasathay kee bhaasha mem haaepotemshan (hypotemsion) ke naam se jaamate haim। yuum to lo baladapareshar koe beemaaree naheem hotee lekin yah shareer mem panap rahee anay gmbheer beemaaree ka smket hotee hai। ise mem jab kisee ke shareer mem rakata-paravaah saamaanay se kam ho jaata hai to use niman rakatachaap ya lo balad pareshar kahate hai। naaramal balad pareshar 120/80 hota hai। ise mem dila, kidanee, phephaड़e aur dimaag mshik ruup se ya puuree tarah se kaam karana bhee bmd kar sakate haim। Symptoms: - mkhom ke age mdhera chhaana - ulatee aur daayariya - garadan ka low blood pressure) 1. dil kee beemaaree (heart disease)- baladapareshar kam homa dil kee gmbheer beemaaree se joड़a hota hai, dil kee beemaaree se haarat kee mmsapeshiym kamajor ho jaatee haim, jisase haarat parayaapat khuun ko pamap naheem kar paata aur hamaara beepee lo rahane lagata hai। dil ke mareejom aur eneemiya ke rogee lo beepee ko lekar saavadhaan rahem। 2. arathosatetik haaeparatemshan taaep (arthostetic hypertension type)- esamem mareej ko khaड़e hone par chakakar ate haim, kayomki usaka balad pareshar ekadam se 20 paॉemt neeche  jaata hai। yah naravas sisatam par adhaarit hota hai। lekin kae baar davaaom ke saaed ephekat se ya elarajee se bhee ho sakatee hai। 3. khuum kee kamee tatha anay ka (less blood and other reasom)- shareer ke mdaruunee mgom se khuun bah jaane ya khuun kee kamee se, khaane mem paushatikata kee kamee ya aniyamitata se, phephaड़om ke ataik se, haarat ka vaॉlav kharaab ho jaame se, lo beepee ho sakata hai। achaamak sadama lagane, koe bhayaavah daृshay dekhane ya khabar sonane se bhee lo beepee ho sakata hai। esake alaava (other reason & causes of low blood pressure) - garabhaavasathaa, haaramon asmtolan jaise ki thaayaraॉed kee sakariyata kam ho jaana - balad shogar davaaom ke parabhaav se - satarok tatha leevar smbmdhee beemaariym - kochh avashayak vitaamin jaise bee12 aur ayaran kee kamee Treatments: baladapareshar lo hai to kaya karem (some tips to prevent low blood pressure) - tormt baith ya let jaaem, motathiym bheemchem, bmdhem, kholem, pair hilaayem। - namak aur cheenee vaala paanee ya chaay peeem। pairom ke meeche do takie lagaakar letem। - jo log pahale se haae beepee kee dava kha rahe haim, ve dava khaana bmd kar dem। - kam se kam ath gilaas paanee aur anay pey roj peeem। - bhojan mem kaarabohaaedaret kee maatara kam kar dem। - en sab ke alaava toranat daॉkataree salaah lem। Home Remedies: - niman rakatachaap se peeड़it log namak jayaada khaaem - lagaataar chakakar  rahe hom, to paanee jayaada peeem - ek kap shakarakmd ka juus din mem do baar peeem - mitatee ke baratan mem raatabhar kishamish bhigaakar rakhem। sobah kishamish chabaakar khaaem aur paanee pee lem - sobah khaalee pet tolasee ke patate ke ras mem shahad milaakar khaaem - raat mem baadaam bhigaakar rakhem, sobah en baadaam ke chhilake utaarakar pees lem aur duudh ke saath ubaalem। es duudh ko gonagoma peeem। Disease: saphed baala- gare heyar (Grey Hair) Description: saphed baala- gare heyar (Grey hair) umar ke saath baalom ka saphed hona paraakaृtik hai lekin kae baar kam umar mem hee baal saphed hone lagate haim। isa kae baar haaramonal gaड़baड़ee, badalatee laaephasataael aur paraduushaण vaale maahaul ke kaaraण bhee ho sakata hai। maujuuda samay mem teenej mem hee bachachom ke baal saphed hone lagate haim। Symptoms: - umar se pahale baal saphed ho jaana - baal naajok hona - baal patale ho jaana - baalom ka tekasachar ख़raab hona Reasons: kaaraण- (Cause of Grey Hair) melaanin ke adhaar par hee baalom ka rmg kaalaa, saphed ya bhuura hota hai। jinake baalom mem melaanin kee kamee hotee hai unake baalom ka rmg halaka hota hai jinake baalom mem melaanin jayaada hota hai unake baal kaale hote haim। jin logom ke baal saphed ho jaate haim unake baalom mem melaanin khatam ho jaata hai। melaanin pigamemt baalom ke phaॉleekal mem rahata hai। kochh maamalom mem thaॉeraaeda, ameemiya ya anovmshik kaaraणom se bhee baal saphed ho sakate haim। baal saफ़ed hone ke anay kaaraण (Other Reasons & Causes of Gray Hair) - vitaamin bee, ayaran aur kaॉpar tatha ayodeen jaise tatavom kee kamee se baal saphed hote haim। jin logom ke khaane mem em minaral kee kamee hotee hai unake baal samay se pahale saphed hone lagate haim। - ise vayakati jo bahot jayaada gosasail hote haim ya bahot jaladee tanaav mem ate unake baal bhee jaladee saphed home lagate haim। - kochh vayakatiyom mem umar se pahale baalom ka saphed hona anovmshik hota hai। - bahot lmbe samay tak kisee beemaaree se peeड़it rahane ya jaladee jaladee beemaar paड़ne vaale logom ke baal bhee umar se pahale saphed hone lagate haim। - baalom kee dekhabhaal theek parakaar se n kee jaae ya baalom kee saphaae ka dhayaan n rakha jaae to bhee baal umar se pahale saphed hone lagate haim। - bahot jayaada rasaayan vaale shaimpuu ya baalom ke utapaad jaise ki heyar kalar ya jel adi esatemaal karane vaale logom ke baal bhee jaladee saphed hone lagate haim। - bahot jayaada paraduushaण vaale maahaul ya dhuup mem rahame se bhee baalom ka rmg uड़ne lagata hai। Treatments: baalom ko kaala karame ke lie upachaar (Tips & Remedies to prevent gray hair) - kachache papeete ka pesat sir par takareeban 10 minat lagaakar rakhem। isa karane se kochh hee dinom mem baalom ka jhaड़na ruukega saath hee baal kaale bhee homge। etana hee naheem baalom se demdaraph bhee khatam hogaa। - baal dhone ke lie kemikal shaimpuu ka esatemaal bmd karem, esakee jagah besam aur duudh ya dahee ka esatemaal karem। isa karane se baalom ka paraakaृtik rmg bana rahegaa। - baal dhone ke lie mvala paaudar aur neembuu ka esatemaal karem। shikaakaae aur reetha milaakar ghar par hee shaimpuu bhee banaaya ja sakata hai। - sir mem laal payaaj ko peesakar usaka ras lagaaem। isa karane se bhee saphed baal kaale home lagate haim saath hee baalom ka jhaड़na bhee bmd ho jaata hai। - dahee mem kaalee mirach aur neembuu ka ras milaakar sir kee tavacha aur baalom par lagaaem। takareeban adhe ghmte baad baal dho dem, isa karane se baal kaale hone lagemge। - desee ghee bhee saphed baalom ko kaala karane ka saral upaay hai। tel kee jagah desee ghee se baalom kee masaaj karem। - mvale ka parayog khaane mem bhee karem। mvala khaane se bhee baal kaale hote haim। Home Remedies: ajakal umar se pahale hee baalom ka pakana ya saphed hona am samasaya bamatee ja rahee hai। baalom kee theek se dekhabhaal n ho paane aur paraduushaण ke kaaraण, hamaare baal asamay hee saphed ho jaate haim। baalom ko kalar karana es samasaya ka koe upachaar naheem hai lekin kochh ghareluu upachaar ajamaakar ap apane baalom ko saphed hone se rok sakate haim। jaanie saphed baalom ko kaala karane ke ghareluu nosakhe (Home Remedies for Grey Hair) 1. payaaj ka ras (Onion juice)- kochh dimom taka, nahaane se 1/2 ghmta pahale rojaana sir mem payaaj ka pesat lagaaem। esase baal kaale hone lagemge। 2. kachacha papeeta (Raw papaya)- sapataah mem kam se kam 3 din das minat tak kachache papeete ka pesat sir mem lagaaem। esase baal naheem jhaड़emge aur kaale bhee hone lagemge। 3. maariyal tel (Coconut oil)- bhaृmgaraaj aur ashavagmdha kee jaड़em baalom ke lie varadaan maanee jaatee haim। enaka pesat naariyal ke tel ke saath baalom kee jaड़om mem lagaaem aur 1 ghmte baad gonagone paanee se achachhee tarah se baal dho lem। esase bhee baal kaale hote haim। 4. meembuu ka ras (Lemon jiuce)- neembuu ke ras mem mvala paaudar milaakar use sir par lagaane se bhee saphed baal kaale ho jaate haim। 5. desee ghee (Desi ghee)- paratidin shodadh ghee se sir kee maalish karane se bhee saphed baal kaale hote haim। 6. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ko kadaduukas kar shahad mem mila lem। ese baalom par kam se kam sapataah mem do baar niyamit ruup se lagaaem। baalom ka saफ़ed hona kam ho jaaegaa। 7. jaituun ka tel (Olive oil)- jaituum ke tel ko halaka garam karem। esamem 4 garaam kapuur milaakar es tel se maalish karem। esakee maalish se kochh hee samay mem ruusee khatam ho jaaegee aur baal bhee kaale rahemge। 8. mvala (Aamla)- mvale ke paaudar mem neembuu ka ras milaakar use niyamit ruup se lagaaem। shaimpuu ke baad mvala paaudar paanee mem gholakar lagaane se bhee baalom kee kmdeeshanimg hotee hai, aur baal bhee kaale hote haim। mvala kisee na kisee rop me sevam bhee avashay karate rahem। 9. til ka tel (Sesame oil)- saradiyom mem til adhik se adhik khaaem। til ka tel bhee baalom ko kaala karane mem madad karata hai। 10. kaalee mirach (Black pepper)- adha kap dahee mem chotakee bhar kaalee mirach aur chamamach bhar neembuu ras milaakar baalom mem lagaae। 15 minat baad baal dho lem। saphed baal phir se kaale hone lagemge। 11. memhadee (Henma)- lohe kee kaड़aahee mem ek katoree mehmdee paaudara, do baड़e chamamach chaay ka paanee, do chamamach mvala paaudara, ek chamamach neembuu ka rasa, do chamamach dahee, shikaakaae v reetha paaudara, ek mda (agar ap lena chaahem to), adha chamamach naariyal tel v thoड़aa-sa katatha daalakar raat ko bhigo dem। ese sobah baalom mem lagaaem, phir do ghmte baad dho lem। esase baal bina kisee nokasaan ke kaale ho jaaenge। isa maah mem kam se kam ek baar avashay karem। Disease: hadadee pharaikachar ya hadadee ka khisakana (Bone Fracture Or Dislocation) Description: hadadee pharaikachar ya hadadee ka khisakana (Bone fracture or dislocation) pharaikachar (Fracture)- hadadee ka tuutana hee hadadee ka pharaikachar kahalaata hai। hadadee kae kaaraणom se tuut sakatee hai, kaheem girane se, takakar lagane se, jhataka lagane se ya achaanak se dabaav paड़ne para। hadadee ka khisakana (Dislocation of bone) - do hadadiym jab joड़e hoe sathaan se khisak jaatee haim to ese disalokeshan ya hadadee ka khisakana kahate haim। do hadadiym ek joड़ par jaakar milatee haim, lekin es joड़ par chot lagane ke kaaraण esee joड़ se hadadiym khisak jaatee haim। hadadiyom ke khisakane par bhee bahot darad hota hai aur smbmdhit sathaam par suujan  jaatee hai। Symptoms: - asahaneey tarah se darad hona - asa-paas kee tmtarikaaom mem kashati ke kaaraण akaड़n - pharaikachar kee jagah par suujan  jaana - pharaikachar ke asa-paas ke utakom mem asathirata - pharaikachar vaale sathaan ka puuree tarah se kaam bmd kar dema - behosh hona Reasons: kaaraण- (Causes of bone frtacture or dislocatiom) pharaikachar ke kae kaaraण ho sakate haim। hadadiyom ke kamajor hone ya hadadiyom se smbmdhit kaimsara, sisata, ऑsatiyoporosis adi hone se। pharaikachar ke baad hadadee mem darad ke bhee kae kaaraण ho sakate haim- - hadadiyom ke asa-paas ke narav edimgasa, jo hadadee ke tuutane par sakariy hokar dimaag ko darad ka smket dete haim। - hadadiym tuutane se rakatasataraav ka hona aur suujan anaa, jisase darad hota hai। - pharaikachar hone par mmsapeshiym sikoड़ kar hadadee ko bachaane kee koshish karatee haim, yah bhee darad ka kaaraण hota hai। - isee koe doraghatana home par jisase hadadiym parabhaavit hom। - hadadiyom ka pharaikachar vayakati kee umar par bhee nirabhar karata hai kayomki jayaada umar mem pharaikachar ke chmses baढ़ jaate haim। kochh sathitiyom mem asahaneey darad bhee ho sakata hai jaise- - smkaramaण hone par - galat tareeke se palaasatar lagaame para, bahot dheela ya bahot taaet Treatments: upachaara- (Tips to prevent bone fracture or dislocation) - pharaikachar vaalee jagah kee baraph se sikaae karem। suujan kam hogee aur darad se araam milegaa। - peeड़it vayakati ko puuree tarah araam karana chaahie। smbhav ho to smbmdhit jagah ko hilaane-dolaane se bachem। - garam sikaae karane se bhee araam milata hai। - yadi haath ya pair kee hadadee tuutee ho to use omchaae par karake rakhem। - pharaikachar vaale sathaan ke asa-paas kee jagah par maalish karem। - adha anaamaas roj khaaem। - red meet khaane se bachem। - parijaravetiv khaana n khaaem। saavadhaaniym- (Precautions) - kaar mem baithakar hamesha seet belat pahanem। - koe khel khelate samay ya saaekil aur motarasaaekil chalaate samaya, smbmdhit sephatee upakaraण jaruur pahanem। - yadi kisee ko ऑsateeporosis hai, to niyamit vayaayaam karem aur hadadiyom ko majabuut karane vaalee daaet lem। Disease: chikan paॉkasa- chechak (Chickenpox) Description: chikan paॉkasa- chechak (Chickenpox) chechak ek vaayaral smkaramaण (viral infection) hai jisase shareer par chhaale kee tarah daane banate haim aur unamem khojalee (itching) hotee hai। chechak ise logom ko jayaada hota hai jo beemaar n paड़te hom ya jimahomne chechak se bachane ke lie teekaakaraण n karavaaya ho। pahale ke samay mem yova hone tak har koe chechak rog se ek n ek baar jaruur parabhaavit hota tha lekin aj ke samay mem es tarah ke rogom mem kamee ae hai। jayaadaatar logom ke lie, chechak ek halakee beemaaree hai। phir bhee, yah teeka lagaaya jaana behatar hai। chechak ke teeke chechak aur usakee smbhaavit jatilataaom ko rokane ke lie ek sorakashit aur parabhaavee tareeka hai। Symptoms: - thakaan (kamajoree) mahasuus hona - bokhaara, siradarad - bhuukh mem kamee - shareer par laala-golaabee, chhote daanom ka ubharana Reasoms: kim logom ko hota hai adhik khataraa? (Risk Factors of Chicken Pox) chechak atayadhik smkaramit hotee hai, aur yah tejee se phail sakatee hai। vaayaras ke daame ke saath seedhe smparak mem ane se ya khmsane ya chheemkane se hava mem baikateeriya phailane se duusarom ko ho sakatee hai। chechak (chechak) ka khatara tab aur adhik hota hai jaba: - kisee ko kabhee chechak n hoe ho। - chechak ke lie teekaakaraण n karavaaya ho। - bachache jo sakuul ya haॉsatal mem smkaramaण se parabhaavit hoe hom। Treatments: upachaar (Treatments of Chicken Pox) - ek chamamach bekimg soda (baking soda) ko ek gilaas paanee mem gholakara, es paanee ko ruue kee sahaayata se shareer par lagaaem। chechak se mijaat milegee। - chechak ke dauraan hone vaalee khojalee se bachame ke lie otameel (oatmeal) ko paanee mem daalakar nahaaem। - chechak (chechak) se hone vaalee khojalee se bachane ke lie kailaamaaen loshan (calamine lotion) ko daanom ke opar lagaaem। - din mem do se teen baar parabhaavit sathaan par shahad lagaaem। - chechak ko jaladee theek karane ke lie gaajar aur hare dhaniya ka suup bamaakar peeem। - chmdan ke tel mem ruue bhigaakara, parabhaavit sathaam par lagaaem। - haree matar ko ubaalakar usaka pesat banaakara, daanom par lagaaem, araam milegaa। - elovera ka taaja ras nikaalakar daanom par lagaaem। tipas (Tips for Chicken Pox) - yadi chechak ke saath bokhaar bhee hai to khuub pey padaarath peeem। paanee, juus aur suup samay samay par lete rahem। yadi bachacha smkaramit mm ka duudh peeta ho, to mm ko duudh naheem pilaama chaahie। - daanom ko n khojalaaem aur haathom ke naakhuum chhote rakhem। raat mem sote samay khojalaane se bachane ke lie haathom par galavas (gloves) pahanem। - khojalee se bachane ke lie shareer ko thmda rakhem। halake kapaड़e pahamem aur garam paanee se nahaane se bachem। - es baat ka bhee dhayaan rakhem ki smkaramaण ghar ke duusarom sadasayom tak m phaile। smkaramit vayakati ke kapaड़e, bisatar adi duur rakhem aur umahem ghar ke anay sadasayom ke kapaड़om se alag hee dhoem। Home Remedies: shareer mem tejee se khojalee honaa, laal daane nikal ana chikan paॉkas ya chechak (Chickem pox) ke paramokh lakashaण haim। 1 varash se lekar 10 varash tak ke bachachom mem chikan paॉkas ka khatara jayaada hota hai। khaana-paan mem hoe aniyamitata chikan paॉkas ke phailane ka paramokh kaaraण hotee hai। es dauraan naakhuun se chakatatom ko hataane kee koshish naheem karanee chaahie, isa karane se yah phailata hai। chechak (Chechak) ke samay khaana-paan ka uchit dhayaan rakhana chaahie। masaaledaar aur ऑyalee khaana khaane se bachem। chikanapaॉkas ke kisee mareej ko kabhee esaparim naheem denee chaahie। esase usakee haalat kharaab ho sakatee hai। chikan paॉkas hone par baahar aur bheeड़ vaalee jagah par jaane se parahej karem। ho sake to es dauraan logom se duur rahem। jaanie chikan paॉkas se bachaav ke ghareluu nosakhe (Home Remedies for Chicken pox) niman upachaarom ko apanaakar es beemaaree se raahat paae ja sakatee hai: 1. jae ka ata (Oat Flour)- chikan paॉkas hone par shareer mem bahot tej khojalee hotee hai। khojalee se bachane ke lie jae ke ate ko paanee mem milaakar sanaan karana chaahie। 2 leetar paanee mem 2 kap jae ka ata milaakar lagabhag 15 minat tak ubaalem, pake ate ko ek kaॉtan ke baig mem achachhee tarah se bmdhakar baॉth tab mem daalakar mahaaem। 2. bhuura siraka (Brown Vinegar)- adha kap bhuure sirake ko paanee mem daalakar nahaane se shareer mem ho rahee khojalee se nijaat paayee ja sakatee hai। esase daanom kee suujan kam hotee hai aur daane suukhame bhee lagate haim। 3. neembuu ka ras (Lemon Juice)- neembuu ka ras peene se chikan paॉkas mem raahat milatee hai। upachaar ke lie samay samay par ek gilaas saaph paanee mem neembuu nichoड़kar peete rahem। 4. meem kee patatiym (Margos Leaves)- neem kee patatiyom ko garam paanee mem daalakar nahaane se khojalee samaapat hotee hai। neem paraakaृtik ruup se emtee baikateeriyal goणom se bharapuur hota hai। ise mem chikan paॉkas theek karane mem behad phaayademmd hai। 5. bekimg soda (Baking Soda)- adha chamamach bekimg soda ko ek gilaas gonagone paanee mem milaaem aur es lep ko puure shareer par lagaakar suukhane dem। esase chikanapaॉkas jalad theek ho jaata hai। 6. seb ka siraka (Apple Cider Vinegar)- adha kap seb ke sirake ko halake garam paanee mem milaakar nahaame se raahat milatee hai। es paamee mem takareeban 20 minat tak jaruur baithem। 7. vitaamin e tel (Vitamin E Oil)- vitaamina-e yokat tel ko shareer par lagaane se chikam paॉkas ke dauraan hone vaalee khojalee se raahat milatee hai। 8. gaajar (Carrot)- ubale gaajar aur dhaniya khaane se chikan paॉkas se ae kamajoree kam hotee hai। gaajar aur dhaniya ka suup banaakar peene se raahat milatee hai। 9. harabal chaay (Herbal Tea)- tolasee, gemda aur kaimomaael ko milaakar chaay bamaaee phir usamem shahad ya neembuu milaakar peejie। es chaay ko din mem 3-4 baar peene se raahat milatee hai। 10. haree matar (Green Pea)- haree matar ko paanee mem pakaakar esake paanee ko shareer mem lagaaee, esase chikan paॉkas ke laal chakatate samaapat hote haim। 11. adarak (Ginger)- baath tab mem thmda paanee lem aur usamem adarak daalakar tees minat tak chhoड़ dem। usake baad es paamee mem baith jaaem। esase chikanapaॉkas ke dauraam hone vaalee khojalee mem araam milata hai। Disease: haija (Cholera) Description: haija (Cholera) haija ek smkaraamak beemaaree (infectious disease) hai, jo mtom ko parabhaavit karatee hai aur jisamem paanee kee tarah patale dasat lag jaate haim। haija ka elaaj samay rahate n kiya jaae to vayakati mem paanee kee kamee (dehydration) ho jaatee hai, jisase vayakati kee maut bhee ho sakatee hai। haija duushit paanee peene ya duushit khaana khaane ke kaaraण phailata hai। isa paanee ya khaana jisamem vaaebariyo koleree baikateeriya (vibrio cholerae becteria) maujuud ho, haija ka kaaraण banata hai। haija (Haija) isee jagah par jayaada phailata hai jahm, saaph saphaae ka abhaav ho, seevarayokat paanee kee sapalaae ho, saaga-sabajee seevar ke paanee mem ugaae ja rahee hom ya kisee ka ghar naale adi ke paas sathit ho। haijaa, bachachom se lekar bojoragom taka, kisee mem bhee ho sakata hai। garabhavatee mahilaaom tatha bachachom mem bhee es rog ke hone kee ashmka jayaada rahatee hai kayomki unakee paratirodhak kashamata kam hotee hai। haija mem vayakati ke shareer se paanee ke saath kae jaruuree lavaण, sodiyam aur poteshiyam adi bhee nikal jaate haim, jisase vayakati ke shareer ka rakat amaleey ho jaata hai aur vayakati kee maृtayo ho jaatee hai। Symptoms: - dasat ekadam patale aur chaaval ke paanee jaise hona - dasat ke saath ulatiym hona - parabhaavit vayakati ko atayadhik payaas lagana - parabhaavit vayakati ko peshaab kam ama - shareer kee mms peshiyom mem imthan homa Reasons: haija ka kaaraण (Causes of Choler in Hindi) 1- duushit paanee, bhojana, phal ya duudh adi ka parayog karane se। 2- rogee vayakati ke smparak mem rahane se, masalana, usake saath khaane, uthane-baithane, usake davaara esatemaal kie gae kapaड़e pahanane, usake davaara esatemaal kie gae kisee bhee saamaan ko esatemaal karane se। 3- makakhiym bhee haija (Haija) phailame ka baड़a kaaraण haim। khole mem kee gae shauch ya gmdagee par baithakar makakhiym baikateeriya lekar duusaree jagahom par phaila detee haim, jisase haija phailata hai। 4- khaane ko bina dhake rakhanaa, aur use khaanaa। 5- paanee ko bina dhake rakhanaa। 6- kachacha ya adhapaka bhojana, khaasakar mms khaanaa। Treatmemts: upachaar (Treatment of Cholera) haija ka elaaj karane se pahale rogee ko saapha-saphaae ka vishesh dhayaan rakhana haahie। haija akasar saapha-saphaae kee kamee ke kaaraण bhee phailata hai। haija hone par niman upaay apanaane chaahie: - duushit bhojana, paanee ya kisee anay khaaday padaarath ka esatemaal n karem - baasee bhojan n karem - paratayek khaaday padaarath aur paanee ko hamesha dhak kar rakhem - shareer mem paanee kee kamee n home dem। - beemaaree ho rahee ho to neembuu kee shikmjee, dahee, chhaachha, paanee tatha oaraes adi peete rahem - yadi vayakati ke dasat aur ulatee n ruuk rahe hom, to use tormt asapataal le jaaem - paratayek vayakati ko haija (Haija) se smbmdhit teeka jaruur lagavaana chaahie - rogee ke esatemaal se smbmdhit har cheej ko duusare logom se alag rakhem - paanee mem phimaael daalakar pharash ko saaph karem, isa karame se keetaaणo mar jaate haim। Home Remedies: pey padaarath kee maatara baढ़aayem। paanee, neembuu paanee, chhaachh adi peete rahem। ghar par oaraes taiyaar karem, esake lie chaar kap paanee mem chhah chhote chamamach cheenee aur adhee chhotee chamamach namak milaaem aur jitana jayaada pee sakem, peeem। dahee mem kela milaakar khaaem। adarak ko kadaduukas karake shahad ke saath milaakar khaaem। yadi shauch mem khuun ke dhababe  rahe hom to adarak n khaaem। ek gilaas paanee mem shahada, neembuu aur namak milaakar piyem। 10 se 20 mileegaraam jimk kee jaruurat roj hotee hai, ise mem jimk ke sapaleememt lem। payaaj aur kaalee mirach ko peesakar pesat banaaem। ese dim mem teen baar ek haphate ke lie khaaem। laumg daalakar paanee ko ubaalem aur chhaanakara, es paanee ko peeem। dahee mem methee paaudar aur jeera paaudar daalakar khaaem। neembuu ke ras mem kachachee haladee kee jaड़em 2 ghmte ke lie bhiga kar rakhem aur baad mem peesakar ek kmtenar mem rakh lem। ek kap paanee mem es pesat kee kochh maatara ko paanee aur shahad milaakar peeem। Disease: jaraman meejalas ya ruubela (German Measles) Description: jaraman meejalas ya ruubela (German measles) naaka, sms kee nalee aur phephaड़om se smbmdhit smkaramaण ko ruubela kahate haim। yah ek tarah ka khasara hai jise ruubiyola ya jaraman meejalas ke naam se bhee jaana jaata hai। yah behad smkaramit hota hai aur tejee se ek vayakati se duusare vayakati mem phail jaata hai। smkaramit vayakati ke smparak mem ane se yah tejee se duusare vayakati ko bhee smkamit kar deta hai। Symptoms: - gaal ke mdar neele ya bhuure dhababe najar ana - jalan ke saath laal mkhem - naak ka bmd hona - nirmtar khmsee bane rahanaa, - mmsapeshiyom mem imthan aur akaड़n mahasuus hona - sir darad honaa, - shareer par laala-golaabee, chhote daanom ka ubharama - bokhaar Reasons: kaaraण aur jatilataaem- (Cause and Complications of German Measles) ruubela ka kaaraण, smkaramit vayakati ke smparak mem ana hee hai। smkamit vayakati ke khmsane aur chheemkane se rog ke jeevaaणo hava mem tairane lagate haim aur esake smparak mem ane vaale kisee bhee vayakati ko parabhaavit kar sakate haim। chhote bachache, garabhavatee mahilaaem ya isa koe bhee vayakati jisakee emayuunitee kam ho, ruubela ka shikaar ho sakata hai। ruubela se peeड़it vayakati mem kae jatilataaem bhee ho sakatee haim, khaasakar garabhavatee mahila ke shisho mem- - motiyaabimd - baharaapan - shareer ke kae mgom mem diphekat - maanasik ruup se kamajoree - saamaanay shaareerik vikaas n hona - umgaliyom aur ghotanom mem aratharaaetis ke lakashaण ana Treatments: tipas (Tips to Prevent German Measles) - shareer ko puuree tarah se araam dem। - dosatom, sahakaramiyom, khaasakar garabhavatee mahilaaom ko apanee beemaaree ke baare mem bataaem aur khod se duur rahame kee salaah dem। - ise logom se bhee duur rahem jinakee emayuunitee kamajor ho। - smkaramit vayakati apane esatemaal kee sabhee cheejem duusare logom se duur rakhe। - duusare logom ko smkaramit vayakati ke smparak se bachana chaahie। saath hee rogee ko khod bhee es smbmdh mem saavadhaanee rakhamee chaahie। upachaar (Treatment of German measles) paanee mem neembuu daalakar peeem। naariyal ka paanee peeem। likoresee kee jaड़ ke paaudar mem shahad milaakar rogee ko chataaem। neem kee patatiyom ko daalakar paanee garam karem, es paanee se smkaramit vayakati ko sanaan karaaem। lahason kee kaliyom ko peesakar usamem shahad milaakara, rogee ko chataaem। mvala paaudar ko paanee ke saath milaakara, es paanee se shareer pomchhe। jau ke paanee mem baadaam ke tel kee kochh buumde daalakar peeem। dhayaan rakhane yogay baatem (Precautions for german measles) - rogee ko ekmt kamare mem rakhem, jahm ghar ke anay sadasay kam jaate hom। - rogee ko garam paanee peene ko dete rahem। khaasakar sobah khaalee pet jaruur garam paanee peeme ko dem। - rogee ko samaya-samay par tarah tarah ke juus peeme ko dem। - emayuunitee baढ़aane vaala khaanaa, phal aur sabajiym khaane ko dem। - rogee ko suuraj kee roshanee se bacha ke rakhem। - duudh ya duudh se bane anay khaaday padaarath rogee ko n dem। - rogee ka kamara hamesha saaph aur havaadaar rakhem। Disease: enaphaluuemja (Influenza) Description: enaphaluuemja (Influenza) enaphaluuemja ko saadhaaraण bhaasha mem phaluu (flu) ke naam se jaana jaata hai, jisamem shavasan tmtar mem smkaramaण (infection in respiratory system) ho jaata hai। es tarah ka phaluu adhikatar saradiyom ke mausam mem vaayaral beemaaree ke ruup mem hota hai। yah un logom ko jayaada parabhaavit karata hai jinakee rog paratirodhak kashamata kisee beemaaree ke kaaraण kam hoe ho। Symptoms: - asaamaanay thakaan mahasuus homa। - kaph - chakakar ana - chheemk ana - thmd ke saath bokhaar anaa, - tavacha ka meela paड़na - naak bahana hona - pet ya chhaatee par dabaav mahasuus hona aur darad hona - mareej par behoshee haavee ho - mmsapeshiyom mem darad - sms phuulana - sms leme mem kathinaae - siradarad hona - ulatee Reasons: kaaraण (Reasons of Influenza) enaphaluuemja naam ke vaayaras se hee yah rog phailata hai। phaluu ka vaayaras naaka, mkh aur momh kee masakas membaren ke davaara shareer mem paravesh karata hai। har baar jab bhee enamem se kisee bhee mg ko haath lagaaya jaata haim, vayakati khod ko khod hee phaluu ke jeevaaणo se smkaramit karata hai। phaluu teem parakaar ka hota hai, e, bee aur see। taaep e aur bee vaarashik enaphaluuemja ka kaaraण hote haim jisase lagabhag 20 pheesadee log parabhaavit hote haim। taaep e mem echa1ema1, echa2ena2 aur echa3ena3 shaamil haim। taaep e ke emphaluuemja mem parivaratan hota hai jisase parabhaavit vayakati ko parayaapat emayuunitee naheem mil paatee। taaep see bhee phaluu ke lakashaण darashaata hai lekin es tarah ka phaluu kam hota hai। haalmki teenom tarah ka phaluu ek hee tarah se phailata hai aur enake lakashaण bhee ek jaise hee hote haim। jatilataaem- (Complicatioms during influenza) - yovaa, bachachom tatha 65 kee umar se adhik ke bojoragom mem jatilata ho sakatee hai। - garabhavatee mahilaaom ko bhee phaluu ka khatara jayaada rahata hai। - emphaluuemja se nimoniyaa, kaan mem smkaramaण, saaenas smkaramaण aur baromkaaetis ka khatara baढ़ jaata hai। - yadi uchach shareणee ka phaluu ho to, emteevaayaral davaaem upayokat rahatee haim, anayatha vayakati kee maut bhee ho sakatee hai। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Influenza) - garam paanee mem neembuu daalakar peeem - thmda aur baasee khaana n khaaem - logom se haath n milaaem - paanee se bheegane ke baad shareer ko achachhee tarah sokhaaem - paratidin vayaayaam karem - shareer kee rog paratirodhak kashamata baढ़aane vaale khaaday padaarathom ka sevan karem - garabhavatee mahilaaem aur bachachom ko peene ka paamee ubaalakar dem - ashavagmdha aur kaalamegh jaisee jaड़ee buutiym shareer ka taapamaan kam karane mem madad karatee haim - paanee mem ajavaayan daalakar ubaal lem। paamee tak tak ubaalem jab tak adha n rah jaae, es paanee ko samas samay par peete rahem। tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Influenza) - shareer ko puuree tarah araam dem - naak ko samaya-samay par saaph karate rahem - garam paanee kee botal ya heetimg paid se sikaae karem - bina haath dhoe kabhee khaana n khaaem - jayaada se jayaada taral padaarath lem, suupa, neembuu paanee adi peete rahem Disease: meninajaaetis (Memingitis) Description: meninajaaetis (Menimgitis) meninajaaetis ko dimaagee bokhaar (Dimagi Bukhar) bhee kahate haim। yah amataur par vaayarasa, baikateeriyaa, kavaka, parajeevee, aur kochh jeevom ke smkaramaण ke kaaraण hota hai। shaareerik dosh ya kamajor paratirakasha paraणaalee ko avaratak baikateeriyal meninajaaetis se joड़a ja sakata hai। yah ek tarah ka emphekashan hota hai jo mashatishak aur reeढ़ kee hadadee kee rakasha karane vaale membaren mem suujan paida kar deta hai। adhikmsh maamalom mem esaka kaaraण vaayaras hota hai। haalmki, dimaagee bokhaar ke kochh gaira-smkaraamak kaaraण bhee maujuud haim। Symptoms: - chhote bachachom mem, niman lakashaणom par gaur karana chaahie- (symptoms in toddlers) - bahot tej ya karaah kar rona - tej ya asaamaanay smse - peela ya daamom vaala chehara - laal ya baimganee rmg ke dhababe - baड़e bachachom mem, niman lakashaणom ko dekhana chaahie- (symptoms in younger children) - garadan mem akaड़n - peeth aur joड़om mem gmbheer darad - bahot tej sir darad - chamakadaar roshanee se chiढ़ hona - bahot thmde haath aur pair - kmpana - tejee se sns lena - mmsapeshiyom mem darad - haathom aur pairom ka thmda hona - bokhaar - siradarad - ulatee Reasons: dimaagee bokhaar ke kaaraण (Causes of Meningitis) meninajaaetis mem baikateeriya baladasatareem mem paravesh karake dimaag aur sapaaen kaॉrad mem chala jaata hai। kae baar jokaam ya saaenas kee samasaya hone se bhee yah baikateeriya naak aur momh ke davaara shareer mem paravesh kar jaate haim aur dimaag mem suujan paida kar dete haim। dimaagee bokhaar (Dimagi Bukhar) ka emteebaayotik davaaom se elaaj kiya ja sakata hai। meninajaaetis ko jmchane ke lie galaas tesat bhee kiya ja sakata hai। galaas tesata- yadi kmch ke gilaas ke kimaare ko shareer ke opar hoe dhababom par dabaaya jaae to yah phed naheem hote। yah meninagokokakal sepateekaamiya (menimgococcal septicaemia) ka lakashaण hota hai। es avasatha se peeड़it vayakati ke shareer par golaabee rmg ke daane ho jaate haim jo baad mem baimganee rmg ke baड़e daanom mem tabadeel ho jaate haim। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Meningitis or Dimagi Bukhar) - shareer ko puuree tarah araam dem। - rogee ko mdhere aur shmt kamare mem rakhem। - likavid phuud n lem। oaraes ka ghol garam paanee mem lem। - rogee ko anaar ka juus dem aur lahason ka sevan bhee karavaayem। - shareer ke taapamaan ko kam karane ke lie baraph ke tokaड़om ko kapaड़e mem lapetakar sikaae karem। - yadi rogee ko ulatee ho rahee hom, to use ek taraph karavat lekar litaayem jisase ulatee kee mahak use n ae। Disease: haarat balaॉkej (Heart Blockage) Description: haarat balaॉkej (Heart blockage) haarat balaॉkej mem manoshay kee dhaड़kam sochaaruu ruup se kaam karana bmd kar detee haim। es dauraam dhaड़kan ruuk ruuk kar chalatee hai। kochh logom me yah samasaya janam ke saath se hee shoruu ho jaatee hai jabaki kochh logom mem baड़e hone par samasaya vikasit hotee hai। janamajaat balaॉkej kee samasaya ko konagenital haarat balaॉkej (comgenital heart blockage) jabaki baad mem hoe samasaya ko ekavaayarad haarat balaॉkej (acquired heart blockage) kahate haim। adhonik rahana-sahan aur khaane-peene kee adatom ke chalate adhikmsh logom mem haarat balaॉkej kee samasaya am hotee ja rahee hai। haarat balaॉkej ko jmchane ke lie elekatarokaaradiyogaraam (electro cardiogram) tesat kiya jaata hai। Symptoms: - chhaatee mem darada, sms phuulama - jaladee thak jaana - siradarad hona - chakakar ana - behosh hona Reasons: balaॉkej ke kaaraण- (Cause of Heart Blockage) haarat mem balaॉkej ya ruukaavat palaॉk ke kaaraण hotee hai। palaॉkasa, kolesataraॉla, phaita, phaaebar tishayuu aur shavet rakat kaणikaaom ka misharaण hota hai, jo dheere dheere nasom kee deevaarom par chipak jaata hai। palaॉk ka jamaav gaaढ़epan aur usake toड़e jaane kee paravaृtati ko lekar alaga-alag tarah ke hote haim। agar yah gaaढ़aapan haarad hogaa, to ise palaॉk ko satebal kaha jaata hai aur yadi yah molaayam hoga to ese toड़e jaane ke amokuul maana jaata hai, aur ese anasatebal palaॉk kaha jaata hai। satebal palaॉk (Stable Plaque):- satebal palaॉk se ruukaavat kee maatara se koe pharak naheem paड़taa, n hee esase gmbheer haarat ataik hota hai। es tarah ka palaॉk dheere dheere baढ़ta hai, ise mem rakat paravaah ko nae aratareej (artries) ka raasata dhuumdhane ka mauka mil jaata hai, jise koletaral vesel (collateral vessal) kahate haim। ye vesel balaॉk ho chokee arataree ko baaepaas kar detee haim aur dil kee mmsapeshiyom tak avashayak rakat aur ऑkaseejan pahomchaatee haim। anasatebal palaॉk (Umstable Plaque):- asathaae palaॉk mem, palaॉk ke tuutane para, ek khataranaak thakaka ban jaata hai, aur koletaral ko vikasit hone ka puura samay naheem mil paata hai। vayakati kee mmsapeshiym (muscle) gmbheer ruup se daimej ho jaatee haim aur vah kae baar sadan kaaradiek deth (sudden cardiac death) ka shikaar ho jaata hai। Treatments: haarat balaॉkej se bachane ke lie saamaanay tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Heart Blockage) - dhuumarapaam n karem, yahm tak ki koe duusara dhuumarapaan kar raha ho, to bhee khod ko bachaayem। - haृday ko savasath rakhane ke lie dinacharaya mem vayaayaam ko shaamil karana behad jaruuree hai। - isa bhojan karem, jisase haृday ko laabh ho। - haृday ko savasath rakhane ke lie shareer ka vajan niymtarit rakhem। - roj adha ghmta paidal chalem। - liphat kee jagaha, seeढ़iyom ka esatemaal karem। Home Remedies: haarat balaॉkej ke ghareluu upachaara- (home remedies for heart blockage) ek kap duudh mem lahason kee teen se chaar kalee daalakar ubaalem। es duudh ko roj peeem। ek gilaas duudh mem haladee daalakar ubaalem aur gonagona rahane par shahad daalakar peeem। ek gilaas gonagone paanee mem neembuu ka rasa, kaalee mirach aur shahad daalakar peeem। do se teem kap adarak kee chaay rojaana peeem। esake lie paanee mem adarak daalakar ubaalem aur shahad milaakar peeem। methee daane ko raat bhar paamee mem bhigaakara, sobah methee chabaakar khaayem aur bacha ho paanee pee jaaem। khaame mem ya salaad mem alasee ke beejom ka esatemaal karem। khaame mem saamaanay chaaval kee jagah laal yeesat chaaval ka esatemaal karem। Disease: kaan mem smkaramaण (Ear Infection) Description: kaan mem smkaramaण (Ear Infection ) kaan shareer ke sabase mahatavapuuraण aur smvedamasheel mgom mem se ek haim। shareer ka yah ek isa hisasa hai jisaka dhayaan emsaan sabase kam rakhata hai। kaan mem smkaramaण akasar baikateeriyal ya vaayaral smkaramaण (Bacterial Viral Infection) ke kaaraण hota hai jo ki madhay kaan ko parabhaavit karata hai jisamem chhotee hadadiyom kee pahaaड़ee banee hotee hai। esee mem kaan ke parade ke peechhe hava se bharee jagah hotee hai। Symptoms: - kaan mem darad hona - chakakar ana - sir darad - bokhaar - sonaae kam deta hai Reasons: kaan mem smkaramaण kae jokhimom ko paida karata hai। smkaramaण agar jayaada mdar naheem gaya ho to kochh minat ke upachaar aur parakariyaaom ke davaara ese theek kiya ja sakata hai lekin yadi yah mtarik sathaan tak pahomch gaya hai tab ऑpareshan kee maubat bhee  sakatee hai। kaan mem smkaramaण hone ke kaaraण peeड़it ko nimam pareshaaniym ho sakatee hai: * saradarada: kaan ka darad akasar sar mem tanaav paida karata hai। * bokhaara: kaan mem darad ke kaaraण teevar darada, jalam aur bokhaar ho sakata hai। * chakakar anaa: kaam ka darad kae baar sir mem chakakar ane ka kaaraण ban jaate haim। * sonane kee kashamataa: yadi es emphekashan ko lmbe samay tak anadekha kiya jaae to kaan kee sonane kee shakati khatam ho sakatee hai। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Ear Infection in Hindi) kaan ke smkaramaण se bachane ke lie sabase jaruuree hai saapha-saphaae ka vishesh dhayaan rakhanaa। esake atirikat kochh niman baatem par amal kar bhee kaanom ke smkaramaण se bacha ja sakata hai। vaikas kee saphaae (Cleaning of the wax)- kaan mem atirikat vaikas kaan mem baikateeriya ko baढ़aakara, kaan mem smkaramaण paida karatee hai। kaan kee vaikas ko chikitasakom davaara suukasham upakaraणom se saaph karaaya ja sakata hai। amuuman log eyar bad se bhee kaan kee saphaae kar lete haim lekin yadi vekas jayaada hai to use eyar bad se saaph naheem kiya ja sakataa। eyar daraॉpas ka parayog (Use of Ear Drops)- kae dapha kaan kee dava daalane se bhee kaan ke smkaramaण se nijaat mil jaatee hai। chikitasak kaan darad ke lie eyar daraॉp dete haim jisase kaan ke darad ke saath hee vaikas bhee nikal jaatee hai। tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Ear Infection) - saradee jokaam mem achachhee tarah se haath dhone ke baad hee khaanaa-peena khaaem। - saradee jokaam mem baahar jaane se bachem। bheeड़ vaalee jagahom par smkaramaण ka khatara jayaada hota hai। - dhuumarapaan se bachem। - bachachom mem teekaakaraण samay se karavaaem। unahem nayuumokokal teeke jaruur lagavaaem। Home Remedies: ghareluu upaaya- (Home Remedies) 1- kaan mem darad ho to gaimde ke phuul ko peesakar usaka ras daalane se araam hota hai। 2- namak ko garam karake use kapaड़e mem bmdh kar kaan kee sikaae karane se bhee kaan ke darad se araam milata hai। 3- khaana banaane vaale tel mem lahason daalakar tel garam karem। es tel kee kochh buumde teen se chaar baar kaan mem daalem। 4- tolasee ke patatom ka ras mikaalakar kaam ke as paas malane se bhee araam hota hai। dhayaan rahe ras ko kaan ke mdar naheem daalana hai। 5- seb ke sirake mem baraabar maatara mem paanee milaakar ruue ko usamem bhigaaem। es ruue ko kaan ke peechhe kochh der lagaakar rakhem। 6- ऑliv ऑyal ko garam karake, gonagone tel kee kochh buumde kaam mem daalem। 7- garam paanee kee botal se kaan kee sikaae karem। 8- payaaj ko garam karake use mikasee mem peesakar ras nikaal lem। payaaj ke ras kee kochh buumde kaan mem daalem। Disease: daayabitik retimopaithee (Diabetic Retinopathy) Description: daayabitik retinopaithee (Diabetic retinopathy) daayabitik retinopaithee ek beemaaree hai, jo madhomeh (diabeties) se peeड़it vayakati kee retina (nkh ka parada jahm tasaveer banatee hai) ko parabhaavit karatee hai। yah retina ko rakat pahomchaane vaalee maheen nalikaaom ke kashatigarasat hone ke kaaraण hota hai, agar esaka samay par elaaja़ n karaaya jaae to peeड़it vayakati mdhepan ka shikaar ho sakata hai। daayabitik retinopaithee doniya mem mdhepan ka sabase baड़a kaaraण hai, jisake maamale har saal baढ़te ja rahe haim। Symptoms: - mkhom ka baara-baar smkaramit hona - chashame ka nmbar baara-baar badalana - retina se khuun ana - saphed motiyaabimd ya kaala motiyaabimd - siradarad rahama ya ekaaek mkhom kee roshanee kam ho jaana - sobah uthane ke baad kam dikhaae dena Reasoms: daayabitik retinopaithee ke kaaraण (Causes of Diabetic Retinopathy) madhomeh (Diabetes), yadi bahot lmbe samay tak rah jaae to yah shareer ke duusare mgom ko bhee parabhaavit karata hai aur yah parabhaavit mg mkhem bhee ho sakatee haim। daayabiteeja़ rakat vaahikaaom kee deevaar ko parabhaavit karata hai, jisase retima (jisapar chhavi banatee hai) tak ऑkaseejan le jaane vaalee naaड़iym kamaja़or ho jaatee haim। daayabiteeja़ ke mareeja़om mem agar shogar kee maatara niymtarit naheem rahatee, to vah daayabitik retinopaithee kee samasaya se garasat ho sakate haim। es samasaya ka pata tab chalata hai jab yah beemaaree gmbheer ruup le letee hai। mdhepan ka ek paramokh kaaraण hai ‘daayabitik retinopaithee’ bhee hai। daayabitik retinopaithee ke do mokhay charaण hote haim। shoruuatee charaण ko naan parolipheretiv daayabitik retinopaithee (enapeedeeara) kahate haim। es charaण mem retina kashetar kee nalikaaem kashatigarasat ho jaatee haim। saamaanayat beemaaree ka yah shoruuatee charaण hota hai, jisamem lakashaणom ka pata naheem chalata hai। kochh maamalom mem kashatigarasat rakat nalikaaom ke phatane se retina ke madhay bhaag mem rakat फ़ail jaata hai। es sathiti ko daayabitik maikayolopaithee kahate haim, esase daृshati parabhaavit hotee hai aur dhomdhala dikhane lagata hai। esake unanat aur vikasit charaण ko paroleepheretiv daayabitik retinopaithee (peedeeara) kahate haim। yah daayabitik retinopaithee kee sabase sabase gmbheer charaण hai। es charaण mem retina kashetar mem kamaja़or avmchhaneey rakat nalikaaem teja़ee se panapane lagatee haim jo retina kee ऑkaseejan apuurati mem baadha paida kar use kashatigarasat karatee haim। es kaaraण retinal ditechamemt ya galuukoma bhee ho sakata hai। retinopathy) - samaya- samay par mkhom kee jmch karaayem, yah jmch bachachom mem bhee avashayak hai। - rakat mem kaॉlesatarol aur shogar kee maatara ko niymtarit rakhem। - agar apako mkhom mem darada, saal baad har teen maheene par mkhom kee jmch karaayem। - garabhavatee mahila agar daayabitik hai to chikitasak se smparak karem। saamaanay upachaar (Treatment for diabetic retinopathy) - vitaamin e yokat khaaday padaarathom ka sevan adhik karem - paalak ko apane bhojan mem shaamil karem - kaale mguur ke beejom ka ras peeem - salaad jayaada se jayaada khaaem Disease: galuukoma (Glaucoma) Description: galuukoma (Glaucoma) galuukomaa, kaala motiya ya kmch bimdo roga, tmtar mem gmbheer evm nirmtar kashati karate hoe dheere-dheere daृshati ko samaapat hee kar deta hai। kisee vasato se parakaash kee kiraणem mkhom tak pahomchatee haim, v usakee chhavi daृshati patal (Retina) par banaatee hai। retima se yah suuchana vidayot tarmgom davaara masatishak tak netar tmtoom davaara pahomchaae jaatee hai। mkh mem ek taral padaarath bhara hota hai yah taral padaarath mkh ke gole ko chikana kie rahata hai yadi es taral padaarath ka risaav rok jaae to mkh ke mdar ka daab baढ़ jaata hai। galuukoma mem mtar netar par daaba, parabhaavit mkhom kee daab sahane kee kashamata se adhik ho jaata hai, esake pariणaamasavaruup netar tmto ko kashati pahomchatee hai, jisase daृshati chalee jaatee hai। kisee vasato ko dekhate samay galuukoma se garasit vayakati ko keval vasato ka kemdar dikhaae deta hai। samay ke saath sathiti bad se badatar hotee jaatee hai। saamaanayata: log es par ka duusara sabase kaaraण hai। Symptoms: - tayuubalaaet ya balab kee roshanee chaarom or se dhomdhalee dikhane lagatee hai, mkhom mem tej darad bhee hone lagata hai। - dhomdhalaapana, kae rogiyom ko raat mem dikhana bhee bmd ho jaata hai - mitalee ya ulatee hona - siradarad Reasons: galuukoma ke kaaraण (Causes of Glaucoma) maanav mkh mem sathit kaaraniya ke peechhe mkhom ko sahee akaar aur poshaण dene vaala taral padaarath (Aqueous Humor Fluid) hota hai, lems ke chaarom or sathit seeliyaree utatak es taral padaarath ko lagaataar banaate rahate haim yah taral padaarath potaliyom ke davaara mkhom ke bheetaree hisase mem jaata hai es tarah se mkhom mem es taral padaarath ka banana aur bahana lagaataar hota rahata hai। savasath mkhom ke lie yah avashayak hai mkhom ke bheetaree hisase mem kitana dabaav rahe yah taral padaarath kee maatar par mirabhar rahata hai। galuukoma rogiyom kee mkhom mem es taral padaarath ka dabaav atayadhik baढ़ jaata hai kabhee-kabhee mkhom kee bahaav nalikaaom ka maarag ruuk jaata hai, lekin seeliyaree otak ese lagaataar banaate hee jaate haim, ise mem jab mkhom mem daृshati-tmto ke opar taral ka dabaav achaamak baढ़ jaata hai to galuukoma ho jaata hai। yadi mkhom mem taral ka etana hee dabaav lmbe samay tak bana rahata hai to esase mkhom ke tmto bhee nashat ho sakate haim। samay rahate yadi es beemaaree ka elaaj naheem karaaya jaata hai to esase daृshati puuree tarah ja sakatee hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar (Treatment and tips to prevent Glaucoma) - khaane mem paalak jayaada khaaem - vitaamin e mkhom ke savaasathay ke lie behad jaruuree hai। ise khaaday padaarath khaaem jinase vitaamin e kee puurati ho। - saumph bhee savasath mkhom ke lie achachha ghareluu nosakha hai। Disease: bavaaseer (Piles) Descriptiom: bavaaseer (Piles) ek asaadhay rog hai। ese hemorahoyadas (Haemorrhoids), paaelas ya muulavayaadhi bhee kahate haim। bavaaseer ko ayoraved mem arash yaani deeraghakaaleen paraaणghaatak beemaaree kaha jaata hai। bavaaseer mem mt ke mtim bavaaseer ke kochh aham kaaraण niman haim: kabaj (Constipation) bavaaseer kee sabase bada़ee vajah pet mem kabaj banana hai। kabaj kee vajah se mal suukha aur kathor ho jaata hai jisakee vajah se Description: mkhom ka emphekashan (Eye Infection) mkhom mem emphekashan haanikaarak suukasham jeevaaणo baikateeriya aur vaayaras ke kaaraण hota hai। ye haanikaarak suukasham jeevaaणo maanasuun ke maheene mem sabase jayaada sakariy hote haim। ye mkhom kee oparee bhaaga, potalee, kaॉramiya aur palakom par akaramaण karate haim jisase mkhom mem suujana, jalam hotee hai। mkh jarorat se jayaada laal ho jaatee hai aur mkhom se jarorat se jayaada paanee ka disachaaraj hone lagata hai। Symptoms: - mkhom se paanee nikalana - mkhom se mavaad nikalana - dhomdhala vijan - mkhom ka suukh jaana - palakom par suujan - mkhom mem khuujalaahat - mkhom mem darad aur jalan - mkhe laal hona Reasons: mkhom ke emphekashan ke kaaraण (Causes and Reasons of Eye Infection) mkhom ke emphekashan se sabase jayaada mkhom kee palakem parabhaavit hotee hai। palakom ke mdaronee hisase mem suujam hone se mkhom kee somdarata to khatam hotee hee hai, samay par elaaj naheem karaame se ghaav hone ka bhee khatara rahata hai। emphekashan jab mkhom ke mdar msuu kee garmthi ko parabhaavit karata hai to suujan se msuu kee garmthi bmd ho jaatee hai aur yah kaaphee darad karane lagata hai। sabase jayaada gmbheer sathiti tab hotee hai jab emphekasham kaॉraniya ko parabhaavit karatee hai। esamem kaॉraniyal alasar ka khatara rahata hai aur mkhom kee roshanee tak chalee jaatee hai। kmjekativaaetis (Conjunctivitis)- kmjekativaaetis mkhom ka sabase kaॉman emphekasham hai jise pimk ae bhee kahate haim। yah ek vaayaral emphekashan hai jo kaaphee tejee se phailata hai। agar mm ko esaka emphekashan hai to navajaat ko bhee yah emphekashan ho sakata hai। vaaeral keraatitees (viral keratitis)- pimk ae kee tarah yah bhee ek ka़ॉman ae emphekasham hai jo harapis ke vaayaras (Herpes simplex virus) ke kaaraण hota hai। yah bhee kaaphee tejee se phailata hai। phmgal keraatitees (Fumgal keratitis)- yah ek phmgal emphekashan hai jo mkhom mem kmtekat laims lagaane se ho sakata hai। 2006 mem yah emphekashan us samay phir ऑragenik maitar ke jaane se hota hai। taraakoma (Trachoma)- yah emphekashan kaaphee gmbheer hota hai aur ganadee jagah mem tejee se phailata hai। gmdagee par panapane vaale makakhiyom aur
