hota hai, jisake esatemaal se nkhom ke smkaramaण ko theek kiya ja sakata hai। aluu ko patale- patale tokaड़om mem kaat lem। raat mem sone se pahale us kate hoe aluu ko 15 minat tak apanee nkhom ke opar laga kar rakhem aur baad use utaar dem। Disease: peeliya (Jaundice) Description: peeliya (Jaundice) peeliya ek isa rog hai jo ek vishesh parakaar ke vaayaras aur kisee kaaraणvash shareer mem pitat yaani rakat mem bileerobin (Bilirubin Disorder) kee maatara baढ़ jaane se hota hai। esamem mareej ko peela peshaab hota hai। usake naakhuuna, tavacha aur mkhom ka saphed bhaag peela paड़ jaata hai aur mareej ko kaaphee kamajoree, kabaja, jee michalaamaa, siradarada, bhuukh n lagana adi shikaayat hone lagatee hai। yah bahot hee suukasha‍m vishaaणo (Virus) se hota hai। shoruu mem jab rog dheemee gati se v maamuulee hota hai tab esake lakashaण dikhaae naheem pada़te haim, lekin jab yah gmbheer ho jaata hai to mareej kee mkhe v naakhuun peele dikhaae dene lagate haim। jin vaayaras se yah hota hai usake adhaar par mokha‍yath peeliya teen parakaar ka hota hai (Types of Jaundice) vaayaral haipetaaetis e, vaayaral haipetaaetis bee tatha vaayaral haipetaaetis naॉn e v naॉn bee। shareer mem esiditee ke badha़ jaane, kaaphee dimom tak maleriya rahane, pitat nalee mem patharee atakane, jayaada sharaab peeme, adhik namak aur teekhe padaarathom ke sevan se aur khuun mem rakatakaणom kee kamee hone se bhee peeliya (Piliya) rog hota hai। Symptoms: - mkh ke saphed bhaag ka peela ho jaana - amaashay mem suujan hona - jee michalaana - tavacha ka rmg peela ho jaana - daahimee pasaliyom ke neeche bhaareepan ana aur darad hona - pitat ke kaaraण mal ka rmg pheeka ya saphed ho jaana - pet mem darad hona - bhuukh naheem lagana - vajam lagaataar kam hona - shaam mem thakaa-thaka mahasuus karana aur 102 digaree ke asapaas bokhaar rahana Reasons: peeliya rog ke kaaraण (Causes and Reasons of Jaumdice) jab shareer mem laal rakat koshikaaem 120 din ke saaekil mem ek nechoral parakariya ke tahat tuutatee hai to vesat baae parodakat ke rop mem bileerobin (Bilirubin Disorder) ka utapaadan hota hai। bileerobin ke jarie shareer kee saaree gmdagee livar se chhan kar baahar nikalatee hai। yah gmdagee peshaab aur mal ke jarie baahar nikalatee hai। agar livar mem smkaramaण hai ya phir rakat mem bileerobin kee maatara 2.5 se jayaada ho jaatee hai to livar ke gmdagee saaph karane kee parakariya avarodadh ho jaatee hai aur esee parisathiti mem peeliya kee beemaaree ho jaatee hai। peeliya rog ke anay kaaraण (Other Reasoms & Causes of Jaundice) agar kisee smkaramaण se laal rakat koshika apanee saamaanay parakariya se pahale hee tuutane lagatee hai to rakat mem bileerobin kee maatara badha़ne lagatee hai। es parisathiti ko paree hepatik jaॉnadis kahate haim। maleriyaa, sakil sel eneemiyaa, theleeseemiya mem aur kae anovmshik kaaraणom se bhee rakat mem bileerobin kee maatara achaanak badha़ne lagatee hai jisase peeliya (Piliya) rog hota hai। agar kisee kaaraण se livar ko nokasaan pahomcha hai to livar se bileerobin banane kee kashamata hee kam ho jaatee hai। ese emtaraa-hepaatik jaॉnadis bhee kaha jaata hai। vaayaral haipetaaetis (Viral Hepatitis), leevar ka alakohalik hona (Alcohol), tej bokhaar (Fever), leevar kaimsar (Liver Cancer), galat davaaom ke sevan aur pairaasitaamol (Medicine Side effects) ke jayaada sevan se bhee emtaraa-hepaatik jaॉnadis hote haim। motaapa mem leevar saaerosis hone ka khatara rahata hai। jisase emtaraa-hepaatik jaॉnadis kee smbhaavana rahatee hai। gaॉl balaadar mem patathara, painakariyaaj ka sahee dhmg se kaam naheem karanaa, painakariyaaj kaimsar ya phir gaॉl balaadar ke kaimsar mem bhee livar davaara baae parodakat bileerobin ko shareer se nikaalane kee parakariya bmd ho jaatee hai। nateeja rakat mem bileerobin kee maatara kaaphee badha़ jaatee hai aur gmbheer peeliya rog ho jaata hai। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur elaaj (Care and Treatment for Jaundice) - dihaaedareshan hone par ae vee phaluuyadas (IV fluids in case of dehydration) - emtee baayotikas (antibiotics) - emtee vaayaral dava (antiviral medicimes) - balad tarmsaphayuujan (blood transfusions) - sateraॉyadas (steroids) - keemotherepee, redieshan therepee aur navajaat ke lie phototherepee (chemotherapy/radiation therapy & phototherapy for newborns) - duudh v paamee ubaal kar peeem। - taaja v saaph aur garam bhojan karem। - sa‍vacha‍chh shauchaalay ka hee parayog karem। - seerimj ko 20 minat tak ubaal kar hee lagavaaem। - peene ke lie hamesha savachachh aur baikateeriya rahit paamee ka hee esatemaal karem। - khaana banaame, parosane, khaane se pahale v baad mem aur shauch jaane ke baad mem haath saabon se acha‍chhee tarah dhona chaahie। - bhojan jaaleedaar alamaaree ya dhaka‍kan se dhak kar rakhana chaahie, taaki makakhiyom v dhuul se bachaaya ja sakem। - rogee bacha‍chom ko daॉka‍tar jab tak yah n bata dem ki ye rog moka‍t ho chuuke hai sa‍kuul ya baahar naheem jaane de। - raka‍t dene vaale va‍yakatiyom kee puuree tarah jmch karane ke baad hee rakat lem। agar rakat mem bileerobin kee maatara jayaada hogee to apako bhee peeliya ho sakata hai। Home Remedies: peeliya rog suukasham vishaaणo ke kaaraण hota hai। es rog ke hone par vayakati ke naakhon aur mkhem peelee dikhaae detee haim। chikitasa kee bhaasha mem peeliya ko vaayaral haipetaaetis (Viral Hepatitis) kahate haim। peeliya rog saapha-saphaae ke abhaav mem ya duushit paanee aur bhojan ke sevam ke kaaraण hota hai। peeliya rog ke hone par vayakati ko bhuukh n laganaa, bokhaar rahanaa, jee michalaanaa, sir mem darad honaa, peshaab ka peela ana tatha kamajoree v thakaan laganaa, jaise lakashaण najar ate haim। peeliya hone par vayakati ka leevar parabhaavit hota hai। yadi samay rahate peeliya rog ka upachaar n kiya jaae to vayakati kee maृtayo bhee ho sakatee hai। jaamem peeliya se bachaav ke ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies for Jaundice) 1. tamaatar ka ras (Tomato juice)- peeliya hone par ek gilaas tamaatar ke ras mem ek chotakee namak aur kaalee mirach milaakar sobah khaalee pet peeem। araam milegaa। 2. muulee kee patatee (Radish leaves)- muulee kee patatiyom ko peesakara, usaka ras nikaalem। lagabhag adha leetar muulee kee patatiyom ka ras rojaana peeem। das din ke bheetar rogee ko peeliya se araam milegaa। 3. papeete kee patatee (Papay leaves)- ek chamamach papeete kee patatee ke pesat mem ek chamamach shahad milaakara, rojaana takareeban do haphatom tak khaaem। peeliya ke upachaar ke lie yah behad phaayademmd ghareluu nosakha hai। 4. ganana (Sugarcane)- gananaa, paachan kariya ko doruusat karata hai saath hee leevar ko bhee behatar tareeke se kaaray karane mem madad karata hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas ganane ke ras mem neembuu ka ras milaakar rojaana do baar peeem। 5. tolasee kee patatee (Basil leaves)- tolasee kee das se panadarah patatee ka pesat banaakara, gaajar ke ras mem mila lem। es ras ko rojaanaa, do se teen haphatom tak peeem। peeliya rog se raahat milegee। 6. jau (Barley)- ek kap jau ko teem leetar paanee mem achachhee tarah ubaal lem aur teen ghmte tak dhak kar rakh dem। es paanee ko din mem kae baar peeem। 7. neembuu (Lemon)- neembuu leevar ko kashatigarasat home se bachaata hai। ek gilaas paanee mem do neembuu nichoड़em aur peeem। 8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam kee 8 giree, 2 khajuur aur 5 elaayachee ko paanee mem raatabhar bhigaakar rakhem। sobah sabake chhilake utaarakara, peesakara, pesat taiyaar karem। esamem thoड़a sa makakhan aur cheenee milakar khaaem। 9. haladee (Turmeric)- ek gilaas gonagona paanee lem aur usamem haladee milaayem, es paanee ko dim bhar mem teen se chaar baar peeem। peeliya ke upachaar ke lie behad parabhaavee upaay hai। 10. chhaachh (Buttermilk)- peeliya hone par chhaachh behad laabhakaaree hai। dahee ko mathakar chhaachh taiyaar karem aur esamem kaalee mirach aur bhona jeera milaakar peeem। 11. kela (Banana)- pake hoe kele ko kochalakara, usamem shahad milaayem। es tarah ke kele ko din mem do baar khaaem। 12. gaajar ka ras (Carrot juice)- gaajar ka taaja ras nikaalakar peeem, peeliya mem raahat milegee। 13. bel kee patatee (Wood apple leaves)- bel kee patatee ko peesakar paaudar bana lem। es paaudar ko paanee mem milaakar rojaana peeem। peeliya ke upachaar ke lie behad parabhaavee upaay hai। 14. kaimomaael chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaael peeliya rog mem behad laabhakaaree hai। kaimomaael kee patatiyom kee chaay banaakar peene se peeliya rog jaladee theek hota hai। es chaay ko peeliya theek hone ke baad bhee peena jaaree rakh sakate haim। 15. mvala (Gooseberry)- mvala vitaamim see se bharapuur hota hai। peeliya rog mem mvale ka sevan karane se behad laabh hota hai। mvale ke sevan se leevar bhee majabuut hota hai। Disease: duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati dosh (Hyper Myopia) Description: duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati dosh (Hyper Myopia) duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati dosha, mem koe bhee vayakati duur kee cheeज़om ko asaanee se aur saaफ़ dekh sakate haim jabaki esamem kareeb kee cheeज़e dhomdhalee (blurr) dikhaae detee haim। duuradaृshati dosh ko savaasathay kee bhaasha mem haaeparopiya (hyperopia) kahate haim। duuradaृshati dosh kitana gmbheer hai yah apake dekhane kee kashamata par nirabhar karata hai। dekhane ke lie nkh ke do bhaag jimamedaar hote haim, kaॉraniya aur lemsa। kaॉraniya nkh ke saamane ka paaradarashee hisasa hota hai jabaki lems nkh ke mdar bana hota hai jo ki cheeज़om ko dekhane par unake shep mem bhee badalaav karata hai। kaॉraniya aur lems donom ek saath kaaray karate haim aur ane vaalee roshamee ko milaate haim aur ese retina par phokas karate haim। retinaa, ae baॉl yaamee mkh ke gole ke peechhe hota hai। jab nkh mem parakaash paravesh karata hai to us par theek se phokas naheem ho paataa, yahee duur daृshati dosh hota hai। yadi nkh ka gola saamaanay se chhota ho tab bhee duur daृshati dosh ho sakata hai। duur daृshati dosh bahot am samasaya hai jise asaanee se theek bhee kiya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - asaamaanay thakaan mahasuus hona। - nkh ke chaarom aur jalan ya darad - tanaavagarasat hona - dhomdhala dikhana (mkh ke ekadam paas kaa) - paढ़ne likhane mem dikakat hona Reasons: duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati dosh ke kaaraण (Causes & Reasons of Hyper Myopia) duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati dosh mem duur kee cheejem saaph aur paas kee cheejem dhomdhalee najar atee haim। mkh ke visharaam kee sathiti mem, parakaash kee sammtar kiraणem daृshatipatal kee smvedanasheel parat se kochh peechhe phokas hotee haim। esee kaaraण vayakati ko paas kee cheejem dekhane mem pareshaanee hotee hai। esake alaava yadi maata pita ko duur daृshati dosh hai to yah bachachom ko bhee parabhaavit kar sakata hai। esake alaava umar baढ़ne ke saath bhee yah samasaya shoruu ho sakatee hai। duuradarashita ko duur karane ke lie sabase asaan tareeka chashama ya kaॉnataikat lems hota hai। lems ke parayog se nkhom mem paravesh karane vaalee roshanee par behatar tarah se kemdarit kar paate haim। Treatments: duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati kee rokathaam ke lie tipas (Treatment & Tips to Prevent Hyper Myopia) - let kar naheem paढ़na chaahie। - paढ़ne likhane ke dauraan behatar roshanee honee chaahie। - haree sabajiym aur phalom ka parayog khaane mem jaruur karem। - teevee ya kmpayuutar par lagaataar kaam na karem, lagaataar na dekhem। - teevee ya kmpayuutar par kaaray karate vaक़t bhee kamare mem parayaapat roshamee homa jaroree hai। Home Remedies: duuradarashita ya duuradaृshati dosh ke ghareluu upaaya- (Home Remedies for Hyper Myopia) nkhom kee raushanee tej ho esake lie vitaamin se puuraण bhojam karem। duudh aur dahee jaise khaaday padaarath jaruur khaaem। mda bhee nkhom ke lie behad phaayademmd hai। saumpha, misharee aur baadaam ko baraabar maatara mem milaakar paaudar banaaem aur sobaha- shaam khaaem। baadaam aur gaumd se bane ladaduu bhee nkhom ke lie phaayademmd haim। nkhom kee roshanee tej karane ke lie salaad (salad) jaruur khaaem। nkhom ke vayaayaam (Eye exsercise) jaruur karem। Disease: momh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer) Descriptiom: momh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer) maauth alasar ko momh mem chhaala ana kahate haim। momh ke mdar jo naram aur molaayam otak hote haim, jise mayuukas membaren (mucous membrane) kahate haim, usee mem chhaale pada़te haim। yah akasar khaane ke dauraan ya kaaphee garam khaane se gaal ke chamada़e ke katane se hota hai। momh mem agar chhaale ho jaaem to kochh bhee khaane mem kaaphee pareshaanee hotee hai। khaana to duur paanee peema bhee moshakil ho jaata hai। chhaale hone par momh mem tej jalan aur darad hota hai। kochh logom ko to bhojan nalee tak mem chhaale ho jaate haim। momh mem chhaala (Muh ke Chhale) ana ek naaramal beemaaree hai, jo kochh dinom baad apane ap theek ho jaatee hai। kochh logom ko chhaale baara-baar ate haim। ise logom ko apanee puuree daॉkataree jmch karaanee chaahie, taaki sahee elaaj kiya ja sake। momh mem chhaale hone ke kae kaaraण hote haim। kae baar pet kee garamee se bhee chhaale ho jaate haim। Symptoms: - chabaane aur barash karane mem pareshaanee - bhuukh mem kamee - masaaledaara, khatata aur namakeen cheej khaane par tej jalan - momh ke mdar saphed aur laal gola-gol chhaale Reasons: momh mem chhaalom ke kaaraण (Causes of Mouth Ulcer) kabaj (Constipation) lmbe samay tak kabaj rahane se momh mem chhaale  jaate haim। ayoraved ke anosaar momh mem chhaale pet kee kharaabee tatha pet kee garamee kee vajah se hote haim। kabaj esakee muul vajah hai। gaal ya jeebh ka katana (Injury in Cheek and Tounge) kae baar koe cheej khaate samay dmtom ke beech jeebh ya gaal ka hisasa  jaata hai, jisakee vajah se chhaale ho jaate haim। ise chhaale momh kee laar se apane-ap theek ho jaate haim। davaaom ke saaed ephekat (Medicine Side Effects) davaaom ke saaed ephekat kee vajah se bhee momh mem chhaale hote haim। lmbe samay tak emteebaॉyotik davaaom sevan karane se momh mem chhaale ane kee smbhaavana jayaada hotee hai। jayaada emteebaॉyotik ke sevan se hamaaree mtom mem laabhadaayak keetaaणoom kee smkhaya ghat jaatee hai, nateeja momh mem chhaale ho jaate haim। dmtom kee galat smrachana (Wrong Structure of Teeth) dmtom kee galat smrachana kee vajah se bhee momh mem chhaale hote haim। yadi dmt aड़e-tirachhe, nokeele ya adhe tuute hoe haim aur esakee vajah se ve jeebh ya momh mem chobhate haim ya unase lagaataar ragaड़ lagatee rahatee hai, to vahm chhaale ho jaate haim। Treatments: elaaj aur dekhabhaal (Treatment of Mouth Ulcer) - jab tak chhaale khatam naheem ho masaaledaar aur khatata khaana bmd kar dem। - khuub paanee peeem। - gonagone namaka-paanee se kolala karem। - momh ko hamesha saaph rakhem। - darad hone par pen kilar dava le sakate haim। - chhaale vaale jagah par emtee-sepatik jel lagaaem। - medeekedet maauth vaash se momh saaph karem, kolala karem। - sobah sobah gaay ke duudh se bane dahee ke saath ek kela khaane se araam milata hai। - khuub tamaatar khaaem। tamaatar ka ras ek galaas paanee mem milaakar kolala karane se chhaale mit jaate haim। - yadi chhaale saamaanay haim, to vitaamin 'bee' kaॉmapalekas tatha pholik esid kee goliym 2-3 din tak lene se chhaale theek ho jaate haim। - chhaale par boro galisareen bhee lagaae ja sakatee hai ya poteshiyam paramaimganet ke ghol se kolala karane par chhaale khatam hote haim। Home Remedies: momh ke mdar kee satah ke kisee bhee tarah se katane ya usake opar koe phoड़a nikalame se alasar ya chhaala ho jaata hai। momh ka alasar hone par vayakati ka momh tatha jeebh parabhaavit ho jaate haim jisase vayakati ko kochh bhee khaane ya peeme mem pareshaanee hotee hai। jaanie momh ke chhaalom se bachaav ke ghareluu nosakhe (Home remedies for mouth ulcer): 1. naariyal ka duudh (Coconut milk)- naariyal ka duudh momh ke alasar mem darad se raahat deta hai saath hee jalan ko duur karata hai। upachaar ke lie ek chamamach naariyal ke duudh mem thoड़a sa shahad milaakar alasar ke opar lagaaem। es upaay ko dim mem teen se chaar baar karem। esake alaava naariyal ke duudh se kolala karame par bhee araam milata hai। 2. dhaniya ke beej (Coriamder seed)- dhaniya ke beej bhee momh ke alasar se raahat dete haim। alasar se hone vaalee jalan ko bhee duur karate haim। upachaar ke lie paanee mem dhaniya ke beej daalakar ubaalem aur es paanee ko chhaanakar alag rakhem। es paanee ko momh mem ghoma ghoma kar kolala karem। es upaay ko bhee din bhar mem teen se chaar baar karem। 3. bekimg soda (Baking soda)- bekimg soda ya sodiyam baae kaarabonet bhee momh ke alasar se nijaat dila sakata hai। esidik khaane- peene se hone vaale alasar mem yah behad laabhakaaree hai। upachaar ke lie ek chhotee chamamach bekimg paaudar mem paanee milaakar pesat taiyaar karem aur parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। 4. shahad (Honey)- momh ke alasar se raahat dene mem shahad bhee behad parabhaavee hai। shahad mem emtee ऑkaseedemt aur emtee maaekarobal goण hote haim। upachaar ke lie ruue ke phaahe ko shahad mem dobaakara, parabhaavit sathaam par lagaaem। esee tarah galisareen aur vitaamin e tel ko bhee lagaaya ja sakata hai। 5. elovera (Aloevera)- elovera ka rasa, parabhaavit sathaam par lagaane se alasar se hone vaale darad se raahat milatee hai। elovera paraakaृtik emteesepatik kee tarah kaaray karata hai jisase chhaale jaladee theek hote haim। 6. dhaniya patatee (Coriander leaves)- dhaniya patatee ko kachacha chabaane se momh ke alasar se raahat milatee hai। dhaniya patatee mem फ़ॉlik esid ke saath vitaamin bee 1, bee 2, bee 6 aur vitaamin see paaya jaata hai। dhamiya patatee ko dmdee ke saath lagabhag 10 minat tak chabaana chaahie। esake parayog se momh se ane vaalee doragmdh se bhee raahat milatee hai। 7. tolasee (Basil)- tolasee mem emtee vaayarala, emtee baikateeriyal aur emtee phmgal goण paae jaate haim। upachaar ke lie 5 se 6 tolasee kee patatiyom ko dhokar achachhee parakaar chabaakar khaaem aur usake baad thoड़a paanee pee lem। es upaay ko dim mem do baara, sobah aur shaam karem। 8. baraph (Ice)- barapha, alasar ke kaaraण momh mem hone vaale darad se raahat detee hai। baraph ko parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se, smbmdhit jagah thoड़ee der ke lie sonan paड़ jaatee hai jisase alasar se hone vaalee jalan aur darad se raahat milatee hai। Disease: alasar (Ulcer) Description: alasar (Ulcer) pet ya chhotee mtom mem hone vaale alasar ko pepatik alasar (Peptic Ulcer) ke ruup mem jaana jaata hai। pet ke pepatik alasar ko gaisatarik alasar bhee kahate haim। alasar ahaar aur tanaav ya phir pet mem amal (acid) kee atirikat maatara jama hone se hota hai। amaashay ka alasar pet ke alasar se jayaada kaॉman beemaaree hai। pepatik alasar amaashay aur pet ke beech kee patalee sorakasha deevaar mem ghaav ke baad chhed ho jaane se hota hai। lmbe samay tak emteebaayotikasa, darad aur sateraॉyad kee dava khaane ke alaava sharaab ke sevan se pet aur amaashay ka alasar hota hai। pet mem esid aur emjaaem ke banane se chhotee mt ke upar amaashay ke paas chhed ya ghaav ho jaata hai jise alasar kahate haim। adhikmshath yah helikobaikatar paaeloree (helicobacter pylori) naam ke ek jeevaaणo ke smkaramaण se hota hai। kochh logom mem alasar ke lakashaण asaanee se jabaki duusarom mem ye jaladee naheem dikhaae pada़te haim। kabhee-kabhee alasar unahem bhee ho jaata hai, jinahomne esake kisee bhee lakashaण ka anobhav naheem kiya hai। Symptoms: - agar pet ka darad alasar ke kaaraण ho raha hai, to raat mem aur jab bhee ap bhuukhe hom, yah achaanak teevar ho sakata hai। - khaana khaame ke do ghmte baad bhuukh mahasuus karanaa। - gais aur dakaar mem vaृdadhi। - thakaavat ka ahasaas honaa। - pet bhara ho mahasuus honaa, aur dher saara taral padaarath pee paane mem asamarathataa। - bhuukh mem kamee। - vajan ghatanaa। - seeme kee hadadiyom aur pet kee naabhi ke beech kisee bhee sathaam par darada। - halakee matalee (nausea), jo sobah jaagane par sabase am hotee hai। Reasons: alasar ke kaaraण (Causes of Ulcers) koe bhee ek khaas kaaraण maheem hota hai jo alasar ke lie utataradaayee hota hai। bahot saare kaaraण ke parabhaav se alasar paida hota hai। lekin yah sapashat hai ki pet aur amaashay ke baach emjaaem aur paachak ras ke asmtolan se jo esid banata hai usee se alasar banata hai। am taur par adhikmsh alasar H. Pylori baikateriya ke smkaramaण se hee hota hai। yah baikateriya pet aur chhotee mt ke beech jo sorakasha deevaar hotee hai, vaheem rahata hai। amataur par yah koe mokasaan naheem pahomchaata hai। lekin esake smkaramaण se kabhee-kabhee pet ke mdaronee satah aur mt mem suujan ho jaatee hai jo baad mem alasar ka rop dhaaraण kar leta hai। pen kilaras aur emtee emphalaametaree dava ke lagaataar sevan se chhotee mt aur pet ke beech kee sorakasha deevaar mem suujan aur chhed ho jaata hai jisase alasar hone kee smbhaavama rahatee hai। aur bhee haim kae vajah (Other Reason for Ulcer) sharaab aur dhuumarapaan ka jayaada sevan kisee gmbheer beemaaree kee vajah se redieshan therepee kee vajah se kise ho sakata hai alasar (Whom May be More Prone to Ulcer) pet ke alasar ke dher saare kaaraण hone par bhee jin logom mem esake vikasit hone ka adhik khatara hota hai, ve haim: ech paaeloree baikateeriya se smkaramit loga। niyamit ruup se daragas ya soe se davaaom ka sevan karane vaale loga। alasar ke paarivaarik etihaas vaale loga। niyamit ruup se sharaab peene vaale loga। leevara, gorade, ya phephada़om se joda़ee beemaariyom vaale loga। 50 saal se adhik umar ke loga। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur elaaj (Treatmemt for Ulcer) - poha aur saumph ko baraabar maatara mem milaakar chuuraण bana leejie, 20 garaam chuuraण ko 2 leetar paanee mem sobah gholakar rakhie, ese raat tak puura pee jaaem। ala‍sar mem araam milegaa। - patata gobhee aur gaajar ko baraabar maatara mem lekar juus bana leejie, es juus ko sobaha-shaam eka-ek kap peene se pepatik alasar ke mareejom ko araam milata hai। - ala‍sar ke mareejom ke lie gaay ke duudh se bane ghee ka esatemaal karana phaayademmd hota hai। - ala‍sar ke mareejom ko baadaam ka sevan karana chaahie, baadaam peesakar esaka duudh bana leejie, ese sobaha-shaam peene se ala‍sar theek ho jaata hai। - sahajan ke pata‍te ko peesakar dahee ke saath pesat banaakar lem। es pesa‍t ka sevan din mem ek baar karame se ala‍sar mem phaayada hota hai। Home Remedies: alasar (ulcer) shareer kee oparee tavacha ya mayuukas jhilalee par ubhara ho ghaav hota hai। alasar jayaadaatar helikobaikatar paayaloree (Helicobacter pylori) naam ke jeevaaणo davaara hota hai। pet kee mt (Intestine) mem kae parakaar ke daravay nikalate haim jo bhojan ko pachaane mem sahaayak hote haim lekin jab yah daravay jayaada maatara mem nikalate haim to pet v mt kee komal tavacha ko jalaane lagate haim। esake kaaraण pet mem ghaav ban jaata hai। jaanie alasar se bachaav ke ghareluu upaay (Home remedies for ulcer): 1.poha (Bittem rice)- poha alasar ke upachaar mem behad phaayademmd hai। poha aur saumph ko baraabar maatara mem milaakar paaudar bana lem। es paaudar kee 20 garaam maatara ko 2 leetar paanee mem gholakar rakh deejie। dopahar se raat tak es paanee ko puura khatam karem। alasar se raahat milegee। 2. patata gobhee aur gaajar (Cabbage and carrot)- patata gobhee mem lekatik esid hota hai jisase emeeno esid bamata hai jo pet mem rakat ka paravaah baढ़aata hai। esake saath hee patata gobhee mem vitaamin see (vitamin c) bhee uchach maatara mem hota hai। patata gobhee aur gaajar ko baraabar maatara mem milaakar juus taiyaar karem aur sobah shaam eka-ek kap peeem। 3. naariyal (Coconut)- naariyal mem emteebaikateeriyal goण paaye jaate haim, jo ki alasar paida karane vaale baikateeriya ko maar dete haim। naariyal ke duudh aur paanee mem bhee emtee- alasar goण paaye jaate haim। alasar ke upachaar ke lie rojaama naariyal paanee peeem। naariyal ke tel ka sevan bhee alasar se bachaata hai। 4. gaay ka duudh (Cow milk)- haladee mem emtee baikateeriyal goण hote haim, gaay ke duudh mem haladee milaakar peeme se bhee alasar rogiyom ko laabh milata hai। 5. baadaam (Almond)- alasar rogiyom ko baadaam peesakara, khaane se laabh hota hai। baadaam ko peesakar usaka duudh jaisa banaakar peeem। 6. sahajan (Drum stick)- sahajan kee phalee bhee savaasathay ke lihaaj se behad phaayademmd hai। esamem emtee baikateeriyal goण hote haim jo rogom se laड़ne mem sahaayak hote haim। sahajan kee phalee ko peesakara, dahee ke saath milaakar khaane se alasar rog mem araam milata hai। 7. shahad (Honey)- kachacha shahad bhee pet ke alasar mem behad laabhakaaree hai। shahad mem galuukoj pairaॉkasaaed (glucose peroxide) paaya jaata hai, jo pet mem maujuud haanikaarak baikateeriya ko khatam kar deta hai। esake saath hee shahad ke sevan se pet kee jalan se bhee araam milata hai। 8. kela (Banana)- kela mem emteebaikateeriyal tatav paae jaate haim। kela khaane se esiditee se bhee raahat milatee hai। kachacha aur paka donom hee tarah ka kela khaane se alasar rogiyom ko behad araam milata hai। kachache kele kee sabajee banaakar usamem ek chotakee heemg milaakar khaaem। 9. lahason (Garlic)- lahason pet ke alasar mem behad laabhakaaree hai। upachaar ke lie do se teen lahason kee kaliyom ko kochalakara, paanee ke saath khaaem। 10. belaphal (Wood apple)- pet ke alasar mem belaphal aur usakee patatiyom ka sevan bhee behad laabhadaayak hai। patatiyom mem maujuud teninas pet ko, kisee bhee tarah ke nokasaan se bachaata hai। belaphal ka ras bhee pet kee jalan aur darad ko duur kara, alasar se bachaata hai। Disease: daayariya (Diarrhea) Description: daayariya (Diarrhea) lagaataar luuj moshan yaani patala dasat anaa, ulatee hona daayariya kahalaata hai। daayariya vaayarala, baikateriyal smkaramaण ke kaaraण to hota hee hai lekin sabase kaॉman kaaraण hai khaana-paan mem gada़bada़ee, paraduushit paanee aur mt kee gada़bada़ee। din mem agar teen se adhik baar paanee ke saath patala dasat ho raha ho to yah daayariya ka lakashaण hai। daayariya mem shareer mem paanee kee kamee ho jaatee hai jise dihaaedareshan kahate haim jo kaaphee gmbheer hota hai। esase shareer kamajor ho jaata hai, shareer mem smkaramaण phailane ka khatara kaaphee badha़ jaata hai। samay par elaaj naheem hone par mareej kee jaan bhee ja sakatee hai। am taur par daayariya 3 se 7 dinom tak pareshaan karata hai। daayariya vaise to kabhee bhee ho sakata hai, lekim barasaat mem vaayaral daayariya jayaada pareshaan karata hai। esakee vajah gmda paanee aur khaanaa-peena hai। daayariya achaanak ho jaata hai aur koras puura hone ke baad hee khatam hota hai। pet mem jayaada eseeditee bamane se bhee daayariya hotee hai। yah sabhee umar ke logom ko pareshaan karata hai। ekayuut daayariya (Acute Diarhea) vayasakom ko saal bhar mem ek baar aur bada़e bachachom ko do baar hota hai। es beemaaree mem sabase jayaada khatara dihaaedareshan se hota hai, jisamem shareer se saara paanee aur khatam ho jaata hai। mt mem paanee jaane se pahale hee vo paas ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - mtom mem suujan se ho daayariya - patala dasat ya luuj moshan (paanee kee taraha) agar do haphate tak rahe। - dasat ke saath khuuna, mv aur pota ata hai। esase shareer kaaphee kamajor ho jaata hai। - ulatee, mitalee ane ke saath patala dasat ata hai। yah pet aur mt mem esiditee banane se hota hai। Reasoms: daayariya ke kaaraण (Causes & Reasons of Diarrhea) vaayaral daayariya (Viral Diarrhea) vaayaral emphekashan se sabase jayaada daayariya hota hai। esake lakashaण kabhee saamaanay to kabhee kaaphee gmbheer ho jaate haim। patala dasata, luuj moshana, pet mem maroड़ ana aur bokhaar esake saamaanay lakashaण haim। vaayaral daayariya 3 se 7 din tak rahata hai। vaayaral daayariya niman vaayaral smkaramaण ke kaaraण hote haim rotaavaayaras (Rotavirus)- navajaat bachachom mem rotaavaayaras vaayaral smkaramaण se vaayaral daayariya ka khatara rahata hai। esase bachane ke lie bachachom ko emtee rotaavaayaras emjekashan bhee lagaaya jaata hai। norovaayaras (Norovirus)- yah vaayaral daayariya vayasakom aur sakuul jaate bachachom ko sabase jayaada pareshaan karata hai। narasimg homa, de keyar semtar aur resatoremt mem esake smkaramaण ka khatara sabase jayaada rahata hai। edenovaayarasa(Adenovirus)- yah vaayaral smkaramaण har umar ke logom ko hota hai। baikateeriyal smkaramaण se daayariya (Bacterial infections) baikateeriyal smkaramaण se ho daayariya kaaphee seeriyas hota hai। baikateeriyal smkaramaण paraduushit paanee, bhojana, phuud pavaaejanimg se hotee hai। baikateeriyal smkaramaण se hoe daayariya mem lagaataar ulatee anaa, lagaataar luuj moshan hote rahanaa, dasat ke saath siraph paanee ane kee shikaayat se mareej kee haalat kaaphee gmbheer ho jaatee hai। baikateeriyal smkaramaण se pet mem gais bhee ban jaatee hai। gmbheer baikateeriyal smkaramaण mem kabhee-kabhee dasat ke saath khuuna, pota aur mv bhee atee hai। aur bhee haim kae vajah (Some more causes) mtom mem suujan ke baad bhee daayariya hota hai e-kolaae ke smkaramaण se bhee daayariya hota hai alakohal sevan ke saaed ephekat mem bhee daayariya hota hai daayabiteej ke mareej ko bhee daayariya kee shikaayat rahatee hai rediyotherepee, keemotherepee mem bhee daayariya kee shikaayat hotee hai kisee khaas emteebaayotikas ke sevan se bhee daayariya hota hai, khaasakar vaise emtee baayotikas jo mt par parabhaav daalate haim parajeevee jo paraduushit paanee aur khaane ke jarie hamaare pet mem jaata hai, vo hamaare paachan tmtar ko bigaada़ deta hai aur jisase daayariya kee shikaayat hotee hai kaimsar kee davaa, vajam ghataane kee davaa, balad pareshar kee dava ke saaed ephekat kee vajah se bhee daayariya hota hai elarajee se bhee daayariya hotee hai, khaasakar vaise cheej khaane se masalama- aratiphishiyal saveetanar ya duudh mem laikatoj kee maatara rahane se daayariya ho sakata hai। Treatments: elaaj aur dekhabhaal (Treatment and Care for Diarrhea) - daayariya hone par tela-masaalom vaale khaane se parahej karana chaahie। - daayariya mem duudh ya duudh se bane padaarath naheem khaana chaahie, mareej kee haalat aur bigada़ jaatee hai। - kele, chaavala, seb ka morababa aur tosat ka misharaण jise baraat kahate haim, esake sevan se daayariya mem raahat milatee hai। - kachacha kela aur chaaval mtom kee gati ko niymtarit karane aur dasat rokane mem sahaayata karate haim। - parayaapat maatara mem taral padaarath lem lekin agar phir bhee daayariya badha़ raha ho to tormt daॉkatar se smparak karem। Home Remedies: jab vayakati kee paachan kariya (Digestive System) sochaaruu ruup se kaaray karana bmd kar detee hai, tab use ulatee aur patale dasat hone lagate haim। yahee sathiti daayariya kahalaatee hai। daayariyaa, baikateeriyal tatha vaayaral emphekasham (Bacterial and Viral Infection) ke kaaraण hota hai, jo duushit bhojan ya khaane ke davaara vayakati ke shareer mem pahomch kara, paachan kariya ko parabhaavit karate haim। daayariya kai dauraan vayakati ke pet mem darad hota hai, pet mem imthana, jee michalaana adi samasayaaem bhee ho sakatee haim। daayariya ke dauraan vayakati ko dee-haaedareshan (Dehydration) ho sakata hai, jisase sathiti aur bhee bigaड़ sakatee hai। daayariya ke lakashaण vayakati mem do se chaar din mem ubharate haim। jaanie daayariya se bachaav ke lie kochh ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies of Diarrhea) neeche diye gae upachaarom ke davaara daayariya beemaaree mem raahat paae ja sakatee hai: 1. dahee (Yogurt)- dahee mem maujuud baikateeriyaa, shareer mem maujuud vishaile baikateeriya ka naash kara, daayariya se bachaate haim। daayariya ke upachaar ke lie do katoree dahee khaane se hee behad araam milata hai। saade chaaval mem dahee milaakar bhee khaae ja sakatee hai। 2. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ka parayog phuud paॉejanimg (food poisoning) hone par bhee kiya jaata hai, ise mem daayariya se raahat deme mem bhee adarak kaaphee parabhaavashaalee hai। adarak ke parayog se pet kee imthan (stomach cramps) aur darad se bhee raahat milatee hai। upachaar ke lie adarak ko kadaduukas karake, usamem shahad (homey) milaakar khaaem। esake tomrat baad paanee n peeem। adarak kee chaay (bina duudh kee) bhee kaaphee araam detee hai। 3. methee daana (Methidana)- daayariya ke elaaj ke lie methee daana behad phaayademmd bataaya gaya hai। ek chhotee chamamach methee daana ko chabaakara, ek baड़ee chamamach dahee khaane se daayariya se nijaat milatee hai। esake alaava ek chamamach methee daana aur jeera (cumin) ko bhuum kar paaudar bana lem aur do baड़ee chamamach dahee mem milaakar khaaem। es misharaण ko din bhar mem teen baar khaane se behad araam milata hai। 4. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ka siraka bhee daayariya mem behad phaayademmd hai। seb ke sirake ka esidik goण, daayariya ke baikateeriya ko khatam kar deta hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas paanee mem ek chamamach siraka milaaem aur pee lem। es misharaण ko ek din mem do se teen baar tab tak peeem jab tak daayariya theek n ho jaae। 5. kela (Banana)- kele mem kaaphee maatara mem paikatim tatav (pectin contemt) aur pauteshiyam hota hai, esalie daayariya mem kela khaane kee salaah dee jaatee hai। daayariya hone par do se teen pake hoe kela roj khaaem। 6. kaimomaael chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaael daayariya ke upachaar mem behad phaayademmd hai। daayariya ke upachaar ke lie kaimomaael kee chaay banaakar peeem। 7. saphed chaaval (White rice)- saadaa, saphed geele chaaval bhee daayariya ke dauraan khaane kee salaah dee jaatee hai। es tarah ke chaaval sopaachay hote haim। es tarah ke chaaval khaane se dasat kam ate haim। saada chaaval ko thoड़a geela karake khaaem। savaad ke lie chaaval mem dahee milaakar kha sakate haim। 8. gaajar ka suup (Carrot soup)- gaajar ka suup bhee daayariya mem behad phaayademmd hai। daayariya ke dauraam shareer mem hoe poshak tatavom (mutrients) kee kamee ko puura karane ke saath hee gaajar ka suup emayuunitee (immunity) ko majabuut karata hai। suup bamaane ke lie, gaajar ko kaat kar ubaal lem aur jab gaajar ubalakar paanee mem ghol jaae taba, paanee ko chhaan kar alag kara lem। esamem savaadaanosaar namaka, bhona jeera aur kaaleemirach paaudar milaaem। Disease: sosatee (Lethargy) Description: sosatee (Lethargy) kae baar shareer mem saphuurati (energy) naheem rahatee। shareer ekadam thaka ho mahasuus karata hai, aur bahot kamajoree mahasuus hotee hai। kae baar alas etana hota hai ki hamesha neemd atee rahatee hai। esee avasatha ko lithaarajee ya sosatee kahate haim। tanaavapuuraण maahaul ya poshaण kee kamee ke kaaraण shareer kamajor hone lagata hai। kae baar raat mem achachhee meemd n sone par bhee agale din thaka ho mahasuus karate haim। lekin jayaada sosatee shareer ke lie behad haanikaarak bhee hai। kae baar yah sosatee maut kee vajah bhee ho sakatee hai, kayomki jayaada sosatee se baren ke selas bhee sosat hone lagate haim aur dheere dheere kaaray karana bmd kar dete haim। puure shareer kee savabhaavik parakariya dheemee paड़ jaatee hai, jo kae samasayaaom ka kaaraण ho sakatee hai। ise mem shareer ko ekativ banaaye rakhana behad jaruuree hota hai। Symptoms: - ekmt achachha lagana - kamajoree mahasuus hona (Weakness in Body) - kisee kaam mem man n lagana - chhote se chhota kaam karane mem chiड़chiड़aana - har samay neemd aur alas ana - har samay lete rahane ka man hona - man mem hamesha nakaaraatamak vichaar ana Reasons: sosatee ke kaaraण (Causes of Lethargy) sosatee ka anobhav sabhee ko hota hai, lekin thoड़a araam karane ya raat kee neemd ke baada, agalee sobah tak sosatee duur ho jaatee hai। yadi esake baad bhee sosatee banee rahe to yah beemaaree ka smket ho sakata hai। kisee bhee vayakati kee sosatee ka asar n keval usake shaareerik balaki maanasik v saamaajik satar par bhee paड़ta hai। sosatee, vayasat dinacharayaa, kharaab jeevan shailee, beemaariym, aniyamit v asmtolit khaana-paan v anay kaaraणom se ho sakatee hai। amataur par achachhee meemd lene aur aur dinacharaya mem badalaav se es samasaya ko kaaphee had tak theek kiya ja sakata hai lekin kae baar chikitasak kee salaah lenee hee paड़tee hai। es samasaya ke anay kaaraण (Reasons of Lethargy) kamajoree kee vajah se। jayaada tamaavagarasat rahane se। neemd puuree n hone kee vajah se। shareer mem vitaamin kee kamee se। shareer mem khuun kee kamee kee vajah se। Treatmemts: sosatee se bachane ke upaay (Tips to Prevent from Lethargy) - roj yog aur vayaayaam karem। - sobah kee taajee hava mem tahalem। - tanaavamokat rahane ka parayaas karem। - khaane mem vitaamin kee maatara baढ़aaem। - kam se kam 8 ghmte kee neemd jaruur lem। - mvale ka morababa bhee shareer ko saphuurati deta hai। - halaka smgeeta, halakee avaaj mem somem। esase bhee maanasik sosatee duur hotee hai। - kae baar sogmdhit telom kee maalish se bhee shareer kee sosatee aur sosatee mitaae ja sakatee hai। - smtolit aur paushatik bhojan karem, jisamem haree sabajiym, daalem, dahee aur mausamee phal shaamil hom। - apanee umgaliyom ke porom se chehare kee masaaj karem। isa karane se balad sarakoleshan baढ़egaa, jisase vayakati ekativ mahasuus karegaa। Home Remedies: bhaagadauड़ bharee adhonik jimdagee aur kae tarah ke tanaava, n keval shaareerik balaki maanasik ruup se bhee vayakati ko thaka dete haim। thakaavat har kisee ko hotee hai paranato kae logom ko puure shareer mem darad kee shikaayat rahatee hai। darad ko kam karane ke lie log akasar penakilar le lete haim। ye davaaem tomrat araam detee haim paranato lamabe samay tak esaka parayog nokasaan pahomcha sakata hai। aee jaanem thakaavat se bachaav ke lie ghareluu nosakhe (Home remedies for lethargy) 1. gareem tee (Green tea)- thakaavat ko duur karane ke lie ek kap gareen tee peena behad parabhaavee hai। niyamit ruup se gareen tee peene se vajan bhee kmtarol mem rahata hai। mmsapeshiyom mem darad (muscle paim) hone par ap gareen tee behad laabhakaaree hai। 2. adarak kee chaay (Ginger tea)- adarak kee chaay kodaratee penakilar ke ruup mem kaaray karatee hai। yah vayakati ko tarotaaja bhee mahasuus karaatee hai। tolasee ke kaaढ़e mem adarak milaakar bhee peeya ja sakata hai। 3. saumph (Saumf)- kisee pakavaan mem savaad baढ़aane ke saath hee saumph sms mem taajaग़ee laane mem bhee behad parabhaavakaaree hai। saumph ka parayog rasoe mem ja़ruur hota hai। saumph khaane se pet saaफ़ rahata hai aur ap khod ko tarotaaja mahasuus karate hai। 4. ajavaayan (Ajwain)- ajavaayam ke patate bhee darad nivaarak dava kee tarah kaam karate haim। yah shareer ke tuute-phote kee mg kee maramamat karane aur joड़om ke darad mem bahot laabhaparad hote haim। 5. kadaduu ke beej (Pumpkin seed)- kadaduu ke beej mem maiganeeshiyam hota hai, jo alas v thakaavat se laड़ne mem madad karata hai। adhe ghmte kee ekasarasaaej mem agar ap thaka ho mahasuus karatee haim to esaka matalab hai ki apamem maigameeshiyam kee kamee hai। vayaayaam ke dauraan shareer mem ऑkaseejan ke niramaaण ke lie maiganeeshiyam jaruuree hai। esakee kamee kee vajah se thakaavat jaladee hotee hai। 6. akharot (Wallnut)- akharot mem omega 3 phaitee esid paaya jaata hai। omega 3 phaitee esid n keval thakaan aur alas se raahat deta hai, balaki yah avasaad se bhee bachaata hai। esalie akharot khaane se apakee jhapakiyom kee samasaya duur hogee। 7. anaaj (Whole grain)- anaaj mem phaaebar kee maatara adhik hotee hai। esalie alas aur thakaan mitaane mem yah madadagaar saabit hota hai। amaaj mem kaॉmapalekas kaarabohaaedaret (complex carbohydrate) hote haim। ye thakaan se laड़me mem madadagaar hote haim। 8. laal mirach (Red chilly)- laal mirach mem vitaamin see paaya jaata hai, jo thakaam duur karata hai। laal mirach se dimaag ekativ rahata hai aur ham hamesha tarotaaja mahasuus karate haim। 9. dahee (Curd)- dahee mem maujuud achachhe baikateeriya paachan tmtar (immume system) ko majabuut rakhate haim। 4 sapataah tak din mem do baar yadi dahee khaaya jaae to shaareerik aur maanasik sehat ke saath rog paratirodhak kashamata bhee baढ़tee hai aur thakaan kam hotee hai। Disease: masatishak ka daura (Cerebral Stroke) Description: hamaare shareer mem masatishak aur maaड़iyom ko paraaणvaayo (Oxygen) aur poshak tatavom kee nirmtar apuurati rakat vaahikaaom se rakat ke davaara kee jaatee hai। jab bhee en rakatavaahikaaom mem kisee kaaraण kashati pahonchatee hai ya avarodh niramaaण hota hai tab masatishak ke kochh hisasom ko rakat kee apuurati bmd ho jaatee hai। jis tarah haraday ko rakat kee apuurati n hone par haृdayaghaat  jaata hai, usee parakaar masatishak ke kochh hisase ko 3 se 4 minat se jayaada rakat n milane par paraaणvaayo aur poshak tatavom ke abhaav mem nashat hone lagata hai, ese hee masatishak ka daura bhee kahate haim। Symptoms: - kamajoree mahasuus hona (Weakness im Body) - disha aur niradesh samajhane mem pareshaanee - siradarad hona - bharam kee sathiti - bolane mem takaleeph hona - jee michalaana aur ulatee hona - shareer ke ek hee taraph ke chehare, haath ya tmg mem sonanapan - dheere ya asapashat bolama - achaanak laड़khaड़aanaa, chakakar anaa, shareer ka smtolan bigaड़na - ek ya domom nkhom se dekhane mem kathimaae Reasons: masatishak ke daure ke kaaraण (Causes & Reasons of Cerebral Stroke) masatishak ka daura hone ke mokhayata: 2 kaaraण hote haim, jo niman haim: 1. arakatata masatishak ka daura (Ischemic stroke)- daura paड़ne ka sabase am kaaraण hai। yah dimaag ke kisee rakatavaahinee ke smkeeraण hone ya avarodhar niramaaण home ke kaaraण hota hai। yah bhee do parakaar ka hota hai- 1.1. tharomabotik satarok (Thrombotic stroke)- es parakaar ke masatishak ke daure mem masatishak kee rakat vaahinee mem khuun ke jam jaane ke kaaraण ya thakake ke kaaraण avarodh ho jaata hai। jin rogiyom mem khuun ke mdar kolesataraॉl ka paramaaण jayaada hota hai, ise rogiyom kee rakatavaahinee mem bheetaree satar par vasa jama ho jaatee hai jise palaak kahate hai। es par khuun ka thakaka jama ho jaane par dheere-dheere puuree rakatavaahinee mem avarodh hone lagata hai aur masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat n milane par tharomabotik satarok paड़ jaata hai। 1.2. embolik satarok (Embolic stroke)- es parakaar ke masatishak ke daure mem rakat ka thakaka ya emjekashan ya salaaem davaara galatee se rakat vaahimee mem paravesh kiya ho hava ka chhota bolabola masatishak ke kisee chhotee rakatavaahinee mem phasane ke kaaraण rakatavaahinee mem avarodh niramaaण ho jaata hai aur masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat n milane par embolik satarok paड़ jaata hai। 2. rakatasataraav masatishak ka daura (Hemorrhagic stroke)- masatishak kee kisee rakatavaahinee mem rakatasataraav home ke kaaraण hone vaale es parakaar ke masatishak ke daure behad gmbheer hote hai। uchach rakatachaapa, rakat vaahinee kee janamajaat vikaृti ya rakat vaahinee mem pholaav ke kaaraण masatishak mem rakatasataraav ho sakata hai। esake do parakaar haim- 2.1. emtaraa- karaaniyal haimarej (Intra-cranial hemorrhage)- es parakaar mem masatishak ke kisee rakatavaahinee mem rakatasataraav hone ke kaaraण masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat kee apuurati mem kamee ane ke kaaraण baren selas ko kashati pahomchatee hai। es parakaar ke masatishak ke daure ka paramokh kaaraण uchach rakatadaab hai। lagaataar kae samay tak uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran rakatavaahinee kamajor aur kaड़ee ho jaatee hai aur pariणaamata: phat jaatee hai। 2.2. saba- arakanoed haimarej (Sub-archnoid hemorrhage)- es parakaar mem masatishak aur kapaal ke beech ke satar mem kisee rakatavaahinee mem rakatasataraav hone ke kaaraण sab arakanoed sapes mem rakat ekatarit ho jaata hai। esaka paramokh kaaraण rakat vaahinee kee janamajaat vikaृti ya rakat vaahinee mem pholaav hota hai। es parakaar mem rogee ko tej saradarad ka anobhav hota hai। 2.3. tarmsemt eshachemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack)- ek teesare parakaar ka bhee masatishak ka asathaae daura hota hai jisame satarok ke lakashaण kochh minatom se lekar kochh ghmto tak hee rahate haim aur baad mem theek ho jaate haim। ese tarmsemt eshachemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack) ya teeaee (TIA) kaha jaata hai। yah es baat kee chetaavanee deta hai ki apako koe samasaya hai aur esaka elaaj n karaane par nikat bhavishay mem apako satarok paड़ sakata hai। Treatments: masatishak ka daure se bachane ke lie upaay (Treatments & Tips to Prevents Cerebral Stroke) - sharaab aur dhuumarapaan bmd karem। - phala, sabajiym etayaadi ahaar lena chaahie। - tanaav se duur rahem। niyamit vayaayaam aur yog karem। - agar ap motaape ke shikaar hai to apana vajan niymtarit rakhem। - agar baara-baar siradarad kee pareshaanee hotee hai to chikitasak se esakee jnch karaaem। - agar ap uchach rakatachaap (Hypertensiom), madhomeh (Diabetes), haraday rog (Heart disease) se peeड़it haim to niyamit daॉkatar se jnch karaate rahem। Disease: maayopiya (Myopia) Description: ajakal adhikaash logom kee mkhom mem ripharaikativ (Refractive) vikaar yaani kiraणom ke vakar kee samasaya ke lakashaण dikhaae dene lage haim। esamem nikat daृshati dosh yaani maayopiya (Myopia) se sabase jayaada log parabhaavit haim। chikitasakom ke anosaara, bachapan mem dekhane kee kashamata ka vikaas aur kishoraavasatha mem mkh kee lmbaae baढ़tee hai lekin nikat daृshati dosh hone kee vajah se yah kochh jayaada hee baढ़ jaatee hai। isee sathiti mem mkh mem jaanevaala parakaash retina par kemdarit naheem hotaa। esee vajah se tasaveer dhomdhalee dikhaae detee hai lekin es dosh ko kaॉnatekat lems ya sarajaree se theek karaaya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - chakakar ana - bachachom ko sakuul mem balaik borad par likha ho n dikhana - teleevijan dhomdhala dikhana - mkhom ka bhaimga hona - duuree par likhe akashar n paढ़ paana - sir mem darad rahana Reasons: maayopiya ke kaaraण- (Causes & Reasons of Myopia) ise log jo nikat daृshati dosh kee samasaya se pareshaan haim yaami ki jinahem thoड़ee duur kee cheejem bhee saaph dikhaae naheem deteem, use ripharekativ erar (Refractive error) kahate haim। maayopiya se garasat logom mem aebaॉl bahot lmbee ho jaatee hai ya phir kaॉraniya (Cornia) bahot jayaada karavee ho jaata hai jisase mkh mem pahomchane vaala parakaash theek tarah se phokas naheem kar paataa। ise mem kisee bhee cheej kee tasaveera, retina par n banakara, usake saamane ban jaatee hai jisase cheejem dhomdhalee dikhaae detee haim। yah samasaya umar ke saath baढ़tee jaatee hai। maayopiya kee samasaya se juujh rahe log chashama ya kmtekat laims ke jariye samasaya se nijaat pa sakate haim lekin samasaya jayaada ho to ऑpareshan davaara maayopiya ka elaaj smbhav hai। esake alaava niman kaaraण bhee haim: (Other Reasons & Causes of Myopia) daayabiteej (Daibetes) se garasit hone para। anovmshikee (Genetic Disorder) kaaraणom se bhee isa ho sakata hai। lmbe samay tak ek hee laims ka parayog karamaa। (Use of lenses) kisee bhee cheej ko bahot paas se ghuurakar kaaray karanaa। kam roshanee mem koe kaaray karanaa, jaise paढ़na ya teevee dekhanaa। Treatments: maayopiya se bachaav ke lie saamaanay upachaar (Treatment & tips for Myopia) - bareethimg vayaayaam karem। - tariphala chuuran rojaana lem। - lmbe samay tak teleevijan dekhane ya paढ़ne se bachem। - jahm kaam karem, vahm parayaapat roshanee honee chaahie। - mkhom kee roshanee baढ़aane ke lie mvala ka parayog karem। - momh mem paanee bhar kar mkhom ko taaje paanee se dhoem। - paraduushaण ya dhuup mem nikalane se pahale mkhom par chashama pahamem। - likaresee kee jaड़ ka paaudar aur shahad milaakar duudh ke saath lem। - maariyala, misharee, saumph aur baadaam ko milaakar mikasar taiyaar karem aur paaudar banaayem। din mem do baar khaaem। Disease: khararaate lena (Snoring) Description: sote vakat sms ke saath tej avaaj aur vaaebareshan (Sound & Vibratiom) ana khararaate (Snoring) kahalaata hai। khararaate lema saadhaaraण-see pareshaanee hai, lekin jab yah beemaaree ka ruup le letee hai to gmbheer samasaya ban jaatee hai। sms lene mem baara-baar rokaavat hone par shareer mem ऑkasijan ka leval kam ho jaata hai, jisase beepee baढ़ jaata hai। shareer mem ऑkasijan kam hote hee dil ko ऑkasijan ke lie jayaada pareshar lagaana paड़ta hai। jab yah samasaya baढ़ jaatee hai to haarat ataik bhee ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - sobah uthane par gale aur naak ka suukha hona - din ke samay bhee neemd mahasuus hona - chhote chhote kaamom ke baad bhee thakaan mahasuus hona aur alas ana - gale aur naak se tej avaaj nikalana - sote vakat momh khol jaana aur hava nikalana Reasons: khararaate ya sanorimg ke kaaraण- (Causes & Reasons of Snoring) jayaadaatar logom ko lagata hai ki khararaate ane kee vajah jayaada thakaan hai esalie ve ese anadekha kar dete haim। esase samasaya gmbheer ho jaatee hai। daraasala, sote samay sms mem rokaavat khararaate ane kee mokhay vajah hai। gale ke pichhale hisase ke smkare ho jaane par ऑkasijan smkaree jagah se hotee hoe jaatee hai, jisase asapaas ke tishuu vaaebaret (Tissue Vibrate) hote haim। esee se khararaate ate haim। kae baar log peeth ke bal sote haim, jisase jeebh peechhe kee taraph ho jaatee hai। taaluu ke peechhe yuuvayal (taaluu ke peechhe thoड़aa-sa lataka ho mmsa) par jaakar lag jaatee hai, jisase sms lene aur chhoड़ne mem rokaavat ane lag jaatee hai। esase sms ke saath avaaj aur vaaebareshan hone lagata hai। neeche vaale jabaड़e ka chhota hona bhee khararaate ane ka ek kaaraण hai। jab vayakati ka jabaड़a saamaanay se chhota hota hai to letane par usakee jeebh peechhe kee taraph ho jaatee hai aur sms kee nalee ko balaॉk kar detee hai। ise mem sms lene aur chhodana़e ke lie pareshar lagaana paड़ta hai, jis kaaraण vaaebareshan hota hai। naak kee hadadee teढ़ee hona (Crooked Nose Bone) aur usamem mms baढ़a (Meat soar) honaa। esamem bhee sms lene ke lie pareshar lagaana paड़ta hai। Treatments: khararaate ya sanorimg se bachaav ke lie upaaya- (Tips & Treatments to Prevent Snoring) - some kee pojeesham badalem। - nashe vaale padaarathom se duur rahem। - takiye ke kavar badalate rahem। - raat ke samay halaka khaana khaaem। - gale kee regayolar ekasarasaaej karem। - khuub paanee peeem aur shareer ko haaedaret rakhem। - naak kee hadadee mem samasaya ho ya phir mms baढ़a ho to daॉkatar se samay rahate milem। - kae baar pareganemsee mem vajan badhana़e ya sone kee sathiti sahee n hone par bhee khararaate ate haim। ise mem karavat lekar sona chaahie। - peeth ke bal sone kee bajaay karavat lekar soem। esase sms kee nalee mem rokaavat naheem hotee। sote samay sir ko thoड़a omcha karake soem। esase apakee jeebh aur sms kee nalee mem rokaavat naheem aegee। - agar khararaate ane ka kaaraण jayaada vajan hai to samay rahate vajan kmtarol karem। jim jaॉen karem। niyamit yog aur ekasarasaaej karane se vajan ko kmtarol kiya ja sakata hai। Disease: samabaran (Sunburn) Description: sanabaran ya dhuup se jholasana (Sunburn) dhuup ke kaaraण tavacha ka parabhaavit hona am baat hai। koe bhee vayakati yadi dhuup mem jayaada der rahata hai to suuray kee kiraणom usakee tavacha (Skin) ko mokasaan (Damage) pahomcha sakatee haim। yadi tej dhuup kee vajah se tavacha jayaada jal ya jholas jaae to yah sathiti sanabaran (Sunburn) kahalaatee hai। Symptoms: - parabhaavit hisasa chhuune par garam lagata hai। - parabhavit hisasa gahara laala, kaala ya gahara bhuura najar ata hai। - dhuup se ane ke baad tormt tavacha ke pharak ko dekha ja sakata hai। - parabhaavit hisase par jalan aur darad mahasuus ho sakata hai। - tavacha par paramaanemt pharak aya hai esaka pata 24 ghmte ke mdar dekha ja sakata hai। - tavacha ruukhee tatha bejaan najar atee hai। - chhote chhote chhaale ya paanee vaale daane bhee ho sakate haim। - parabhaavit jagah par suujan bhee  sakatee hai। - bokhaar ke saath ulatee bhee lag sakatee hai। Reasons: sanabaran ya dhuup se jholasane ke kaaraण (Causes & Reasons of sunburn) suuraj kee alataraavaॉyalet kiraणom ke seedhe taur par smparak mem ane par sanabaran hota hai। shareer paraakaृtik ruup se mailemin (Natural melanin) ka niramaaण karake khod ko suuraj kee kiraणom ke parakop se bachaata hai। mailenin ek rmjak yaani pigamemt (Pigment) hota hai jo tavacha ke rmg ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। kaale ya smvale logom kee tavacha gore rmg ke logom kee apekasha kam daimej hotee hai kayomki smvalee tavacha mem pigamemt jayaada banata hai। gore (Fair) logom mem pigamemt kam hota hai esalie unakee tavacha suuray ke smparak mem ane par jaladee kashatigarasat hotee hai। esake alaava maidaanee elaakom (Grounded Area) mem rahane vaale logom kee apekasha pahaaड़ee elaakom (Hill Tract) mem rahane vaale logom kee tavacha bhee jaladee kashatigarasat (Damage) hotee hai kayomki vahm suuraj maidaan kee apekasha najadeek aur tej hota hai। Treatments: dhuup se jholasane ya sanabaran se bachaav ker lie upaay (Tips & Treatmemt for Sunburn) - puuree baahom ke kapaड़e pahanem। - kheere, tamaatar aur aluu ka ras lagaaem। - sanabaran vaale hisase par thmdee patatiym rakhem। - har chaar ghmte par sanasakareen lagaaem। - dhuup mem jaame se adha ghmta pahale sanasakareen ka parayog karem। - koshish karem ki sobah 10 se shaam 4 ke beech dhuup mem n jaaem। - dhuup se jholasee tavacha par elovera bhee behad phaayada pahomchaata hai। - kaॉtan ka kapaड़a thmde duudh mem bhigaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। - parabhaavit hisase par thmdee dahee lagaane se bhee bahot araam milata hai। - dhuup mem nikalane se pahale khod ko achachhee tarah se dhakakar nikalem, masalan mkhom par chashamaa, sir par sakaaraph ya kaip pahanem। Disease: galaso (Mumps) Description: galaso (Mumps) galaso (Mumps) ek vaayaral smkaramaण (Viral Infection) hai। yah haalmki shareer ke kae hisasom ko parabhaavit kar sakata hai lekina, mokhay ruup se laar garmthiyom ko parabhaavit karata hai jo kaan aur jabaड़e ke beech mem paratayek gaal ke peechhe sathit hotee haim। galaso laar garmthiyom (Salivary Glands) kee suujan (Swelling) aur darad (Pain) ka kaaraण bamata hai। yah rog mokhay ruup se 5 se 15 varash kee umar mem adhik dekhane ko milata hai। laड़kom kee apekasha laड़kiyom mem (Specially in girl) yah rog jaladee hota hai। emteebaayotik davaaom se galaso ka elaaj smbhav naheem hai, yah do haphatom mem yah apaneap hee samaapat ho jaata hai। darad mivaarak dava jaise ebuuparophen ya peraasitaamol ka upayog kiya ja sakata hai aur suuje hoe bhaag par thmda paik lagaane se bhee madad milatee hai। ek saadhaaraण se pareekashaण se galaso kee poshati ho sakatee hai kayomki kaanom ke ekadam saamane jabaड़e mem suujan dikhaae detee hai। kalachar ya rakat pareekashaण (Blood test) davaara bhee nidaan kee poshati ho sakatee hai। rakat mem emteebaॉdee kee upasathiti asaanee se vaayaral smkaramaण kee poshati kar deta hai। Symptoms: - kaan mem darad hona - pet mem darad hona - bhuukh n lagana - chabaame aur nigalane mem darad hona - bokhaar - siradarad - gaalom mem suujan dikhaae dena - kamaja़oree Reasons: galaso ke kaaraण (Reasons & Causes of Mumps) galaso ya mamapas perotid garmthiyom mem vaayaral smkaramaण (Viral Infection) se hone ke kaaraण hone vaalee beemaaree hai। yah garmthiym laar banaatee haim jo chehare ke donom taraph jabaड़e kee hadadee ke meeche sathit hotee hai। yah smkaramit laar (Infected Saliva), chheemkane ya khmsane (Sneezing or Coughing) tatha smkaramit vayakati (Infected Person) ke saath baratam saajha karane adi se ek vayakati se duusare vayakati mem phailatee hai। mamapas ke vaayaras se smkaramit mareeja, perotid garmthi mem suujan shoruu hone ke 7 dim pahale aur 7 dim baad tak smkaramaण phaila sakata hai। lakashaणom kee shoroat amataur par vaayaras se smparak ke baad 14-18 dinom mem hotee hai। isa kaha jaata hai ki koe bhee vayakati keval ek baar hee galaso se peeड़it hota hai, lekin kochh log dobaara bhee smkaramit ho sakate haim। mamapasa, khaana aur paanee sheyar karane se bhee phail sakata hai। yuum to yah rog bachachom mem jayaada dekhame ko milata hai lekin esake lakashaण kisee bhee umar ke vayakati ko parabhaavit kar sakate haim। yah bahot gmbheer beemaaree naheem hai lekin kae baar samasaya baढ़ bhee jaatee hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar Home Remedies: jaanem galaso ya mamapas ke ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies for Mumps) phalom ka ras n peeem। parayaapat maatara mem paanee peeem। emaemaar ke teeke lagavaayem। teekha ya amaleey khaane se bachem। suuje hoe hisase par thmdee ya garam patatee ka sek karem। kaalee mirach ka lep parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se araam milata hai। elovera ko chheelakar us par haladee daalakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। adarak ko peesakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se bhee mamapas mem araam milata hai। peepal ke patate ko sek kar us par ghee ya tel lagaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par bmdhem। methee ke paaudar mem jau ka ata milaakar parabhaavit sathaam par lep karane se araam milata hai। baragad ke peड़ kee patatiyom ko bhee tel lagaakar garam karake parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se araam milata hai। Disease: kaalee khmsee (Whooping Cough) Description: kaalee khmsee (Whooping Cough) vahuupimg kaph ya kaalee khmsee (Whoopimg cough) gmbheer kisam kee khmsee hotee hai, jo jayaadaatar 5 se 15 varash ayo tak ke bachachom ko hotee hai। ese kokor khmsee bhee kaha jaata hai। yah khmsee bachachom mem home vaalee ek smkaraamak tatha khataranaak beemaaree hai। yah mokhayata: shavasan tmtar (Respiratory System) ko parabhaavit karatee hai। bhaarat jaise vikaasasheel desh mem paratayek ek laakh kee abaadee par 578 bachache paratayek varash es beemaaree se garasit hote haim। yah rog laड़kom kee tolana mem laड़kiyom ko jayaada hota hai। 6 maheene se kam umar ke bachachom mem es beemaaree se maृtayo dar adhik hotee hai। haalmki yah beemaaree saal ke kisee bhee maheene mem ho sakatee hai kimto saradee ke mausam mem kaalee (kokora) khmsee hone kee bahot adhik smbhaavana rahatee hai। baara-baar khmsee hone aur ulatee hone se bachache shaareerik ruup se bahot kamajor ho jaate haim। kochh bhee khaate-peete samay khmsee ka daura paraarmbh ho jaata hai। lagaataar khmsee ka daura chalane par ulatee hotee hai। baara-baar ulatee hone par khaaya ho bhojan pet se baahar nikal jaata hai। kae baar aushadhi khilaate samay bhee khmsee shoruu ho jaatee hai aur ulatee hone jaane ke kaaraण aushadhi bhee nikal jaatee hai। khmsee ke rogee bachache ko bisatar par jaame ke baad thoड़ee der baad khmsee ka parakop adhik hota hai। bachache ke jora-jor se bolane aur chilalaame par khmsee ka daura paraarmbh ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - ghabaraahat homa - khmsate- khmsate mkh se paanee ana - sms bmd hone ka ehasaas homa - bokhaar ya jokaam hona - gale kee nasom ka phuul jaana - chehare ka peela paड़ jaana - khmsate khmsate gale ka ruumdh jaana - hava jayaada leme kee chhatapataana - sms lene mem ghor ghor kee avaaj ana Reasons: kaalee khmsee ke kaaraण- (Cause & Reason of Whoopimg Cough) kaalee khmsee (Whooping cough) himophaaelas paratosis (Haemophilus Pertussis) jeevaaणoom ke smkaramaण se hotee hai। rog ke jeevaaणo rogee bachache kee maak aur momh mem chhipe rahate haim। jab rogee bachache jor se khmsate aur chheemkate haim to rog ke suukasham jeevaaणo vaayo mem phailakar duusare savasath bachache tak pahomch jaate haim। rogee bachache se baatacheet karane, usake saath uthane-baithane se yah rog duusare bachachom mem bhee phail jaata hai। ghar mem kisee ek vayakati ko kaalee khmsee ho jaane par dheere-dheere puure ghar mem khmsee phail jaatee hai। chhote bachachom mem kaalee khmsee kee utapatati saradee-jokaam ke kaaraण hotee hai। adhik saradee lagane, paamee mem adhik bheegane v saradee ke dinom mem nmge pmv ghuumame se saradee-jokaam hota hai। ise mem kochh bachache muumgaphalee, akharot v anay koe meva aur ghee, tel makakhan se banee cheejem khaakar thmड़a paanee peete haim to unahem khmsee ho jaatee hai jo saradee ke parakop se kaalee (kokora) khmsee mem parivaratit ho jaatee hai। kochh bachachom ko kaalee khmsee ka rog elarajee ke kaaraण hota hai। elarajik vasato ke smparak mem ane par sms lene mem pareshaanee hotee hai। gale mem jalan v khojalee hotee hai। gale mem suujam hone se khmsee ka parakop baढ़ne ke kaaraण rogee ko bahot peeड़a hotee hai। khmsate hoe rogee ka momh laal paड़ jaata hai। momh se laar girane lagatee hai। mkhom mem se msuu bahane lagate haim। rogee bachache bhayabheet hokar rome lagate haim। anat mem ulatee hone par khmsee ka parakop kochh kam ho jaata hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar Home Remedies: jaanem kaalee khmsee se bachaav ke ghareluu upaay (Home Remedies for Whooping Cough) 1. sohaagaa, kalameeshoraa, phitakaree, kaala namak aur yavakashaar ko peesakar chuuraण taiyaar kar lem। ese tave par bhuunakar 2-2 garaam kee maatara mem shahad ko milaakar bachachom ko chataane se kaaleekhmsee duur ho jaatee hai। esake alaava tave par bhona ho sohaaga v vmshalochan ko milaakar shahad ke saath rogee bachache ko chataane se bhee kaaleekhmsee duur hotee hai। 2. peepala, kaakaड़aasimgee, atees aur baheड़a sabhee aushadhiyom ko 20-20 garaam kee maatara mem lekar baareek kuuta-peesakar chuuraण taiyaar kar lem। esamem 10 garaam nausaadara, 10 garaam bhona ho sohaaga milaakar pees lem। esake 3 garaam chuuraण ko din mem 2-3 baar chaatane se kaalee khmsee duur ho jaatee hai। 3. aड़uusa ke suukhe patatom ko mitatee ke baratan mem rakhakara, ag par garam karake usakee raakh ko taiyaar kar lem। us raakh ko 24 se 36 garaam tak kee maatara mem lekar shahad ke saath rogee ko chataame se kaaleekhmsee duur ho jaatee hai। 4. muulee ka 50 mileeleetar ras aur ganane ka ras milaakar din mem 2 baar pilaane se kokar khmsee mem laabh milata hai। 5. 3 mileeleetar naariyal ka tel halaka garam karake bachache ko pilaane se khmsee ka parakop kam ho jaata hai। naariyal kee jata kee bhasam karake lagabhag 1 garaam ka chautha bhaag shahad mem milaakar ya paanee se khaaem। esase 2-3 baar mem hee khmsee ka veg v khmsee khatam ho jaatee hai। 6. adarak ke ras ko shahad mem milaakar 2-3 baar chaatane se kaalee khmsee ka asar khatam ho jaata hai। 7. 3 baadaam raat ko paanee mem daalakar rakh dem। sobah uthakar baadaam ke chhilake utaarakar lahason kee ek kalee aur misharee ke saath milaakar pees lem। es misharaण ko bachachom ko khilaane se kaalee khmsee duur ho jaatee hai। 8. bachachom ko kokar khmsee hone par lahason kee maala pahanaate haim jisase esakee gmdh khmsane ke saatha-saath anadar chalee jaatee hai aur esee ka ras adha chamamach shahad ke saath bhee pilaaem। esase kaalee khmsee duur ho jaatee hai। das buumd ya ek chamamach lahason ka ras (umar ke anosaara) shahad milaakar paratidin do-teem baar sevan karane se khuub laabh milata hai। 9. tave ko ag par rakhakar laumg ko bhuun lem, phir us laumg ko peesakar shahad mem milaakar chaatane se kaalee khmsee theek ho jaatee hai। bachachom ko kaalee khmsee mem ek chauthaae garaam se kam golochan ko sobaha-shaam shahad ke saath chataane se laabh milata hai। 10. tolasee ke patatom ke 3 garaam ras mem shahad milaakar chaatane se kaaleekhmsee mem bahot adhik laabh milata hai। 11. tolasee ke patate aur kaaleemirach samaan maatara mem pees lem। esakee muumg ke baraabar kee goliym bana lem। eka-ek golee ko chaar baar dena chaahie। esase kaalee khmsee nashat ho jaatee hai। 12. kaalee khmsee hone par bachachom ko bisatar par solaane se pahale usake seene aur kamar par kapuur ko tel mem milaakar maalish karem, kaalee khmsee banad ho jaaegee। 13. haladee kee 3-4 gmthom ko toड़kar tave par bhuumem aur peesakar chuuraण bana lem। es chuuraण ko 3-3 garaam sobaha-shaam paanee se leme se kaaleekhmsee mem araam ata hai। Disease: parosatet disaऑradar (Prostate Disorder) Description: parosatet disaऑradar (Prostate Disorder) parosatet galaimd jayaada baढ़ jaane par parosatet disaऑradar (Prostate Disorder) kahalaata hai। lagabhag tees pheesadee porosh 40 kee umar mem aur pachaas pheesadee se bhee jayaada porosh 60 kee umar mem parosatet kee samasaya se pareshaan hote haim। parosatet galaimd ko poroshom ka duusara dil bhee maana jaata hai। pauruush garmthi shareer mem kochh behad jaruuree kariya karatee hai। jaise yuureem ke bahaav ko kmtarol karana aur parajanan ke lie seemen banaanaa। jaise-jaise umar baढ़tee hai, yah garmthi baढ़ne lagatee hai। es garmthi ka apane ap mem baढ़na hee haanikaarak hota hai aur ese beepeeech (Benign Prostatic Hyperplasia) kahate haim। parosatet garmthi ke jayaada baढ़ jaane se muutar utasarajan kee pareshaanee ho jaatee hai। garmthi ke akaar mem vaृdadhi ho jaane par muutar nalika avarodadh ho jaatee hai aur yahee peshaab rokane ka kaaraण banatee hai। parosatet garmthi ke akaar mem vaृdadhi hone ka kaaraण sapashat naheem hai। baढ़tee umar ke saath poroshom ke shareer mem hone vaala haaramon ka parivaratan ek kaaraण ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - raat ko kae baar peshaab ke liye uthanaa। - muutar kee kochh maatara muutaraashay mem shesh rah jaatee hai, es shesh rahe muutar mem rogaaणo panapate haim। - peshaab karane mem kathinaae mahasuus honaa। - peshaab karane ke baad bhee muutar kee buumde tapakatee rahatee haim, yaani muutar par niymtaraण naheem rahataa। - isa mahasuus hota hai ki peshaab  raha hai lekin baatharuum mem jaane par buumda-buumd ya roka-rok kar peshaab hota hai। - peshaab mem jalan mahasuus hotee hai। - mdakoshom mem darad uthata rahata hai। - jaladee jaladee peshaab honaa। - peshaab kee dhaar chaaluu hone mem vilmb honaa। Treatments: parosatet upachaar (Treatment & Tips to Prevent Prostate Disorder) parosatet garmthi mem vaृdadhi hone par mareeja़ ko chikitasakeey upachaar kee avashayakata hotee hai। muutar thailee ke lagaataar bhare rahane se goradom par dabaav baढ़ jaata hai, jisase enake kharaab hone ka ख़tara paida ho jaata hai। rog kee paraarmbhik avasatha mem davaaom davaara garmthi kee vaृdadhi ko kam karane ka parayaas kiya jaata hai। kochh mareeja़om ko davaaeyom se koe laabh naheem hotaa, isee sathiti mem shalayakariya karake rogee ke shareer se parosatet garmthi nikaal dee jaatee hai। chikitasa kee adhonik padadhati se kam se kam cheera-phaaड़ v rakata-saraav davaara parosatet garmthi kee beemaaree ka elaaj smbhav hai। isee hee ek adhonik takaneek hai leja़r kiraणom se parosatekataॉmee। lejar parosatekataॉmee (Laser Prostatectomy) esamem lejar kiraणom ke maadhayam se parosatet garmthi ke us hisase ko kaatakar alag kar diya jaata hai jisase muutar nalika ka maarag avaruudadh ho raha thaa। leja़r parosatekataॉmee mem ek phaaebar ऑpatik teleesakop duurabeen ko mareeja़ ke muutaradavaar se muutaraashay kee or bheja jaata hai। yahm parosatet garmthi ke baढ़e hoe hisase ko kaatakar nikaal diya jaata hai aur parosatet ke tokaड़e ko muutaraashay mem dhakel diya jaata hai। muutaramaarag mem nalee daal dee jaatee hai jisase muutar utasarajan nirabaadhit ruup se hota rahata hai। muutaraashay mem dhakele gae garmthi ke bache hoe hisasom ko vahm se nikaal diya jaata hai। parosatet ke m tokaड़om ko paitholaॉjee (Pathology) jmch ke lie bheja jaata hai jahm garmthi ke akaar mem vaृdadhi ke kaaraणom kee jmch kee jaatee hai। parosatet garmthi ke leja़r sarajaree se nikaalane ke baad peshaab karane kee baढ़ee avaृtati, teevar echachha v muutaraashay puuraणta: khaalee n hone jaisee shikaayatem duur ho jaatee haim aur muutar ka paravaah bhee theek ho jaata hai। parosatet garmthi ko hataane se kaya samasaya  sakatee hai? (Problems to Remove Prostate Gland) parosatet garmthi ke saraav se shokaraaणoom ko poshaण aur sorakasha milatee hai। shalayakariya davaara garmthi ko nikaal die jaane par koe vipareet parabhaav naheem padata kayomki parosatet ke alaava semaaenal vesikalas (Seminal vesicles) bhee es kaaray ko karatee hai। Home Remedies: jaanem parosatet disaऑradar ke ghareluu upachaar (Home Remedies of Prostate Disorder) 3 se 4 leetar paanee rojaana peeem। bhojan mem vitaamin see kee maatara jayaada lem। charabeeyokat aur vasaayokat bhojam ka parayog bmd kar dem। rojaama soyaabeen khaaem esase tetosataron ka leval kam ho jaata hai। alasee ko mikasee mem peesakar paaudar bana lem aur paratidin 20 garaam paanee ke saath lem। chaay aur kaॉphee ka sevan n karem, esase muutaraashay gareeva kathor hotee hai jisase peshaab karane mem dikakat hotee hai। seetaaphal ke beej kachacha ya bhuun kar ya phir duusare beejom ke saath milaakar kha sakate haim। ese apane har din ke khaane mem shaamil kiya ja sakata hai। ese salaad mem milaakar bhee khaaya ja sakata hai। poha mem milaakar ya suup mem daalakar bhee kha sakate hai। kachache seetaaphal ke beej mem kaaphee maatara mem poshak tatav maujuud hote haim। jaise ayarana, phaॉsaphorasa, taripatophaina, kaॉpara, maigameeshiyama, maiganeeja, vitaamin ke, paroteena, jaruuree phaitee esid aur phaaetosaterola। ye beej jimk ke behatareen sarotom mem se ek maane jaate haim। har din 60 mileegaraam jimk ka sevan parosatet se juujh rahe mareejom mem behad phaayada pahomchaata hai aur unake savaasathay mem bhee sodhaar karata hai। en beejom mem beetaa-satiosaterol bhee hota hai jo tesatosateron ko dihaaedarotesateron mem badalane naheem detaa। jisase es garmthi ke baढ़ne kee smbhaavama n ke baraabar ho jaatee hai। Disease: edas (AIDS) Description: edas ya ekavaayarad emayuun dephisiemshee simdarom (Acquired Immune Deficiency Syndrome) doniya kee sabase khataranaak aur jaanaleva beemaariyom mem se ek hai। yah echaaevee vaayaras ke kaaraण phailame vaala rog hai। doniyaabhar mem edas ke saravaadhik maamale asorakashit yaun smbmdhom ke kaaraण hote haim। Symptoms: - akaaraण vajan ghatate jaanaa। - gale ya bagal mem suujan bharee gilatiyom ka ho jaanaa। - ta‍vacha par darad bhare aur khojalee vaale chakate ho jaanaa। - bima kisee vajah ke lagaataar daayariya bane rahanaa। - bima kisee vajah ke lagaataar thakaan bane rahana aur tejee se vajan giranaa। - momh mem ghaav ho jaanaa। - momh mem saphed chhaale jaise nishaan honaa। - yaadadaashat mem kamee, dipareshan ya amay dimaagee beemaaree - lmbe samay tak bokhaar rahana Reasons: edas ke kaarak (Causes of Aids in Hindi) doniyaabhar mem edas kee phailane kee sabase baड़ee vajah (Causes of Aids) asorakashit yaun smbmdhom ko maana jaata hai। lekin kae anay kaaraण bhee hai jo edas ke lie jimamevaar maame jaate haim: asorakashit sekas (Unsafe Sex):- ek se adhik saathiyom ke saath yaun smbmdh banaane se echaaevee edas phail sakata hai। yah samalaimgik smbmdhom mem bhee ho sakata hai। smkaramit rogee davaara (From HIV+ Victim):- echaaevee paॉjitiv porosh ya mahila ke saath asorakashit yaun smbmdh banaane ke kaaraण bhee yah phailata hai। smkaramit khuun chadha़aane (Through Blood Transfusion):- bina jmch kiya ho raka‍t garahaण karane ke kaaraण bhee echaaevee se peeड़it home ka khatara rahata hai। yah edas ko phailaane kee duusaree sabase baड़ee vajah maamee jaatee hai। smkaramit soe ke esatemaal se (Through Infected Needles):- daragas kee samasaya na siraph nashe tak seemit hai balaki agar ek hee emjekashan se kae log daragas lem to yah edas ka kaaraण ban sakata hai। siraph daragas hee naheem davaae lene ke dauraan bhee smkaramit soe ka esatemaal haanikaarak hota hai। smkaramit baled se (Through Imfected Blood):- saath hee naae ke yahm bina sataralaaejad (rogaaणo-mokata) usatara ya poraana enaphekated baled (Infected Blade) esatemaal karane se bhee yah phail sakata hai। smkaramit maata se (HIV Positive Mother):- echaaevee smkaramit maata ke davaara yah bachache mem khuun ya parasav ke samay aur duudh pilaane ke dauraam pahomch jaata hai। Treatments: edas se bachaav (Tips to prevent AIDS in Hindi) sorakashit sekas (Use Safety):- edasa, echaaevee smkaramaण aur anay sekas smkaramit beemaariym rokane ke lie hamesha smbmdh banaate samay kmdom adi ka parayog karana chaahie। apane jeevanasaathee ke parati vaphaadaar rahana chaahie aur ek se adhik va‍yakati se yaumasmbmdh banaane se bachana chaahie। esatemaal kee gae soeyom ka parayog na karem (Use Disposable Syringe):- soe lagavaate samay hamesha yah dhayaan rakhem ki disapojebal seerimj ya soeyom ka hee esatemaal ho। khuun ke lena-den se pahale jmch (Test Before Blood Transfusion):- khuun lene ya dene se pahale usakee jmch avashay kar lem। yadi ap echa.ae.vee smkaramit ya edas garasit haim to rakatadaan na karem। garabhavatee mahilaaem dhayaan rakhem (Tips for HIV+ Pregmant):- garabhavatee mahilaaom ko apana echaaevee tesat jaruur karaana chaahie। agar jmch paॉjitiv hai to bachacha ho jaane ke baad echaaevee se garasat mm ko bachache ko apana duudh naheem pilaana chaahie। es kes mem botal se duudh pilaana behatar maana jaata hai। shak hone par echa.ae.vee tesat (HIV AIDS Test):- yadi ap ko echa.ae.vee edas hone ka smdeh ho to tormt apana echa.ae.vee pareekashaण karaana chaahie। echaaevee edas kee davaaeym (HIV AIDS Drugs):- echaaevee paॉjitiv vayakati ko elaaj ke dauraan emtee-retarovaayaral daragas die jaate haim। Disease: jeeka vaayaras (Zik Virus) Descriptiom: ebola vaayaras ke baad doniyaabhar mem atmk phailaanee vaalee nae beemaaree hai jeekaa। jeeka vaayaras logom ke lie etana khataranaak hai ki vishav savaasathay smgathan ne jeeka vaayaras par ga‍lobal emarajemsee ghoshit kee hai। jeeka vaayaras baraajeel samet kae amay amerikee deshom mem phaila ho hai aur enaheem deshom ke ane vaale logom ke davaara esake vishav ke anay deshom mem phailane ke asaar haim। aeye jaanem jeeka vaayaras aur esake smkaramaण ke vishay mem puuraण jaanakaaree (Zik Virus Information in Hindi)। Symptoms: - nkhem laal hona - joda़om mem darad - bokhaar - ulatee - kamaja़oree Treatments: jeeka vaayaras ka elaaj (Treatment of Zik Virus in Himdi) * seedeesee ke anosaar jeeka emphekasham se laड़ne ke lie abhee kisee emjekasham ya davaae ko ejaad naheem kiya gaya hai। esase peeड़it vayakati ko puuree tarah se araam karana chaahie, khuub saara paanee peena chaahie, bokhaar kee saamaanay davaae lenee chaahie। * jeeka vaayaras se smkaramit hone par khod ko machachhar ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie anayatha yah vaayaras machachharom davaara anay logom mem pahomch sakata hai। peeड़it rogee ka machachharom se bachaav bahot jaruuree hai। nota: bokhaar ane par esaparim (Aspirin), baruuphen jaisee davaaeym bilakol naheem lenee chaahie। garabhavatee mahilaaom ke lie khaas niradesh (Tips For Pregnant Women) seedeesee ke davaara anay deshom mem rahane vaalee garabhavatee mahilaaom ko yah sojhaav diya gaya hai ki vah aphareekaa, dakashiण amerika ya jeeka parabhaavit anay deshom mem na jaaem। jeeka vaayaras se parabhaavit jagahom par rahane vaalee garabhavatee mahilaaom ko miman baatom ka khayaal rakhana chaahie: * khod ko machachharom ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie। * raat ko sote samay machachharadaanee ka parayog karana chaahie aur machachharom ke kaatane se bachane vaalee kareem lagaamee chaahie। * agar machachharom ke kaatane par siradarada, hala‍ka bokhaara, laal mkhem, joड़om mem darad jaise lakashaण dikhem to tormt daॉkatar se salaah lenee chaahie। * agar garabhavatee naheem haim to kochh dinom ke lie pareganemsee ke palaan ko taal dena chaahie। garabhavatee mahilaaom ko machachharom se bachane kee puuree koshish karanee chaahie kayomki jeeka vaayaras ke kaaraण unake garabh mem pal rahe bachachom ke masatishak ko sabase adhik nokasaan hota hai।
